# 2.14 Load Control

## 2.14.0-1 Load Control FA: Load Control Document Owner: Stefan Kempf (Nokia); Gangadhar Marishamaiah (Nokia) (ID: 11212325)

## 2.14.1 Overload definition

### 2.14.1.0-1 Overload definition (ID: 11212335)

**2.14.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11212346`)

Overload definition First, 5G-L2-PS separates its processing in 2 parts:

  * A Hard Real-time Processing, i.e. DL and UL schedulers -from pre-scheduler to post-scheduler (see [5G_L2_350_replaced([11150971](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24fcSPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] for DL timing considerations and [5G_L2_454_replaced([11152768](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24rCcPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] for UL timing considerations), constrained by the TTI duration, and triggered by 5G Timer,

  * The remaining Lower Priority Processing, i.e. messages from L1, internal messages between UL and DL schedulers, and CPlane requests from 5G-CP-RT.




**[Before CB009092-A]**

The second part is organized by categorizing the received EM events into three (03) categories with decreasing priorities.

\- Prio 0 (max) is dedicated to msg from 5G-L2-LO, internal and time synchronization msg,

\- Prio 1 is dedicated to msg from L1,

\- Prio 2 is dedicated to CPlane msg + UE msg + debug msg

**[CB009092-A]**

The second part is organized by categorizing the received EM events into four (04) categories with decreasing priorities.

\- Prio 0 (max) is dedicated to msg from 5G-L2-LO, internal and time synchronization msg,

\- Prio 1 is dedicated to Real Time (RT) msg from L1,

\- Prio 2 is dedicated to Non Real Time (NRT) msg from L1,

\- Prio 3 is dedicated to CPlane msg + UE msg + debug msg

**[End CB009092-A]**

---

### 2.14.1.1 L2-PS Schedulers FIFO mechanism principle

#### 2.14.1.1.0-1 L2-PS Schedulers FIFO mechanism principle (ID: 11212357)

**2.14.1.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `12687272`)

L2-PS Schedulers FIFO mechanism principle In case of FD parallelization (applicable to DL scheduler only):

 During the FD scheduling phase, any incoming event in the system FIFO queue, whatever its priority (5G_L2_9349_replaced([11212335](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-k2JfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is pushed into the appropriated software FIFO queue. The processing of events from any FIFO queue is forbidden in this FD scheduling phase.

 After the post-scheduling, if the software FIFO queues are not empty, the events are processed according to their priority and their handling policy defined by R&D parameters rdEventTimeCheckingPolicyForPrio0,.., rdEventTimeCheckingPolicyForPrio3 in 5G_L2_8476_replaced([11190346](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28WBivvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)); this phase corresponds to the FIFO processing phase.

 After the FIFO processing, if the system FIFO queue is not empty, the events are processed according to their priority and their handling policy defined by R&D parameters rdEventTimeCheckingPolicyForPrio0,.., rdEventTimeCheckingPolicyForPrio3 in 5G_L2_8476_replaced([11190346](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28WBivvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). 

In case of no FD parallelization (applicable to UL and DL schedulers):

 The incoming events are enqueued and remain in the system FIFO queue until the end of post-scheduling.

 After the post-scheduling, if the system FIFO queue is not empty, the events are processed according to their priority and their handling policy defined by R&D parameters rdEventTimeCheckingPolicyForPrio0,.., rdEventTimeCheckingPolicyForPrio3 in 5G_L2_8476_replaced([11190346](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28WBivvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). 

**[CB012971-WB]**

If rdEnableDlFdSchOnULCores([12686252](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wQhl0VMfEfCnPp04H8v-AQ)) is set as 1, the following messages can be handled parallelly with FD scheduler on UL Core.

  * DlBufferStatusInd
  * SrsBeamSelectionInd
  * PucchReceiveRespHarqD
  * PuschReceiveRespHarqD
  * PucchReceiveRespPs
  * PucchReceiveRespPsDelayCs



When handling the messages parallelly, if the UEs in the messages are in cs2List, the related messages of these UEs' part shall be buffered and handled afterwards.

**[End CB012971-WB]**

[image-0][image_desc]The image depicts a flowchart illustrating "FIFO Enhancements Principle applied to DL scheduler where FD parallelization occurs." ### 2.14.1.2 Event Time Checking Policy

#### 2.14.1.2.0-1 Event Time Checking Policy (ID: 11212378)

**2.14.1.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11212385`)

Event Time Checking Policy On scheduling state, 5G-L2-PS handle the different priorities (prio 0, prio 1, prio 2 and prio 3 defined in 5G_L2_9349_replaced([11212335](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-k2JfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) events following three (03) policies defined by the R&D parameters rdEventTimeCheckingPolicyForPrio0, ..., 3 defined in 5G_L2_8476_replaced([11190346](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28WBivvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) :

(i) alwaysAllow policy:

Any event under this policy is processed without any checking of the slot processing remaining time. Any event applying this policy is not delaying in slot.

(ii) staticTimeChecking policy:

Any event under this policy is processed

(a) if the slot processing remaining time is greater than

 rdEventTimeBudgetForPrio1_us R&D parameter for prio 1 type event.

 rdEventTimeBudgetForPrio2_us R&D parameter for prio 2 type event.

 rdEventTimeBudgetForPrio3_us R&D parameter for prio 3 type event.

(b) otherwise. the event is pushed in the according prio FIFO queue.

(iii) measuredTimeChecking policy:

Any event under this policy is measured. The event is processed if its cost is lower than the slot processing remaining time, otherwise the event is pushed in the according prio FIFO queue.

At the first time, as there is measurement available for the event;

 rdEventTimeBudgetForPrio1_us R&D parameter is used as initial value for prio 1 type event.

 rdEventTimeBudgetForPrio2_us R&D parameter is used as initial value for prio 2 type event.

 rrdEventTimeBudgetForPrio3_us R&D parameter is used as initial value for prio 3 type event.

The R&D parameters rdEventTimeBudgetForPrio1_us , ..., rdEventTimeBudgetForPrio3_us are defined in 5G_L2_8485_replaced([11190371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28WBjvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.14.1.2.0-2 Event Time Checking Policy Addtional Event Time Checking Policy For Parallel Scheduling (ID: 12687292)

**2.14.1.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12687293`)

Event Time Checking Policy If rdEnableDlFdSchOnULCores([12686252](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wQhl0VMfEfCnPp04H8v-AQ)) is set as 1, the following additional checking for NRT message handling is needed.

\- On DL Core, in loadTypeDlOnly slot, the NRT processing for non-CS2 UEs([11212357](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-k2L_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) shall be ended before: the timing of sending out FdScheduleReq + avgFdCommonTime + avgFdFirstUeTime + (toBeScheduledUeList.size() -1)* avgFdUeTime

\- On UL Core, in loadTypeDlOnly slot, the NRT processing shall be ended before: the timing of starting to handle SlotSynchroInd + avgPreAndTdTime

Where,

\- avgFdCommonTime, avgFdFirstUeTime, avgFdUeTime, avgPreAndTdTime see [11213591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZAfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

\- toBeScheduledUeList see [11196444](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwCeo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

---

### 2.14.1.3 Preventive overload monitoring

#### 2.14.1.3.0-1 Preventive overload monitoring Target Duration Ratio (ID: 11212394)

**2.14.1.3.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `11212420`)

Preventive overload monitoring [Before CB012716-A]

The R&D parameter rdOptimalSlotProcessingRatio (5G_L2_5930_replaced([11190056](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28UMVPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) defines for the hard real-time processing -i.e. UL or DL scheduler-, the target duration ratio, with respect to the whole TTI duration.

It is determined so as to leave enough time for 5G-L2-PS to process the lower priority part (i.e. the 4 FIFO message queues of asynchronous events) in the remaining TTI duration, while ensuring the best possible scheduling capacity.

[CB012716-A]

The target duration ratio is the portion of the slot duration which 5G-L2-PS may use for DL and UL scheduling.

It is determined so as to leave enough time for 5G-L2-PS for FIFO message queue processing (5G_L2_1843_replaced([11212803](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-n5evvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the remaining slot duration, while ensuring sufficient time for DL and UL scheduling.

It is given by the parameter slotProcessingRatio in 5G_L2_15692_replaced([11212528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mESvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB012716-A]

If this target duration is exceeded, 5G-L2-PS enters the overload state.

If several schedulers are deployed on the same core, each scheduler is given a part of the global target duration ratio.

The deployed schedulers in the same core can be of the same cell or different cells.

The schedulers' share of the target duration ratio is specified in 5G_L2_6333_replaced([11212562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

### 2.14.1.4 Corrective overload detection

#### 2.14.1.4.1 TTI processing duration

##### 2.14.1.4.1.0-1 TTI processing duration 5G-L2-PS takes advantage of the 5G Timer btu window to detect the time distance between the expected start time for the current TTI and the real triggering time of the scheduler (EM event). If 5G-L2-PS is late in processing the EM triggering event, it enters the overload state, meaning that the total 5G-L2-PS processing -i.e. scheduler processing plus lower priority processing- for the preceding TTI exceeded the allowed duration. 5G-L2-PS is considered late if the ratio of remaining time in the allowed btu window (with respect to the whole window) is lower than the rdOverloadOuterLoopThreshold R&amp;D parameter. Example with rdOverloadOuterLoopThreshold = 50% : [image-0][image_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating a timing synchronization mechanism, likely within a telecommunications context, possibly 5G. It depicts two main synchronization events, labeled "btuSlotSynchro Ind" and "btuSlotSynchroInd" (with a slight variation in spelling). The diagram uses horizontal lines to represent time or a timeline. A blue line indicates a "5GTimer Requested by L2-RT EO". Below this, a box states "BCN RP1 Basis for 5GTimer". Each synchronization event is associated with an "Acceptable deviation window", represented by a dotted red rectangle. Vertical red lines mark the "btuSlotLowerBoundary" and "btuSlotupperBoundary" for these windows. Arrows and labels indicate timing relationships. For the first event, a green double-headed arrow labeled "btuReferenceSync" points to a blue arrow labeled "N" which points downwards into the "Acceptable deviation window". A green line originates from within the window and branches into two outcomes: 1. A green box with the text "Remaining ratio &gt; 50% =&gt; No overload detected". 2. A gray line leading to an implied outcome not explicitly stated but contrasting with the green box. For the second synchronization event, a similar structure is present. A green double-headed arrow labeled "btuReferenceSync" points to a blue arrow labeled "N+1" which points downwards into the second "Acceptable deviation window". A red line originates from within this window and branches into two outcomes: 1. A red box with the text "Remaining ratio &lt; 50% =&gt; overload detected". 2. A gray line leading to an implied outcome not explicitly stated but contrasting with the red box. The diagram suggests that the system monitors the timing of incoming synchronization signals relative to an expected window. If the timing falls within the acceptable deviation, it's considered normal. If it deviates beyond a certain threshold (indicated by the "Remaining ratio" conditions), an overload is detected. The "N" and "N+1" likely refer to consecutive time slots or synchronization instances.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_11278.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] (ID: 11212438)

#### 2.14.1.4.2 FIFO message queues state

##### 2.14.1.4.2.0-1 FIFO message queues state (ID: 11212446)

**2.14.1.4.2.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `12747237`)

FIFO message queues state At the end of the slot duration (calculated from the slot start on synchroInd), 5G-L2-PS checks the contents of the FIFO message queues starting by the higher priority FIFO queue (prio 1 FIFO queue) to lower priority FIFO queue (prio 3 FIFO queue). The FIFO queues priorities are defined in 5G_L2_9349_replaced([11212335](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-k2JfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The prio 0 FIFO queue content is never checked by 5G-L2-PS as it is not used to trigger the overload state and according 5G_L2_6717_replaced([11212808](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-n5e_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G-L2-PS always processes all messages in prio 0 FIFO queue at the end of the slot duration and prio 0 FIFO queue shall be empty.

5G-L2-PS can enter to overload sate (cs1List is set to 1) triggered by

prio 1 FIFO queue

prio 2 FIFO queue

**[Before CB014680-C]prio 3 FIFO queue**[End CB014680-C]****

(i) overload sate triggered by prio 1 FIFO queue

**[Before CB014680-C]**

if prio 1 FIFO queue contains at least one event being in the queue during N consecutive slots, where N greater than _rdFifoQueuesAgingThresholdForPrio1_Slots R &D parameter (5G_L2_8517_replaced([11190423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Wol_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or prio 1 FIFO queue contains more events than the _rdMaxOverloadQueueSizeForPrio1 _R &D parameter (5G_L2_8501_replaced([11190401](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Wok_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then 5G-L2-PS enters to the overload state._**

**[CB014680-C]**

if prio 1 FIFO queue contains more than 40 events, then 5G-L2-PS enters to the overload state.

**[End CB014680-C]**

(ii) overload sate triggered by prio 2 FIFO queue

**[Before CB014680-C]**

if prio 2 FIFO queue contains at least one event being in the queue during N consecutive slots, where N greater than _rdFifoQueuesAgingThresholdForPrio2_Slots R &D parameter (5G_L2_8517_replaced([11190423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Wol_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or prio 2 FIFO queue contains more events than the _rdMaxOverloadQueueSizeForPrio2 _R &D parameter (5G_L2_8501_replaced([11190401](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Wok_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then 5G-L2-PS enters to the overload state._**

**[CB014680-C]**

if prio 2 FIFO queue contains more than 40 events, then 5G-L2-PS enters to the overload state.

**[End CB014680-C]**

(iii) overload sate triggered by prio 3 FIFO queue

**[Before CB014680-C]**

if prio 3 FIFO queue contains at least one event being in the queue during N consecutive slots, where N greater than _rdFifoQueuesAgingThresholdForPrio3_Slots R &D parameter (5G_L2_8501_replaced([11190401](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Wok_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or prio 3 FIFO queue contains more events than the _rdMaxOverloadQueueSizeForPrio3 _R &D parameter (5G_L2_8517_replaced([11190423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Wol_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then 5G-L2-PS enters to the overload state._**

**[CB014680-C]**

if prio 3 FIFO queue contains more events than the _rdMaxOverloadQueueSizeForPrio3_([11190423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Wol_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), then 5G-L2-PS applies gradual reduction in CS1 List max size based on the number of pending events in prio3 queue as defined in [11212970](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-pHlfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-pHlfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").**

**[End CB014680-C]**

While 5G-L2-PS remains in overload state, the corrective actions are maintained.

5G-L2-PS can exit from overload state in the **[Before CB014680-C]three (03)**[End CB014680-C]following cases:****

(i) overload sate has been triggered by prio 1 FIFO queue

**[Before CB014680-C]**

if there no one event being in prio 1 FIFO queue during N consecutive slots, where N greater than _rdFifoQueuesAgingThresholdForPrio1_Slots (5G_L2_8517_replaced([11190423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Wol_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) AND the number of events present in prio 1 FIFO queue is lower than _rdMaxOverloadQueueSizeForPrio1 (5G_L2_8501_replaced([11190401](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Wok_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) AND greater OR equal to _rdMinOverloadQueueSizeForPrio1 R &D parameter (5G_L2_8509_replaced([11190411](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28WolfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))._**

**[CB014680-C]**

if the number of events present in prio 1 FIFO queue is lower than 40.

**[End CB014680-C]**

(ii) overload sate has been triggered by prio 2 FIFO queue

**[Before CB014680-C]**

if there no one event being in prio 2 FIFO queue during N consecutive slots, where N greater than _rdFifoQueuesAgingThresholdForPrio2_Slots (5G_L2_8517_replaced([11190423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Wol_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) AND the number of events present in prio 2 FIFO queue is lower than _rdMaxOverloadQueueSizeForPrio2 (5G_L2_8501_replaced([11190401](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Wok_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) AND greater OR equal to _rdMinOverloadQueueSizeForPrio2 R &D parameter (5G_L2_8509_replaced([11190411](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28WolfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))._**

**[CB014680-C]**

if the number of events present in prio 2 FIFO queue is lower than 40.

**[End CB014680-C]**

**[Before CB014680-C]**

(iii) overload sate has been triggered by prio 3 FIFO queue

if there no one event being in prio 3 FIFO queue during N consecutive slots, where N greater than _rdFifoQueuesAgingThresholdForPrio3_Slots (5G_L2_8517_replaced([11190423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Wol_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) AND the number of events present in prio 3 FIFO queue is lower than _rdMaxOverloadQueueSizeForPrio3 (5G_L2_8501_replaced([11190401](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Wok_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) AND greater OR equal to _rdMinOverloadQueueSizeForPrio3 R &D parameter (5G_L2_8509_replaced([11190411](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28WolfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))._**

**[End CB014680-C]**

As an example, when overload is triggered due to transient burst of NRT events from CP (like a burst of new users connecting, user addition), scheduler will make time to process these events and get out of overload once the burst is processed.

Flowchart showing the transition overload state <> scheduling state

**[Before CB014680-C]**

[image-0][image_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process related to event queues and states, likely within a system managing priorities and overload conditions. The flowchart begins with an "At slot Startup" state. From the startup state, the process branches into a series of conditional checks based on the state of different priority (prio) FIFO queues. These checks involve parameters like "N consecutive slots," "rdMaxConsecutiveSlotsWithOldestDelay," "rdMaxOverloadQueueSizeForPrioX," and "rdMinOverloadQueueSizeForPrioX." The flowchart has two main states: "Overload State (Cs1 List Size = 1)" and "Scheduling State (Cs1 List Size > 1)". The "Overload State" is entered if certain conditions related to prio 1 FIFO queue are met. Within the "Overload State," there's a step to "Update FIFO queues counters" before proceeding to "Go To Next Slot." The "Scheduling State" is entered if a different set of conditions, involving prio 2 and prio 3 FIFO queues, are met. Similar to the overload state, there's an "Update FIFO queues counters" step before proceeding to "Go To Next Slot." The flowchart uses "YES" and "NO" branches to navigate between different decision points and states. The overall flow seems to determine whether the system is in an overload condition or a scheduling condition based on the occupancy and delay characteristics of prioritized event queues. NO Is prio 2 FIFO queue contains more events than the rdMaxOverload QueueSizeFor Prio2? NO Is prio 3 FIFO queue contains atleast one event being in the queue during N consecutive slots, where N greater than rdMaxConsecutiveSlots With OldestDelay edEventNever Flushed For Prio2? YES YES Is no one event being in prio 2 FIFO queue during N consecutive slots, where N greater than rdMaxConsecutiveSlots With OldestDelayed Event Never Flushe dForPrio2 AND the number of events present in prio 2 FIFO queue is lower than rdMax Overload QueueSizeFor Prio2 AND greater OR equal to rdMin Overload QueueSizeForPrio2 ? NO Is no one event being in prio 3 FIFO queue during N consecutive slots, where N greater than rdMaxConsecutiveSlots With OldestDelayed Event Never Flushe dForPrio3 AND the number of events present in prio 3 FIFO queue is lower than rdMaxOverload QueueSizeForPrio3 AND greater OR equal to rdMinOverload QueueSizeForPrio3 ? NO NO Is prio 3 FIFO queue contains more events than the rdMaxOverload QueueSizeForPrio2? NO YES Scheduling State (Cs1 List Size > 1) Update FIFO queues counters Go To Next Slot[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_11282.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

**[CB014680-C]**

[image-1][image_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process related to FIFO queues and states like "Overload State" and "Scheduling State". The flowchart begins with a starting point labeled "At slot Startup". From there, it proceeds to a decision point: "Is prio 1 FIFO queue contains more than 40 events?". If the answer is "NO", the process moves to another decision point: "Is prio 2 FIFO queue contains more than 40 events?". If the answer to the first question is "YES", it leads to the "Overload State" which includes an action "Update FIFO queues counters" and then a directive "Go To Next Slot". If the answer to "Is prio 2 FIFO queue contains more than 40 events?" is "NO", it leads to a third decision point: "Is prio 3 FIFO queue contains more events than the rdMaxOverloadQueueSizeForPrio3?". If the answer to the second question is "YES", it also leads to the "Overload State". If the answer to the third question is "NO", it leads to a decision point: "Reduction of CS1 List Max size in corrective OLC based on number of pending messages in FIFO prio3 queue?". If the answer to the third question is "YES", it leads to a decision point: "Is the number of events present in prio 3 FIFO queue is lower than rdMaxOverloadQueueSizeForPrio3?". Following the "Overload State", there are three decision points that check if the number of events in each priority queue is lower than a certain threshold (40 for prio 1 and 2, and rdMaxOverloadQueueSizeForPrio3 for prio 3). \- If "Is the number of events present in prio 1 FIFO queue is lower than 40 events?" is "YES", it leads to the next decision point. If "NO", it loops back to the "Overload State". \- If "Is the number of events present in prio 2 FIFO queue is lower than 40 events?" is "YES", it leads to the next decision point. If "NO", it loops back to the "Overload State". \- If "Is the number of events present in prio 3 FIFO queue is lower than rdMaxOverloadQueueSizeForPrio3?" is "YES", it leads to the "Scheduling State". If "NO", it leads to the "Reduction of CS1 List Max size..." decision. The "Scheduling State" is described as "(Cs1 List Size > 1)" and includes an action "Update FIFO queues counters", followed by a directive "Go To Next Slot". The "Reduction of CS1 List Max size..." decision point, if answered "YES", leads to the "Scheduling State". If answered "NO", it leads to the "Scheduling State".[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/FIFO FlowChart v12(B).png[/image_path][/image-1]

**[End CB014680-C]**

### 2.14.2.0-2 Overload control Activation of Load Balancing for N Schedulers (ID: 11212488)

**2.14.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11212497`)

Overload control [Before CB012716-A]

R&D activation parameter rdEnableOLCforNScheduler (5G_L2_12274_replaced([11190587](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28X2tfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall enable Load Balancing for N schedulers in a core.

For deployment with <= 2 cells per L2 sub pool or <2 cells per core or = 2 cells per core (FDD),

if actDynOverloadControl= true and rdEnableOLCforNScheduler = false

if actDynOverloadControl= true and rdEnableOLCforNScheduler = True

Load Balancing functionality is used (support for 4 load states) as defined in 5G_L2_12271_replaced([11214033](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-v1UPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_5850_replaced([11213986](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-v1SPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),5G_L2_7901_replaced([11213922](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vOPPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),5G_L2_5847_replaced([11213912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vOOvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

For FDD cell deployment with 2 or 1 cell(s) per core, the load balancing shall enable any scheduler to exceed more than 450us in a slot such that aggregated slot ratio for all the scheduler does not exceed the optimalSlotProcessingRatio , as defined in 5G_L2_1833_replaced([11212618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrWvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For TDD deployment with 3 cells per L2 Sub pool (5G_L2_4307_replaced([11140781](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23ldUPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Mandatory for rdEnableOLCforNScheduler = TRUE to enable 3 cells per L2 Sub pool

if actDynOverloadControl= true and rdEnableOLCforNScheduler = True

Load Balancing functionality is used (support for 4 load states) as defined in 5G_L2_12271_replaced([11214033](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-v1UPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_5850_replaced([11213986](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-v1SPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),5G_L2_7901_replaced([11213922](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vOPPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),5G_L2_5847_replaced([11213912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vOOvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

if actDynOverloadControl= false and rdEnableOLCforNScheduler = True

Dynamic overload control is disabled including Load Balancing , Static load share shall be allocated for each scheduler as defined in 5G_L2_5841_replaced([11213804](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-unKfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

actDynOverloadControl is received in the PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq (see 5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

### 2.14.2.0-3 Overload control Detection and Reporting of a severe overload Situation (ID: 11212512)

**2.14.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12775858`)

Overload control If rdEnableOverloadErrMsg = 1 (5G_L2_22385_replaced([11191183](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28cIJPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2-PS shall print a Syslog WRN(=Warning) to inform the tester about a persistent and severe overload situation in a certain scheduler.

The overload condition which triggers the warning is based on the frequency the maximum CS1 size is reduced to 1 by the preventive overload control ( floor([Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size [CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive [End CNI-136895-A]) = 1, 5G_L2_1841_replaced([11212749](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-n5cPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or by the corrective overload control (cs1Size = 1, 5G_L2_1853_replaced([11212970](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-pHlfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), evaluated separately per slot load type (5G_L2_6333_replaced([11212562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The occurrence of such reduction is detected on slot basis over a time of 1024 radio frame. The details are described below.

  * At Cell Setup, for each DL or UL scheduler separately and respective active slot type:



L2-PS initializes the internal variables counting the occurrances of overload along an hyperframe:

numOfSlotsMaxCs1ReducPrevOvc[activeSlotType] = 0

numOfSlotsMaxCs1ReducCorrOvc[activeSlotType] = 0

and the internal variables counting the number of slots which are available for scheduling along one hyperframe:

numOfSlotsAvailForScheduling[activeSlotType] = ~~1024~~ 0

where:

activeSlotType = {loadTypeDlOnly, loadTypeMixed} for DL-sch

activeSlotType = {loadTypeUlOnly, loadTypeMixed} for UL-sch

  * For each DL/UL scheduler, at each respective active slot type where at least 1 UE is scheduled or skip (5G_L2_1858_replaced([11213112](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-purPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))



[Before CNI-136895-A] 

L2-PS evaluates floor(avgCs1Size) and cs1Size:

IF ( (DL Scheduler) AND (activeSlotType == loadTypeMixed) AND (TDD FR1) )

{

IF ((cs1Size == 1) AND (floor(avgCs1Size) > 1)) numOfSlotsMaxCs1ReducCorrOvc[activeSlotType]++;

}

ELSE

{

IF (floor(avgCs1Size) == 1) numOfSlotsMaxCs1ReducPrevOvc[activeSlotType]++;

IF ((cs1Size == 1) AND (floor(avgCs1Size) > 1)) numOfSlotsMaxCs1ReducCorrOvc[activeSlotType]++;

}

Note: for the DL-sch in a mixed slot in TDD FR1 deployment, the occurrance of floor(avgCs1Size) == 1 is normal/intended for enough UL traffic, therefore a different condition is applied in this case.

and increments numOfSlotsAvailForScheduling[activeSlotType].

[CNI-136895-A]

L2-PS evaluates floor(cs1ListMaxSizePreventive) and cs1Size:

IF ( (DL Scheduler) AND (activeSlotType == loadTypeMixed) AND (TDD FR1) )

{

IF ((cs1Size == 1) AND (floor(cs1ListMaxSizePreventive) > 1)) numOfSlotsMaxCs1ReducCorrOvc[activeSlotType]++;

}

ELSE

{

IF (floor(cs1ListMaxSizePreventive) == 1) numOfSlotsMaxCs1ReducPrevOvc[activeSlotType]++;

IF ((cs1Size == 1) AND (floor(cs1ListMaxSizePreventive) > 1)) numOfSlotsMaxCs1ReducCorrOvc[activeSlotType]++;

}

Note: for the DL-sch in a mixed slot in TDD FR1 deployment, the occurrance of floor(cs1ListMaxSizePreventive) == 1 is normal/intended for enough UL traffic, therefore a different condition is applied in this case.

and increments numOfSlotsAvailForScheduling[activeSlotType]. [End CNI-136895-A] 

  * At sfn=0, for each DL/UL scheduler and respective active slot type



L2-PS calculates the following ratios:

ratioSlotsMaxCs1ReducPrevOvc[activeSlotType] = numOfSlotsMaxCs1ReducPrevOvc[activeSlotType] / numOfSlotsAvailForScheduling[activeSlotType]

ratioSlotsMaxCs1ReducCorrOvc[activeSlotType] = numOfSlotsMaxCs1ReducCorrOvc[activeSlotType] / numOfSlotsAvailForScheduling[activeSlotType]

and checks the condition to trigger the WRN print:

DL scheduler:

condDlOnlySlots = (ratioSlotsMaxCs1ReducPrevOvc[loadTypeDlOnly] > maxCs1PrevOvcReducThres_perc) OR (ratioSlotsMaxCs1ReducCorrOvc[loadTypeDlOnly] > maxCs1CorrOvcReducThres_perc)

condDlMixSlots = ( (TDD FR1) AND (ratioSlotsMaxCs1ReducCorrOvc[loadTypeMixed] > maxCs1CorrOvcReducThres_perc) ) OR

( (TDD FR2 or FDD) AND ( (ratioSlotsMaxCs1ReducPrevOvc[loadTypeMixed] > maxCs1PrevOvcReducThres_perc) OR

(ratioSlotsMaxCs1ReducCorrOvc[loadTypeMixed] > maxCs1CorrOvcReducThres_perc) ) )

IF(condDlOnlySlots OR condDlMixSlots)

{

Send SysLog WRN message and print the following information:

  * ratioSlotsMaxCs1ReducPrevOvc[loadTypeDlOnly]

  * ratioSlotsMaxCs1ReducCorrOvc[loadTypeDlOnly]

  * ratioSlotsMaxCs1ReducPrevOvc[loadTypeMixed]

  * ratioSlotsMaxCs1ReducCorrOvc[loadTypeMixed]

  * numOfSlotsAvailForScheduling[loadTypeDlOnly]

  * numOfSlotsAvailForScheduling[loadTypeMixed]




}

UL scheduler:

condUlOnlySlots = (ratioSlotsMaxCs1ReducPrevOvc[loadTypeUlOnly] > maxCs1PrevOvcReducThres_perc) OR (ratioSlotsMaxCs1ReducCorrOvc[loadTypeUlOnly] > maxCs1CorrOvcReducThres_perc)

condUlMixSlots = (ratioSlotsMaxCs1ReducPrevOvc[loadTypeMixed] > maxCs1PrevOvcReducThres_perc) OR (ratioSlotsMaxCs1ReducCorrOvc[loadTypeMixed] > maxCs1CorrOvcReducThres_perc)

IF( condUlOnlySlots OR condUlMixSlots )

{

Send SysLog WRN message and print the following information:

  * ratioSlotsMaxCs1ReducPrevOvc[loadTypeUlOnly]

  * ratioSlotsMaxCs1ReducCorrOvc[loadTypeUlOnly]

  * ratioSlotsMaxCs1ReducPrevOvc[loadTypeMixed]

  * ratioSlotsMaxCs1ReducCorrOvc[loadTypeMixed]

  * numOfSlotsAvailForScheduling[loadTypeUlOnly]

  * numOfSlotsAvailForScheduling[loadTypeMixed]




}

Then the counters are reset:

numOfSlotsMaxCs1ReducPrevOvc[activeSlotType] = 0

numOfSlotsMaxCs1ReducCorrOvc[activeSlotType] = 0

numOfSlotsAvailForScheduling[activeSlotType] = 0

maxCs1PrevOvcReducThres_perc = 1%, maxCs1CorrOvcReducThres_perc = 5%.

---

### 2.14.2.1 Processing Ratios

#### 2.14.2.1.0-1 Processing Ratios Slot Processing Ratio (dynamic) (ID: 11212528)

**2.14.2.1.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `12686335`)

Processing Ratios The slot processing ratio is the portion of a slot duration which is available for scheduling, excluding FIFO message queue processing (5G_L2_1843_replaced([11212803](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-n5evvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), on one particular core. It is a dynamic value which 5G-L2-PS shall adjust to the current load on the given core, unless actAdaptiveSchedulerBudgetOlc = FALSE. The value is valid for all slots in the slot pattern. 5G-L2-PS shall determine the slot processing ratio as follows.

IF (actAdaptiveSchedulerBudgetOlc = TRUE) AND

(scs is not equal to 120 (mmWave))**AND**

((duplexMode is not equal to FDD) OR

(l1Variant is not equal to loner)):

At start-up, 5G-L2-PS shall initialize the slot processing ratio as:

**[Before CB012971-WB]**

slotProcessingRatio = rdMaxAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatio_perCent / 100

**[CB012971-WB]**

slotProcessingRatio = maxAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatio / 100

**[End CB012971-WB]**

slotProcessingRatioWithoutAdditionalReserve = slotProcessingRatio

At the beginning of every slot n, after updating the averageSlotUtilization, 5G-L2-PS shall update the slotProcessingRatio as follows:

1) Update the slotProcessingRatioWithoutAdditionalReserve:   
averageSlotUtilization_perCent = 100 * averageSlotUtilization / slotDuration

**[Before CB012971-WB]**

slotProcessingRatioWithoutAdditionalReserve += rdAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatioUnitStep/100 *** (1 – averageSlotUtilization_perCent / rdTargetSlotUtilization_perCent)**

slotProcessingRatioWithoutAdditionalReserve = min{ rdMaxAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatio_perCent, max{ rdMinAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatio_perCent, slotProcessingRatioWithoutAdditionalReserve * 100, 100 * schedulerProcessingTime / slotDuration} } / 100

**[CB012971-WB]**

slotProcessingRatioWithoutAdditionalReserve += rdAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatioUnitStep/100 *** (1 – averageSlotUtilization_perCent / targetSlotUtilization)**

slotProcessingRatioWithoutAdditionalReserve = min{ maxAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatio, max{ rdMinAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatio_perCent, slotProcessingRatioWithoutAdditionalReserve * 100, 100 * schedulerProcessingTime / slotDuration} } / 100

**[End CB012971-WB]**

Note: In a stable operating point, the schedulers' schedulerProcessingTime doesn't exceed the time budget given by slotProcessingRatioWithoutAdditionalReserve. When the schedulers exceed this budget they are likely too loaded to obey to the limit given by slotProcessingRatioWithoutAdditionalReserve. In such a situation it doesn't make sense to reduce the schedulers' budget any further as the schedulers are going to exceed it constantly. 

However, if the averageSlotUtilization has not been updated in slot n as per 5G_L2_15591_replaced([11213737](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAHfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G-L2-PS shall not update the slotProcessingRatioWithoutAdditionalReserve.

2) Apply the additionalReserveRatio:

slotProcessingRatio = slotProcessingRatioWithoutAdditionalReserve - additionalReserveRatio

slotProcessingRatio = max{ rdMinAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatio_perCent, slotProcessingRatio * 100 } / 100

For the TTI trace: appliedAdditionalReserveRatio = slotProcessingRatioWithoutAdditionalReserve - slotProcessingRatio 

IF ((rdAllocateMaxSchShareOnMixedSlot is set '1' **[CB012971-WB] OR rdEnableDlFdSchOnULCores([12686252](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wQhl0VMfEfCnPp04H8v-AQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) is set as 1 **[End CB012971-WB]) AND (loadType == loadTypeMixed))****

slotProcessingRatio = **[Before CB012971-WB]rdMaxAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatio_perCent**[End CB012971-WB]maxAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatio **[End CB012971-WB] / 100 - additionalReserveRatio** ****

slotProcessingRatio = max{ rdMinAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatio_perCent, slotProcessingRatio * 100 } / 100

For the TTI trace: appliedAdditionalReserveRatio = **[Before CB012971-WB]rdMaxAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatio_perCent**[End CB012971-WB]maxAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatio **[End CB012971-WB] / 100 - slotProcessingRatio** ****

Note: To improve UL scheduler performance in TDD FR1, the RT processing share on mixed slots is configured to the maximum slot processing ratio.

ELSE:

**[Before CB012971-WB]**

At start-up, 5G-L2-PS shall initialize the slot processing ratio as:

slotProcessingRatio = optimalSlotProcessingRatio

**[CB012971-WB]**

If rdEnableDlFdSchOnULCores([12686252](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wQhl0VMfEfCnPp04H8v-AQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) is set as 1 ,

The slot processing ratio shall be decided based on load type at the beginning of every slot.

If (loadType != loadTypeMixed)

slotProcessingRatio = rdMaxAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatioParallel_perCent([12686260](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_UreDdVMhEfCnPp04H8v-AQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))

Else

slotProcessingRatio = rdMaxAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatio_perCent([11217224](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_m-wOUfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Else

At start-up, 5G-L2-PS shall initialize the slot processing ratio as:

slotProcessingRatio = optimalSlotProcessingRatio

**[End CB012971-WB]**

slotProcessingRatioWithoutAdditionalReserve = slotProcessingRatio

At the beginning of every slot n, 5G-L2-PS shall apply the additionalReserveRatio:

slotProcessingRatio = slotProcessingRatioWithoutAdditionalReserve - additionalReserveRatio

For the TTI trace: appliedAdditionalReserveRatio = slotProcessingRatioWithoutAdditionalReserve - slotProcessingRatio

With:

  * actAdaptiveSchedulerBudgetOlc is received in the PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * scs is received in the PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * duplexMode is received in L2RtPoolDeploymentInformations (5G_L2_IF_14_replaced([10966124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UMlxPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * l1Variant is received in PsCell_CellSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_61_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * rdAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatioUnitStep is defined in 5G_L2_15241_replaced([11190874](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Zr6vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * averageSlotUtilization is computed in 5G_L2_15591_replaced([11213737](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAHfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * **[Before CB012971-WB]**



**rdTargetSlotUtilization_perCent is defined in 5G_L2_15239_replaced([11190670](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28YdxPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

**rdMaxAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatio_perCent is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_32162_replaced([11217224](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_m-wOUfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

**[CB012971-WB]**

If rdEnableDlFdSchOnULCores([12686252](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wQhl0VMfEfCnPp04H8v-AQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) is set as 1,

targetSlotUtilization is rdTargetSlotUtilizationParallel_perCent([12686262](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aHjRolMhEfCnPp04H8v-AQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

maxAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatio is rdMaxAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatioParallel_perCent([12686260](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_UreDdVMhEfCnPp04H8v-AQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))

Else

targetSlotUtilization is rdTargetSlotUtilization_perCent([11190670](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28YdxPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

maxAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatio is rdMaxAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatio_perCent([11217224](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_m-wOUfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 

[End CB012971-WB]

  * rdMinAdaptiveSlotProcessingRatio_perCent is defined in 5G_L2_15237_replaced([11190862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Zr6PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * optimalSlotProcessingRatio is computed in 5G_L2_1833_replaced([11212618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrWvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * additionalReserveRatio is defined in 5G_L2_16997_replaced([11212539](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mETPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * schedulerProcessingTime is defined in 5G_L2_17152_replaced([11213759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-unIfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * loadType of slot is defined in [11212562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_RSkOsPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  * rdAllocateMaxSchShareOnMixedSlot is defined in [12636738](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kXBNsUBGEfCal_QUJn4xrg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kXBNsUBGEfCal_QUJn4xrg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").

---

#### 2.14.2.1.0-2 Processing Ratios Additional Reserve Ratio (dynamic) (ID: 11212539)

**2.14.2.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11212551`)

Processing Ratios The additional reserve ratio is a one-time reservation of CPU time, valid in the current slot, for tasks with extraordinary high CPU demand. Load control is going to reserve the requested time by subtracting it from the available scheduling time in 5G_L2_15692_replaced([11212528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mESvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). I.e. the time reservation is made at the expense of a lower slotProcessingRatio (5G_L2_15692_replaced([11212528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mESvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the current slot. The additional reserve ratio is given as a portion of the slot duration.

5G-L2-PS can use the additional reserve ratio to reserve time for tasks with the following properties.

  * The task is not part of UE scheduling.
  * The approximate CPU cycle consumption of the task is known.
  * It is certain that the task is going to be executed in the current slot.



Only for such tasks, 5G-L2-PS can request a time reservation by setting additionalReserveRatio to a value which corresponds to the expected CPU consumption of the task in the current slot.

5G-L2-PS must set the required value of additionalReserveRatio in each and every slot. In slots which don't need any time reservation 5G-L2-PS must explicitly set the value of additionalReserveRatio to 0.

At start-up 5G-L2-PS shall initialize additionalReserveRatio as:

additionalReserveRatio = 0

At the beginning of every slot 5G-L2-PS shall update additionalReserveRatio as follows:

additionalReserveRatio = 0

For DPA processing, 5G-L2-PS shall reserve processing time as per 5G_UP_ALG_24651_replaced([11216583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxZwjPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If all of the following conditions are met:

  * actDpaOverloadControl = TRUE.
  * An FDD cell is running on the given core.
  * The given core is in charge of DPA processing for the FDD cell.
  * The current slot is a DPA slot. This includes slots preT2, T2 and T2s as per 5G_L2_15838_replaced([11158839](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25NN8_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).



Then 5G-L2-PS shall set

additionalReserveRatio += [Before PR798513]rdReserveProcessingUsForDpa[PR798513]reserveUsForDpa[End PR798513] / (slotDurationInNs / 1000)

[PR798513] where reserveUsForDpa = min(rounddownn to us(sum of avgDpaProcessTime refer to 5G_L2_15838_replaced([11158839](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25NN8_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for all cell in the core on the slot), rdReserveProcessingUsForDpa).[End PR798513]

5G-L2-PS shall limit additionalReserveRatio to avoid too high values which don't leave enough time for UE scheduling:

additionalReserveRatio = min{ rdMaxAdditionalReserveRatio, additionalReserveRatio }

With:

  * rdMaxAdditionalReserveRatio is defined in 5G_L2_16995_replaced([11190840](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Zr5PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * rdReserveProcessingUsForDpa is defined in 5G_L2_16679_replaced([11190813](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28ZE3_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * actDpaOverloadControl is received in PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

#### 2.14.2.1.0-3 Processing Ratios Post-Scheduling Pattern Ratio (dynamic) (ID: 12645241)

**2.14.2.1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13411964`)

Processing Ratios [Before CB015327-SR-B] The Post-Scheduling Pattern Ratio is a slot-specific correction factor [CB015327-SR-B] The pattern correction time is a slot-specific correction time [End CB015327-SR-B] computed during each slot. It is derived from the IIR-filtered measurement of excess time in the post-scheduling phase for a given slot, compared against a sliding window maximum of pure scheduling time for that same slot. This excess is used to reduce the load in the current slot and used to reduce the risk of systemic processing peaks on certain slots.

In certain slots that consistently take low post processing time may still have higher than average processing time in other scheduling phases. To prevent overcompensation in such scenarios, 5G-L2-PS constrains any increase in scheduling capacity based on the complete duration taken up by all scheduling phases. By using the worst recent performance observed for the given slot, as the duration of other scheduling phases can vary, due to variation in the number of scheduled UEs.

[Before CB015327-SR-B] 

patternRatio(i) = clamp {min {(-postExcessRatio), ratioLimitDueToRuntime}, (-rdLoadPatternCorrectionMaxDecrease), rdLoadPatternCorrectionMaxIncrease}

where:

postExcessRatio is the IIR average post-scheduling excess ratio for given slot ‘i’, given by:

postExcessRatio = (averageExcessPostSchedTimeInNs(i) / slotDurationNs) *100

ratioLimitDueToRuntime = slotAwareOptimalRatio - (maxPureSchedulingTimeInNs(i) / slotDurationNs* 100)

At start-up 5G-L2-PS shall initialize patternRatio for all the slots as:

patternRatio = 0

[CB015327-SR-B] 

At start-up, 5G-L2-PS shall initialize the parameters as follows:

  * loadPatternCorrectionMaxDecreaseNs = rdLoadPatternCorrectionMaxDecrease / 100 * slotDurationNs
  * loadPatternCorrectionMaxIncreaseNs = rdLoadPatternCorrectionMaxIncrease / 100 * slotDurationNs



Whenever the value of the slot duration (slotDurationNs) changes at runtime according to [11157290](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25ErH_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), 5G-L2-PS shall recalculate the value of the loadPatternCorrectionMaxDecreaseNs and loadPatternCorrectionMaxIncreaseNs with the equations specified above for the start-up and with the new value of slotDurationNs.

In every slot, 5G-L2-PS shall compute the pattern correction time as follows.

patternCorrectionTimeNs(i) = clamp {

min{ -averageExcessPostSchedTimeInNs(i), (slotAwareOptimalRatio / 100 * slotDurationNs - maxPureSchedulingTimeInNs(i)) },

-loadPatternCorrectionMaxDecreaseNs,

loadPatternCorrectionMaxIncreaseNs }

Afterwards, 5G-L2-PS shall convert the value of patternCorrectionTimeNs into a ratio of the slot duration with the following equation:

patternRatio = patternCorrectionTimeNs / slotDurationNs * 100

[End CB015327-SR-B] 

The parameters to compute patternRatio shall belong to the same OLC instance. These are:

  * slotAwareOptimalRatio is defined in [11212562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_RSkOsPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  * maxPureSchedulingTimeInNs(i) - Sliding window maximum of pure scheduling time for the slot ‘i’.
  * averageExcessPostSchedTimeInNsIi) - is defined in [11213602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).
  * rdLoadPatternCorrectionMaxIncrease is defined in [12643907](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_9esnkUIZEfC6a_agjpBoXg).
  * rdLoadPatternCorrectionMaxDecrease is defined in [12643910.](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_PnG-cEIaEfC6a_agjpBoXg)
  * slotDurationNs is the slot duration in nano seconds. [CB015327-SR-B] The value can change at runtime as per [11157290](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25ErH_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9). [End CB015327-SR-B]



Note: To disable CS1 adjustment based on the patternRatio by setting both rdLoadPatternCorrectionMaxDecrease and rdLoadPatternCorrectionMaxIncrease to zero.

---

### 2.14.2.2 Slot-aware Load Control

#### 2.14.2.2.0-1 Slot-aware Load Control Load Types (ID: 11212562)

**2.14.2.2.0-1.0-9**  (ID: `12686328`)

Slot-aware Load Control For the purpose of overload control, 5G-L2-PS shall distinguish the slots in the slot pattern by their load type (loadTypeDlOnly, **loadTypeMixed, loadTypeUlOnly ). A slot's load type expresses whether DL data scheduling, UL data scheduling or both is possible in that slot. The load type depends only on the slot pattern and not on whether DL data scheduling or UL data scheduling actually takes place or not. 5G-L2-PS shall determine the slots' load types by means of the k1 values (5G_UP_ALG_9814_replaced([11116101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp1I4fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_549_replaced([11156818](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25CO0PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and k2 values (5G_UP_ALG_2484_replaced([11116264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_551_replaced([11156960](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25C15_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as described below. k1 and k2 values are determined during the cell setup for the slots in the slot pattern **and don't change at runtime. L2-PS shall not change K1 calculation after modifying numPdschPrbInSsbSlots or numPdschPrbInTrsSlots and K1 will be precalculated during setup even if PDSCH scheduling is not allowed in SSB and TRS slots. If numPdschPrbInSsbSlots or numPdschPrbInTrsSlots will be set to 0 (disabled), then K1 will be calculated but will be not used in SSB and TRS slots (actual, current K1 values per slot will be filled considering PDSCH multiplexing settings). The precalcualted value will be stored per slot and not changed any further. In case when numPdschPrbInSsbSlots or numPdschPrbInTrsSlots is changed from zero value to non-zero value this stored value will be used to fill current K1 values per slot. In case when numPdschPrbInSsbSlots or numPdschPrbInTrsSlots is changed from non-zero value to zero value, actual K1 value for this slot will be set to zero. In case when numPdschPrbInSsbSlots or numPdschPrbInTrsSlots is changed from a non-zero value to another non-zero value, K1 for this slot will not be changed.****

5G-L2-PS shall assume that K1 and K2 values are the same for all cells in the same L2 sub-pool.

Rational:

In classic HW , activation of 2 core L2-Sub Pool deployment with 2 cells per L2 Sub Pool are done by enabling Pooling features (refer to 5G_UP_2406_replaced([11387303](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufF4pfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

In vDU, parity of Pooling feature is not yet supported until 23R3.

For effective use of BB pooling it is required to have same frame structure for all cells in the Pool, such a working assumption can be taken in the design to align with Pooling features parity to be reached in future release.

5G-L2-PS shall use the load types for the following:

  * The schedulers' share of the target duration ratio (5G_L2_5479_replaced([11212394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-ldMfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be slot-aware and it shall depend on the slots' load types. The share of one scheduler is called slotAwareOptimalRatio and is a fraction of the **slotProcessingRatio defined in 5G_L2_15692_replaced([11212528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mESvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**
  * Every set of slots with the same load type shall be controlled by a dedicated overload control (OLC) instance which includes preventive overload control (but excludes FIFO message queue processing, see 5G_L2_1843_replaced([11212803](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-n5evvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and corrective overload control (but excludes FIFO message queue processing, see 5G_L2_1855_replaced([11213045](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-puovvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).



5G-L2-PS shall determine the load types, the schedulers' slotAwareOptimalRatio and the OLC instances as follows:

loadTypeDlOnly:

  * A slot has this load type if it has at least one valid k1 value or k1 value for Msg4 A/N (5G_L2_549_replaced([11156818](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25CO0PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and no k2 value.



Note: There is DL data scheduling in these slots (unless all DL buffers are empty). In addition, there might also be SS burst and/or CSI-RS scheduling.

Note: if above6Ghz (i.e. scs received in the PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq is equal to 120) there is FD parallelization in these slots.

  * No matter if DL and UL scheduler are running on the same core or on different cores:



On DL schedulers: slotAwareOptimalRatio = slotProcessingRatio (5G_L2_15692_replaced([11212528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mESvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). DL OLC instance 1 shall be used.

In the event of more than one DL scheduler in the same core, Load Balancing is done between DL schedulers, refer 5G_L2_5841_replaced([11213804](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-unKfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). DL OLC instances 1 of all DL schedulers on the core shall be used.

loadTypeMixed:

  * This type is attributed to slots where both UL scheduler and Dl scheduler are executed
  * When Single K2 mode is activated (see [11348243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubTk2fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) ) a slot has this load type if it has at least one valid k1 value or k1 value for Msg4 A/N (5G_L2_549_replaced([11156818](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25CO0PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and at least one valid k2 value.
  * Note: When MultiK2 mode is activated(see [11348243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubTk2fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) ), some slots with valid K1 and K2 values are not considered as loadTypeMixed but as loadTypeDlOnly since UL data scheduling is performed in the previous slot for two consecutive slots.



Note: There is DL and UL data scheduling in these slots (unless all DL and/or UL buffers are empty). In addition, there might also be SS burst and/or CSI-RS scheduling.

  * If DL and UL scheduler are running on different cores:



On DL schedulers: slotAwareOptimalRatio = slotProcessingRatio (5G_L2_15692_replaced([11212528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mESvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

On UL schedulers: slotAwareOptimalRatio = slotProcessingRatio (5G_L2_15692_replaced([11212528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mESvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If above6Ghz (i.e. scs received in the PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq is equal to 120) while rdEnableParallelDlFdFor4CC != 0, defined in 5G_L2_11388_replaced([11181657](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27VU7PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and the maximum number of cells in the cellgroup (see numberOfActiveCellsInCellGroup, see 5G_L2_11406_replaced([11141036](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23mrcfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is between rdEnableParallelDlFdFor4CC and 4, DL and UL OLC instance 2 shall be used, otherwise DL and UL OLC instance 1 shall be used.

In FR2 8CC configuration (maxNumberOfCells = 8 and maxNumberOfNrCellGroup = 1), if rdActFr2EnhParallelDlFdFor8CC is set to 1 or set to 2 as defined in 5G_L2_14282_replaced([11181667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27VU7vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), DL and UL OLC instance 2 shall be used, otherwise DL and UL OLC instance 1 shall be used.

[CB012971-WB]

If rdEnableDlFdSchOnULCores([12686252](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wQhl0VMfEfCnPp04H8v-AQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) is set as 1, DL OLC instance 2 shall be used.

[End CB012971-WB]

  * Otherwise:



For share calculation in loadTypeMixed slots see 5G_L2_5839_replaced([11213794](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-unJ_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

On DL schedulers: DL OLC instance 2 shall be used.

On UL schedulers: UL OLC instance 2 shall be used.

Note: if above6Ghz (i.e. scs received in the PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq is equal to 120) while the maximum number of cells in the cellgroup (see numberOfActiveCellsInCellGroup, see 5G_L2_11406_replaced([11141036](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23mrcfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 4 and rdEnableParallelDlFdFor4CC != 0, defined in 5G_L2_11388_replaced([11181657](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27VU7PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), DL and UL scheduler are running on different cores and there is no Fd parallelization.

In the event of at least 1 DL and 1 UL scheduler and additional DL/UL schedulers in the same core, Load balancing is done between the DL and UL schedulers on the core, the OLC instance 2 of each of the scheduler are used to evaluate the load state of each of the scheduler.

loadTypeUlOnly:

  * A slot has this load type if it has at least one valid k2 value and no k1 value and no k1 value for Msg4 A/N (5G_L2_549_replaced([11156818](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25CO0PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).



Note: There is UL data scheduling in these slots (unless all UL buffers are empty). In addition, there is also SS burst and/or CSI-RS scheduling in these slots and that is why the UL scheduler is allocated only part of slotProcessingRatio **if DL and UL scheduler are running on the same core.**

  * If DL and UL scheduler are running on different cores:



On UL schedulers: slotAwareOptimalRatio = slotProcessingRatio (5G_L2_15692_replaced([11212528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mESvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) . UL OLC instance 1 shall be used.

  * Otherwise:



On UL schedulers: slotAwareOptimalRatio = rdUlProcessingShareInUlOnlySlots * slotProcessingRatio (5G_L2_15692_replaced([11212528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mESvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). UL OLC instance 1 shall be used.

rdUlProcessingShareInUlOnlySlots is defined in 5G_L2_5893_replaced([11190262](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28VaevvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In the event of more than one UL scheduler in the same core, Load Balancing is done between UL schedulers. refer 5G_L2_5841_replaced([11213804](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-unKfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). UL OLC instances 1 of all the UL scheduler shall be used.

For slots which don't match the above conditions for loadTypeDlOnly, loadTypeMixed or loadTypeUlOnly the load type is undefined.

Notes:

  1. For tdLteConfig0 frame structure, the L2-PS timing is adjusted comparing with legacy TDD FR1 frame structure, for those slots with 1 K1 + 1 K2 or 1 K1 + 2 K2 the DL and UL scheduler are running sequentially in the same core. 



So the load Type check shall follow the legacy L2-PS slot timing or base on the scheduling type. For example, for tdLteConfig0 slot 2, there will be 3 slot types running in different slot individually which are loadTypeDlOnly, loadTypeUlOnly, loadTypeUlOnly. 

Only when NRCELL.actEnhancedPDSCHSchSplSlot is true, there will be only one slot which has both DL and UL scheduling and the load type shall be set to loadTypeMixed.

Refer to [12705724: Relationship between tdLte Config0 and legacy TDD FR1 frame structure's timing](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kFbSo2FcEfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

---

### 2.14.2.3 Preventive Load Control

#### 2.14.2.3.0-1 Preventive Load Control Overview (ID: 11212618)

**2.14.2.3.0-1.0-8**  (ID: `11212663`)

Preventive Load Control A preventive control is needed to avoid the whole 5G-L2-PS to enter overload state by continuously adjusting the 5G-L2-PS scheduling capacity in the current slot, according to the processing duration in the previous slots.

The objective is to maintain the scheduler processing duration as close as possible to the target rdOptimalSlotProcessingRatio (5G_L2_5930_replaced([11190056](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28UMVPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If actTwoCoresL2DeploymentFddFr1 = false

  * When two cell setup on one core , the target rdOptimalSlotProcessingRatio will be multiplied by rdSlotProcessingPercentForTwoCellsPerCore(5G_L2_7002_replaced([11190099](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28UMXPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

  * When two cell setup on one L2 Sub Pool, the target rdOptimalSlotProcessingRatio will be multiplied by rdSlotProcessingPercentforTwoCellsperL2sp (5G_L2_10206_replaced([11190135](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28UzY_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).




5G-L2-PS shall compute the effective optimal slot processing ratio per cell as follows, taking into account the limitations of rdSlotProcessingPercentForTwoCellsPerCore and rdSlotProcessingPercentforTwoCellsperL2sp from above:

IF (2 cells running on the core AND actTwoCoresL2DeploymentFddFr1 = False) : optimalSlotProcessingRatio = rdOptimalSlotProcessingRatio * rdSlotProcessingPercentForTwoCellsPerCore

ELSE IF (2 cells set up on one L2 sub-pool AND actTwoCoresL2DeploymentFddFr1 = False) : optimalSlotProcessingRatio = rdOptimalSlotProcessingRatio * rdSlotProcessingPercentforTwoCellsperL2sp

ELSE IF (2 cells up to [Before CB009836-C] 5 [CB009836-C] 6 [End CB009836-C] set up on one L2 sub-pool AND actTwoCoresL2DeploymentFddFr1 = True): optimalSlotProcessingRatio = rdOptimalSlotProcessingRatio *

(100 - (rdSlotProcessingPercentReductionPerSchedulerForMultipleCellsPerL2sp(5G_L2_15906_replaced([11190144](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28UzZvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) * (Number of schedulers per core in given slot - 1) ) ) / 100

ELSE: optimalSlotProcessingRatio = rdOptimalSlotProcessingRatio

If duplexMode(5G_L2_IF_14_replaced([10966124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UMlxPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is = FDD AND L1Variant(5G_L2_IF_75_replaced([10967982](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UVvtvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = Loner, optimalSlotProcessingRatio = optimalSlotProcessingRatio / 2

IF (single cell running on a core): optimalSlotProcessingRatio += rdSlotProcessingExtensionSingleCell_perCent(5G_L2_12843_replaced([11190121](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28UzYfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

5G-L2-PS shall use the value of optimalSlotProcessingRatio from above as input to 5G_L2_15692_replaced([11212528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mESvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) only.

5G-L2-PS shall not use the value of optimalSlotProcessingRatio from above in any other requirement.

The calculation of UE metrics is the most CPU-consuming part inside the UL and DL schedulers.)

The adjusted scheduling capacity is thus applied to the number of candidate UEs on which these metrics are calculated, i.e. :  
\- The number of UEs in CS1 lists (UL and/or DL),  
When reducing the number of UEs in CS1 list (and then also CS2), at least one candidate UE must remain in each CS2 list, in order to maintain the cell throughput.

This mechanism is implemented separately in both UL and DL schedulers. DL and UL schedulers can be of two different cells in the same L2 Sub Pool. If actTwoCoresL2DeploymentFddFr1 is set to True DL and UL schedulers can be of up to [Before CB009836-C] five [CB009836-C] six [End CB009836-C] different cells in the same L2 Sub Pool.

There can be multiple instances of this mechanism, see 5G_L2_6333_replaced([11212562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Details can be found in 5G_L2_1835_replaced([11212669](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-nSZPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) & 5G_L2_1843_replaced([11212803](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-n5evvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For actTwoCoresL2DeploymentFddFr1 see 5G_L2_16485_replaced([11141119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23mrf_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Impacted requirements :

\- [5G_UP_ALG_4825_replaced([11195013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv4tnvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] for UL Scheduler may select less than rdMaxNumUeTdUl UEs for CS1List construction

\- [5G_UP_ALG_4209_replaced([11174627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudxRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] for DL Scheduler may select less than rdMaxNumUeTdDl UEs for CS1List construction

---

#### 2.14.2.3.1 Scheduling capacity monitoring

##### 2.14.2.3.1.0-1 Scheduling capacity monitoring Algorithm Selection (ID: 11212673)

**2.14.2.3.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11212689`)

Scheduling capacity monitoring [Before CB006784-A]

L2-PS UL scheduler shall follow the algorithm described in 5G_L2_1839_replaced([11212694](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-nSafvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

L2-PS DL scheduler shall follow the algorithm described in 5G_L2_1841_replaced([11212749](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-n5cPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB006784-A]

Both L2-PS UL & DL Scheduler shall follow the algorithm described in 5G_L2_1841_replaced([11212749](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-n5cPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[End CB006784-A]

---

##### 2.14.2.3.1.0-2 Scheduling capacity monitoring Control based on R&amp;D parameters (ID: 11212694)

**2.14.2.3.1.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `11212743`)

Scheduling capacity monitoring [Before CNI-110671]

Adjusted scheduling capacity :

slotSchedulingRatio(N) is computed for slot N as the ratio of slot time used by scheduling :

slotSchedulingRatio(N) = 100 * (SlotProcessingEndTime(N) – SlotStartTime(N) + numOfSkippedFd * fdProcessTime_uSec) / SlotDurationTime

numOfSkippedFd is the number of carriers skipped by Fd schedulers in current slot (cf 5G_L2_236_replaced([11148585](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24RZ4PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

When several Fd Eos run in parallel on multiple cores, numOfSkippedFd is the highest number of skipped carriers by Fd EOs in current slot.

fdProcessTime_uSec is set with rdParallelFdProcessTime_uSec when Fd scheduling is performed in separate EO.

Otherwise fdProcessTime_uSec is set with rdSequentialFdProcessTime_uSec.

[image-0][image_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating a timeline with various events and durations related to 5G communication. The timeline is represented by a horizontal blue line. On the left side, a blue rectangle contains the text "5GTimer Requested by L2-RT EO", indicating a request originating from the L2-RT EO. Moving along the timeline from left to right: \- A green arrow labeled "btuReferenceSync" points to the right, originating from a point labeled "SynchroReceptionBtu". This suggests a synchronization event related to BTU reception. \- A vertical line labeled "SynchroSlotind" is positioned further to the right. \- A red arrow labeled "Slot Processing Duration" originates from "SynchroSlotind" and points to the right. \- A blue arrow labeled "Slot Duration" spans a significant portion of the timeline, starting from a point near "SynchroSlotind" and extending to a point labeled "Schedulingprocessing End". \- A vertical line labeled "Schedulingprocessing End" marks the end of the slot processing. \- A small vertical marker with "N+1" and an arrow pointing upwards is located at the very end of the "Slot Duration" timeline. \- There are also some smaller markers and labels like "T", "N", and "Z" along the timeline, which likely represent specific time points or offsets. The diagram visually represents the timing relationships between synchronization, slot processing, and the overall slot duration in a 5G system.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_11329.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

CapacityRatio(N+1) is computed based on slotSchedulingRatio(N):

CapacityRatio(N+1) = 100 – (slotSchedulingRatio(N) – slotProcessingRatio(N))

A hysteresis mechanism is added:

if computed CapacityRatio(N+1) is between LowerBound and UpperBound, capacity is left unchanged.

If computed CapacityRatio(N+1) is above UpperBound capacity is increased,

if computed CapacityRatio(N+1) is below LowerBound capacity is decreased.

if CapaciityRatio(N+1) < UpperBound and CapacityRatio(N+1) > LowerBound

CapacityRatio(N+1) = 100

With

UpperBound = 1

LowerBound = 100 + rdOvCtrlInnerLoopCapaRatioHysteresisPercent (see 5G_L2_5004_replaced([11190209](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28VacfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

if CapacityRatio(N+1) > 100

increasingStep = (slotSchedulingRatio(N) – slotProcessingRatio(N)) * rdSchedulingCapacityStepIncrease) / slotProcessingRatio(N)

else

increasingStep = 0

And then applied to SchedulingCapacity(N) to get SchedulingCapacity(N+1) as follows :

SchedulingCapacity(N+1) = MAX(1, MIN (CapacityRatio(N+1) * SchedulingCapacity(N) + increasingStep) / 100, MaxSchedulingCapacity))

With MaxSchedulingCapacity equals rdMaxNumUeTdDl for Dl and rdMaxNumUeTdUl for UL scheduler.

With:

  * rdOptimalSlotProcessingRatio is defined in 5G_L2_5930_replaced([11190056](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28UMVPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * slotProcessingRatio(N) is defined in 5G_L2_15692_replaced([11212528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mESvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). It is the value which is valid in the current slot N.



[End CNI-110671]

---

##### 2.14.2.3.1.0-3 Scheduling capacity monitoring Control based on run-time measurements (preventive) (ID: 11212749)

**2.14.2.3.1.0-3.0-9**  (ID: `12775993`)

Scheduling capacity monitoring In every OLC instance defined in [11212556: Slot-aware overload control](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrUPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) 5G-L2-PS shall maintain [Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size [CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive [End CNI-136895-A] as the maximum number of UEs in the CS1 list to be proposed by preventive overload control.

Initialization:

  * At startup 5G-L2-PS shall initialize [Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size [CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive [End CNI-136895-A] in all DL OLC instances with rdMaxNumUeTdDl ([11182022](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27YYNvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and [Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size [CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive [End CNI-136895-A] in all UL OLC instances with rdMaxNumUeTdUl ([11182963](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27fs-fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).



Updates: 

  * At the end of the slot processing 5G-L2-PS shall update [Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size [CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive [End CNI-136895-A] by means of the avgSlotProcessingTime and the avgSlotDelay (see [11213602: Exponential Averages](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) which belong to the same OLC instance as [Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size [CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive [End CNI-136895-A]. However, in FR2, **this update shall only be carried out if avgSlotProcessingTime and avgSlotDelay have been updated in the current slot (see [11213648: Updates of Average Measurements](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZC_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)). In FR1 this update shall be carried out always. 



[PR848579] 5G-L2-PS shall memorize the value of cs1ListMaxSizePreventive before the update in the internal variable cs1ListMaxSizePreventivePrevious. [End PR848579]**

  * 5G-L2-PS shall update an instance of [Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size [CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive [End CNI-136895-A] as:
  * **FR1: slotProcessingRatio = slotProcessingTime / (slotDuration - avgSlotDelay)**
  * **FR2: slotProcessingRatio = avgSlotProcessingTime / (slotDuration - avgSlotDelay)**
  * capacityRatio = 1 - (slotProcessingRatio - slotAwareOptimalRatio)
  * [Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size = avgCs1Size + (capacityRatio - 1)/unitStepInCapacityRatio
  * [CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive = cs1ListMaxSizePreventive + (capacityRatio - 1)/unitStepInCapacityRatio [End CNI-136895-A]



IF (actFdmUeSkippingOlc = TRUE) AND (actFdmScheduling = TRUE)**: 5G-L2-PS shall skip the below instruction.**

ELSE: 5G-L2-PS shall execute the below instruction.

If slotDelay(n) < avgSlotDelay:  
[Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size = avgCs1Size - numSkippedUes * rdCs1ListSizeDecreaseStep  
[CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive = cs1ListMaxSizePreventive - numSkippedUes * rdCs1ListSizeDecreaseStep [End CNI-136895-A]

[PR848579] If correctiveCs1ListMaxSizeReductionFactor < rdMinCs1ReductionOverallForOlcAverage 5G-L2-PS shall discard updates of cs1ListMaxSizePreventive if the updated value is greater than the previous value. To this end, 5G-L2-PS shall set 

cs1ListMaxSizePreventive = min{ cs1ListMaxSizePreventive, cs1ListMaxSizePreventivePrevious }

Note: In slots with correctiveCs1ListMaxSizeReductionFactor < rdMinCs1ReductionOverallForOlcAverage the time measurements in [11213441: Measurements per OLC Instance](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)  
have extraordinarily small values which bias the decisions of preventive load control towards too high max CS1 list sizes. [End PR848579]

where,

  * slotAwareOptimalRatio is specified in [11212556: Slot-aware overload control](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrUPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) and [11213788: DL/UL Load Balancing](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-unJvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9). 5G-L2-PS shall select the value for the load type of the current slot and the right scheduler deployment.
  * unitStepInCapacityRatio = rdMinSlotProcessingTimeForCs1SizeUpdateUs / (slotDuration * slotAwareOptimalRatio)
  * rdMinSlotProcessingTimeForCs1SizeUpdateUs is an R&D parameter described in [11189880](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28S-NvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  * numSkippedUes is described in [11213529: slotProcessingTime](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sx9_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
  * rdCs1ListSizeDecreaseStep is an R&D parameter described in [11189898](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28S-O_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  * actFdmUeSkippingOlc is received in the PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq (see [10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * slotProcessingTime is defined in [11213529: slotProcessingTime](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sx9_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
  * slotDuration is the processing time Budget for a slot and depends on the numerology (FR1 FDD 1000us, FR1 TDD 500us, FR2 TDD 125us), see [11156739: Slot Duration](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25BnwfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
  * [PR848579] correctiveCs1ListMaxSizeReductionFactor is computed in [11212913: Adaptation to Late Slot Processing](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-ogjfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9). [End PR848579]
  * [PR848579] rdMinCs1ReductionOverallForOlcAverage is defined in [11191111](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28bhFvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). [End PR848579]



In FR1 TDD, when actFlexibleBiSlotDurationMode is set to "partial" or "full" and the 750us timing pattern (as defined in [11157164: Eligibility and activation conditions for 0.75ms timing pattern](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25EEEfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) is activated, the biSlot duration is extented by 250us, resulting in a total processing budget of 750us.

**2.14.2.3.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13386489`)

Scheduling capacity monitoring Every OLC instance shall perform the following actions if the value of numOfConsecutiveSlotsWithoutUes in [11213693](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAFPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) is greater than or equal to 100.
