#### 2.14.2.3.2 FIFO message queue processing

##### 2.14.2.3.2.0-1 FIFO message queue processing Prio 0 FIFO Queues (ID: 11212808)

**2.14.2.3.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11212820`)

FIFO message queue processing [Before CB009092-A] 5G-L2-PS always processes all messages in prio 0 FIFO queue.

[CB009092-A] 5G-L2-PS processes the messages in prio 0 FIFO queue according to the policy defined by rdEventTimeCheckingPolicyForPrio0 (5G_L2_8476_replaced([11190346](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28WBivvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB009092-A]

---

##### 2.14.2.3.2.0-2 FIFO message queue processing Prio 1 FIFO Queues (ID: 11212827)

**2.14.2.3.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11212837`)

FIFO message queue processing [Before CB009092-A]

5G-L2-PS always processes all messages in prio 1 FIFO queues.

[CB009092-A]

5G-L2-PS shall apply the policy defined by rdEventTimeCheckingPolicyForPrio1 (5G_L2_8476_replaced([11190346](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28WBivvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to the messages in this queue.

[End CB009092-A]

---

##### 2.14.2.3.2.0-3 FIFO message queue processing Prio 2 FIFO Queue (ID: 11212845)

**2.14.2.3.2.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11212862`)

FIFO message queue processing [Before CB009092-A]

For each message in prio 2 FIFO queue, 5G-L2-PS only processes the message if the remaining time in the current slot exceeds 10us.

[CB009092-A]

5G-L2-PS shall apply the policy defined by rdEventTimeCheckingPolicyForPrio2 (5G_L2_8476_replaced([11190346](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28WBivvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to the messages in this queue.

[End CB009092-A]

This mechanism is only implemented in DL schedulers.

This mechanism is not slot-aware and shall run in all slots on the DL schedulers.

##### 2.14.2.3.2.0-4 FIFO message queue processing Prio 3 FIFO Queue (ID: 11212869)

**2.14.2.3.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11212873`)

FIFO message queue processing 5G-L2-PS shall apply the policy defined by rdEventTimeCheckingPolicyForPrio3 (5G_L2_8476_replaced([11190346](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28WBivvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to the messages in this queue.

This mechanism is only implemented in DL schedulers.

This mechanism is not slot-aware and shall run in all slots on the DL schedulers.

#### 2.14.2.3.3 FIFO message queue processing order

##### 2.14.2.3.3.0-1 FIFO message queue processing order FIFO dequeue in ascending order (ID: 11212885)

**2.14.2.3.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11212896`)

FIFO message queue processing order When there are multi schedulers on one core, if there is any messages in the low prio FIFO message queues, messages pop from the low FIFO queue and handling should be after all schedulers.

And when rdFifoPopAscendingOrderOnTheCore(5G_L2_19453_replaced([11191058](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28a6DfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is true for current cell technology(FR2, FR1 TDD or FDD), the dequeue for all the FIFO on N schedulers on the core should be done from high priority to low priority as bellow:

### 2.14.2.4 Corrective Load Control

#### 2.14.2.4.0-2 Corrective Load Control When overload is triggered by the TTI processing duration, 5G-L2-PS implements a corrective control by reducing [PR817215] or increasing [End PR817215] its scheduling capacity in the current slot, as long as it is in overload state, separately but possibly in addition to the preventive control. The reduced scheduling capacity is applied to: - The number of UEs in CS1 lists (UL and/or DL), - The number of UEs in CS2 lists (UL and/or DL on each CC). [PR817215] The increase in scheduling capacity is applied to: The number of UEs in CS1 lists (UL and/or DL) [End PR817215] This mechanism is implemented separately in both UL and DL schedulers if they are run on different cores. When reducing the number of UEs in either CS1 or CS2 list, at least one candidate UE must remain in both CS1 and CS2 lists. [PR817215] While increasing the number of UEs in CS1 list, the number of UEs must not be increased beyond the absolute maximum number of UEs in CS1 list. [End PR817215] Details can be found in 5G_L2_1847_replaced( 11212913 ) [Before PR817215] &amp; 5G_L2_6715_replaced( 11213061 ) [PR817215], 11213045 &amp; 12645241 [End PR817215] Note that the adjusted scheduling capacity mechanism in the preventive overload control above allows the scheduling capacity to increase again when 5G-L2-PS goes out of the overload state. Impacted requirements: - [5G_UP_ALG_4825_replaced( 11195013 )] for UL Scheduler may select less than rdMaxNumUeTdUl  UEs for CS1List - [5G_UP_ALG_4209_replaced( 11174627 )] for DL Scheduler may select less than rdMaxNumUeTdDl  UEs for CS1List - [5G_UP_ALG_4101_replaced( 11173728 )] CS2 list size may be lower than CS1 list size - [5G_UP_ALG_4766_replaced( 11194284 )]  CS2 list size may be lower than CS1 list size (ID: 12644417)

#### 2.14.2.4.1 Adaptation to late Slot Processing

##### 2.14.2.4.1.0-1 Adaptation to late Slot Processing Algorithm Selection (ID: 11212918)

**2.14.2.4.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11212935`)

Adaptation to late Slot Processing [Before CB006784-A]

UL scheduler shall follow the algorithm described in 5G_L2_1851_replaced([11212942](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-pHkvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

DL scheduler shall follow the algorithm described in 5G_L2_1853_replaced([11212970](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-pHlfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB006784-A]

Both L2-PS DL & UL schedulers shall follow the algorithm described in 5G_L2_1853_replaced([11212970](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-pHlfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[End CB006784-A]

---

##### 2.14.2.4.1.0-2 Adaptation to late Slot Processing Control based on R&amp;D Parameters (ID: 11212942)

**2.14.2.4.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11212962`)

Adaptation to late Slot Processing [Before CNI-110671]

The principle is to reduce the scheduling capacity proportionally to the remaining time in the allowed btu window (with respect to the whole window), as soon as rdOverloadOuterLoopThreshold has been reached.

When several schedulers are deployed on the same core this detection mechanism is performed only on the first scheduler activated in the slot, and the computed ratio is applied to all schedulers running on the same core.

Remaining slot ratio :

if ReceivedSlotNr = PreviousSlotNr + 1 then

RemainingSlotRatio = 1 - (SynchroReceptionBtu - BtuSlotLowerBoundary) /

(BtuSlotUpperBoundary - BtuSlotLowerBoundary)

else (trigger is received too late, so slot is skipped)

RemainingSlotRatio = 0

endif

Where:

SynchroReceptionBtu: BTU polled from BBP UPHWAPI current SW BCN

BtuSlotLowerBoundary: Slot lower scheduling BTU boundary acceptance. ref [5G_L1L2_FLOW_672_replaced([11177470](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeTrwvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]

BtuSlotUpperBoundary: Slot upper scheduling BTU boundary acceptance. ref [5G_L1L2_FLOW_672_replaced([11177470](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeTrwvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]

[image-0][image_desc]The image is a timing diagram illustrating the relationship between different timing signals in a 5G system. It shows three horizontal timelines representing different entities: "5GTimer Requested by L2-RT EO", "BCN RP1 Basis for 5GTimer", and "BCN Antenna (RP1 + HW delay) Basis for L1". The top timeline shows a request for a "5GTimer" from the "L2-RT EO" at a point labeled "N-1". A reference point "Ref BTU" is indicated, with an acceptable deviation range defined by "LB" and "UB" and a parameter "p". There is also a "Slot Offset" indicated. The middle timeline represents "BCN RP1" which serves as the basis for the "5GTimer". It shows time instances labeled "TTI N-1", "TTI N", and "TTI N+1". The bottom timeline represents "BCN Antenna" which is based on "RP1 + HW delay" and serves as the basis for "L1". It shows a starting point at "TTI N-1" with a duration indicated by a purple bar. A "HW delay" is shown between "TTI N" on the middle timeline and "TTI N" on the bottom timeline. This timeline also shows time instances labeled "TTI N" and "TTI N+1". Vertical dashed lines indicate synchronization points at "TTI N-1" and "TTI N". Arrows labeled "N-1" and "N+1" are present at the top, indicating time progression.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_11364.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

Slot scheduling processing acceptance boundaries

Reduced scheduling capacity :

The corrective overload control will further adapt the scheduling capacity from 5G_L2_1833_replaced([11212618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrWvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) as follows:

if remainingSlotRatio < rdOverloadOuterLoopThreshold then

schedulingCapacity(N) = max (remainingSlotRatio * schedulingCapacity(N, 1)

endif

Where:

N: currently processed slot number

rdOverloadOuterLoopThreshold: remaining ratio which triggers overload control. [R&D parameter]

[End CNI-110671]

---

##### 2.14.2.4.1.0-3 Adaptation to late Slot Processing Control based on run-time measurements (corrective) (ID: 11212970)

**2.14.2.4.1.0-3.0-14**  (ID: `13437689`)

Adaptation to late Slot Processing In every OLC instance defined in [11212556: Slot-aware Load Control](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrUPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) 5G-L2-PS shall maintain cs1Size as the maximum number of UEs in the CS1 list to be proposed by corrective load control. Therefore, 5G-L2-PS shall consider the maximum CS1 list size (cs1ListMaxSizePreventive) proposed by preventive load control (see [11212669: Scheduling capacity monitoring](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-nSZPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and reduce it further at the beginning of the current slot n based on the below conditions.

[CB015327-SR-B]   
IF (actEnhCorrectiveOlcForRTSched = FALSE) OR (rdActEnhancedCorrectiveOlc.Bit0 = 0) THEN:

{ 

5G-L2-PS shall proceed as follows. [End CB015327-SR-B]

If slotDelay(n) > avgSlotDelay:

If 2 cells deployed on the same core and actTwoCoresL2DeploymentFddFr1 = False

reductionRatio = 1 - (slotDelay(n) - avgSlotDelay)/ **(2*avgPreAndTdTime)**

Else If ((TDD deployment with 3 cells in one L2 Sub Pool) or (actTwoCoresL2DeploymentFddFr1 = True) )

reductionRatio = 1 - ((slotDelay(n) - avgSlotDelay) * slotAwareOptimalRatio / (avgPreAndTdTime))

For slotAwareOptimalRatio see [11212556: Slot-aware Load Control](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrUPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) and [11213788: DL/UL Load Balancing](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-unJvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

Else:

reductionRatio = 1 - (slotDelay(n) - avgSlotDelay)/avgPreAndTdTime

adaptedCs1ListSize = max{1, cs1ListMaxSizePreventive * reductionRatio}

Else:

adaptedCs1ListSize = cs1ListMaxSizePreventive

5G-L2-PS shall determine the reduction of the maximum CS1 list size performed by corrective OLC in the current slot due to the slot delay as:

correctiveCs1ListMaxSizeReductionFactorDueToSlotDelay = floor{ adaptedCs1ListSize } / floor{ cs1ListMaxSizePreventive }

5G-L2-PS shall use correctiveCs1ListMaxSizeReductionFactorDueToSlotDelay at the end of the slot to check whether the exponential averaging filters shall be updated or not, as described in [11213648: Updates of Average Measurements](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZC_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

IF actLastSchedulerOlcEnh = TRUE:

{

5G-L2-PS shall reduce the CS1 list size in the current slot n further, if the scheduler's remaining slot budget is going to overlap the time reservation for FIFO message queue processing ([11213045: FIFO Message Queue Processing](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-puovvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)). This can happen if another scheduler was running before in the same slot on the same core and has spent more time than allowed. 5G-L2-PS shall compute the following time spans:

remainingSlotBudget = (slotDuration*slotProcessingRatio - slotDelay) * (slotAwareOptimalRatio / (slotProcessingRatio)) - elapsedTimeSinceSlotStart

timeTillSlotReserveStart = timeTillSlotBoundary - (slotDuration * (1 - slotProcessingRatio))

Note: On deployments where every scheduler is running on a core of its own, it is expected that these two time spans are always identical.

5G-L2-PS shall perform the CS1 list size reduction as follows.

IF timeTillSlotReserveStart + margin < remainingSlotBudget:

adaptedCs1ListSize = max { 1, min { adaptedCs1ListSize * timeTillSlotReserveStart / (slotDuration * slotAwareOptimalRatio), adaptedCs1ListSize - 1 } }

}

5G-L2-PS shall adapt the CS1 list size in the current slot based on the appliedAditionalReserveRatio as below:

cs1Size(n) = max{ 1, min { cs1Size(n) * (slotAwareOptimalRatio - additionalReserveRatio) / slotAwareOptimalRatio, maxCs1Size} }

5G-L2-PS shall adapt the CS1 list size in the current slot based on the variation in processing required in post-scheduling phase as described in [13458115: Max CS1 Size Correction (Load Pattern)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_K1xCtS5kEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

[CB015327-SR-B] 

}

ELSE:

{

5G-L2-PS shall compute adaptedCs1ListSize as specified in [13448699: Max CS1 Size Correction (Scheduler Budgets)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_buYmUihpEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

5G-L2-PS shall compute correctiveCs1ListMaxSizeReductionFactorDueToSlotDelay as specified in [13471771: Correction Factor due to Slot Delay](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_hhNeZTlxEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

}

[End CB015327-SR-B]

cs1Size(n) = floor{ adaptedCs1ListSize } or 1 due to FIFO overload as [11212441: FIFO message queues state](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-ldOvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

// Reduction of max CS1 list based on PsUser procedure

For processing procedures on the PsUser interface ([10974490](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U8Mrfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G-L2-PS shall reduce the max CS1 size list if the following conditions are met:

  * The given core is responsible for receiving and responding to requests on the PsUser interface.
  * numOfPendingPsUserProcedures > rdPsUserEventsThreshold



Then 5G-L2-PS shall reduce max CS1 list size as below:

adaptedCs1ListSize = max { 1, adaptedCs1ListSize - rdCs1SizeReductionPerEvent * (numOfPendingPsUserProcedures - rdPsUserEventsThreshold)}

// Reduction of max CS1 list based on C-Plane events

IF nbTotalFlushableEvents > rdMaxOverloadQueueSizeForPrio3:

{

5G-L2-PS shall determine the reduction of the maximum CS1 list size computed by corrective OLC based on number of events in FIFO queue as below:

adaptedCs1ListSize = max { 1, adaptedCs1ListSize - rdCs1SizeReductionPerEvent * (nbTotalFlushableEvents - rdMaxOverloadQueueSizeForPrio3)}

}

// Reduction of max CS1 list based on Low priority event (prio-0) in System queues

5G-L2-PS shall determine the reduction of the maximum CS1 list size computed by corrective OLC based on number of events in low priority System queue as below:

adaptedCs1ListSize = max { 1, adaptedCs1ListSize - rdCs1SizeReductionPerEvent * max { 0, (numOfLowestPrioSysQueueEvents - rdSysQueueOverloadThreshold)} }

with:

numOfLowestPrioSysQueueEvents: the number of lowest priority events (prio-0) present in System Queue at current slot.

IF (/NRBTS/NRcell/actFdmSchedulingInitialBWP =TRUE) AND UPLINK AND (the number of initial transmission of MSG3 > 1):

cs1Size(n) = max(numberOfMsg3Ues,min(floor{ adaptedCs1ListSize }, estimatedCs1ListSize))

With:

IF estimatedPreAndTdTimeExcepMsg3 < avgPreAndTdTime

estimatedCs1ListSize = 12 for FDD, 18 for TDD

ELSE

estimatedCs1ListSize = (estimatedPreAndTdTimeExcepMsg3 - avgPreAndTdTime) / 2 + 12 (for FDD) or 18 (for TDD)

with:

estimatedPreAndTdTimeExcepMsg3 = (slotDuration - slotDelay) * (slotAwareOptimalRatio / numOfCellsPerCore) - avgPostSchedTime - totalFdTimeOfInitialMsg3.

totalFdTimeOfInitialMsg3 = avgFdFirstUeTime + avgFdUeTime * (the number of Initial Msg3 - 1) + avgFdCommonTime.

numberOfMsg3Ues: the number of msg3 to be scheduled at current slot.

The resultant cs1Size(n) is the maximum CS1 list size proposed by corrective overload control for the current slot n.

5G-L2-PS shall determine the reduction of the maximum CS1 list size performed by corrective OLC in the current slot as:

correctiveCs1ListMaxSizeReductionFactor = floor{ cs1Size(n) } / floor{ cs1ListMaxSizePreventive }

5G-L2-PS shall use correctiveCs1ListMaxSizeReductionFactor at the end of the slot to check whether the exponential averaging filters shall be updated or not, as described in [11213648: Updates of Average Measurements](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZC_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

5G-L2-PS shall use correctiveCs1ListMaxSizeReductionFactor in preventive load control, see [11212669: Scheduling capacity monitoring](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-nSZPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

The parameters to compute cs1Size shall belong to the same OLC instance as cs1Size. These are:

  * cs1ListMaxSizePreventive is the maximum CS1 list size proposed by preventive overload control (see [11212669: Scheduling capacity monitoring](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-nSZPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).
  * slotDelay(n) is the initial slot delay for the current slot n, see [11213446: Scheduling Phases](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
  * avgSlotDelay, avgPreAndTdTime, **avgPostSchedTime , avgFdFirstUeTime, avgFdUeTime and avgFdCommonTime are the average measurements of slotDelay & preTdTime as described in [11213602: Exponential Averages](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).**
  * slotAwareOptimalRatio is defined in [11212556: Slot-aware Load Control](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrUPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) and [11213788: DL/UL Load Balancing](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-unJvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
  * actLastSchedulerOlcEnh is received in the PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq (see [10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * numOfCellsPerCore: The number of cells set up on the core.
  * elapsedTimeSinceSlotStart: On the DL scheduler (or UL scheduler) it is the time which has elapsed since the start of DL pre-scheduling (or UL pre-scheduling respectively).
  * timeTillSlotBoundary: The time which is left in the current slot.
  * margin corresponds to 1 us.
  * For actTwoCoresL2DeploymentFddFr1 see 5G_L2_16485_replaced([11141119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23mrf_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * slotDuration is the processing time Budget for a slot and depends on the numerology (FR1 FDD 1000us, FR1 TDD 500us, FR2 TDD 125us), see [11156739: Slot Duration](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25BnwfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
  * numOfPendingPsUserProcedures is equal to the number of request messages received on the PsUser interface to which 5G-L2-PS has not responded yet.
  * nbTotalFlushableEvents is the number of flushable events in Prio3 FIFO queue.
  * rdMaxOverloadQueueSizeForPrio3 is defined in [11190401](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Wok_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Wok_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").
  * rdCs1SizeReductionPerEvent is defined in [12683446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_XvYBkVIqEfCeeMlEb49MrQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_5KBG5p5DEe2A-5U7tzedRA "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_XvYBkVIqEfCeeMlEb49MrQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_5KBG5p5DEe2A-5U7tzedRA").
  * rdPsUserEventsThreshold is defined in [12693585](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_u3jngVigEfCIAJ9nOfeS0w?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_u3jngvigefciaj9nofes0w?oslc_config.context=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2fgc%2fconfiguration%2f9").
  * rdSysQueueOverloadThreshold is defined in [13365815](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_yegKAPaWEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_yegKAPaWEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").
  * [CB015327-SR-B] actEnhCorrectiveOlcForRTSched is received in PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq (see [10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)). [End CB015327-SR-B]
  * [CB015327-SR-B] rdActEnhancedCorrectiveOlc is defined in [13383207](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_6deOpQD9EfGhFrIQm2O4Ew?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9). [End CB015327-SR-B]



In FR1 TDD, when actFlexibleBiSlotDurationMode is set to "partial" or "full" and the 750us timing pattern (as defined in 5G_L2_22818_replaced([11157164](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25EEEfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is activated, the bi-Slot duration is extended by 250us, resulting in a total processing budget of 750us.

---

#### 2.14.2.4.2 Adaptation to Variation in Post-Scheduling Phase

##### 2.14.2.4.2.0-1 Adaptation to Variation in Post-Scheduling Phase Max CS1 Size Correction (Load Pattern) (ID: 13458115)

**2.14.2.4.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12774565`)

Adaptation to Variation in Post-Scheduling Phase This mechanism is slot-aware and slot-specific. 5G-L2-PS adjusts the size of the CS1 list (either increasing or decreasing it) based on the patternRatio for each given slot. This adjustment depends on how long the post-scheduling phase takes during runtime for that given slot, as described in [12645241](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_wjOMNkK0EfCH-cG2YrVgkA).

This mechanism is available for both DL and UL schedulers.

In each OLC instance defined in [11212562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_RSkOsPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ), 5G-L2-PS shall maintain cs1Size, which is the maximum number of UEs allowed in the CS1 list by the corrective overload control. To determine this, it considers the [Before CNI-136895-A] average CS1 list size (avgCs1Size) [CNI-136895-A] maximum CS1 list size (cs1ListMaxSizePreventive) [End CNI-136895-A] proposed by the preventive overload control ([11212669](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_R28uIPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), which is then adjusted by the ‘Late slot processing’ ([11212913](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_TEAXIPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Based on this, it makes further adjustments at the start of the current slot ‘i’ as follows:

cs1Size = clamp {(cs1Size * (slotAwareOptimalRatio + patternRatio(i)) / slotAwareOptimalRatio), 1, maxCs1Size}

The parameters to compute cs1Size shall belong to the same OLC instance as cs1Size. These are:

  * slotAwareOptimalRatio is defined in [11212562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_RSkOsPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  * patternRatio is defined in [12645241](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_wjOMNkK0EfCH-cG2YrVgkA).
  * maxCs1Size is the absolute upper limit of the CS1 list size configured by rdMaxNumUeTdDl ([11182022](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_xLl9IPvOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DL scheduler or rdMaxNumUeTdUl ([11182963](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_2mITNvvOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for UL scheduler.



Note: To disable CS1 adjustment based on the patternRatio by setting both rdLoadPatternCorrectionMaxDecrease (described in [12643910](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_PnG-cEIaEfC6a_agjpBoXg)) and rdLoadPatternCorrectionMaxIncrease (described in [12643907](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_9esnkUIZEfC6a_agjpBoXg)) to zero.

---

#### 2.14.2.4.3 Adaptation to Scheduler Budgets

##### 2.14.2.4.3.0-1 Adaptation to Scheduler Budgets DL Scheduler Budget (ID: 13423156)

**2.14.2.4.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13423161`)

Adaptation to Scheduler Budgets Every DL scheduler shall perform the computation specified in this requirement always, regardless of the value of any activation flags.

At the start of DL scheduling, every DL scheduler shall dynamically compute its own available scheduling budget.

In slots where multiple schedulers are executed sequentially on the same core, every DL scheduler shall assume that other schedulers which have already started scheduling in the current slot have not yet completed their scheduling tasks and thus need a share of the remaining CPU processing time in the current slot. Other schedulers which have already started scheduling in the current slot are DL schedulers and might still have to perform FD scheduling or post-scheduling.

Every DL scheduler shall compute its scheduling budget as follows:

  1. Compute the total scheduling time available for all schedulers in the current slot, excluding time spans unavailable for scheduling due to the slot delay and due to the time reservation for message processing. This is totalSchedulingBudgetNs.



totalSchedulingBudgetNs = (slotDurationNs - slotDelayNs) * slotProcessingRatio

  1. Compute its own scheduling budget by taking a proportional share of totalSchedulingBudgetNs.



schedulerBudgetNs(n) = totalSchedulingBudgetNs * slotAwareOptimalRatio(n) / slotProcessingRatio

With:

  * slotDurationNs: The slot duration in nano seconds.
  * slotDelayNs: The slot delay measured in the current slot as per [11213446: Scheduling Phases](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), in nano seconds.
  * slotProcessingRatio: The ratio of the slot duration available for UE scheduling for all schedulers running in the current slot as per [11212528: Slot Processing Ratio (dynamic)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mESvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
  * slotAwareOptimalRatio: The nominal ratio of the slot duration which is available for one scheduler in the current slot as per [11213788: DL/UL Load Balancing](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-unJvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  * n: Index of the DL scheduler computing this formula.

---

##### 2.14.2.4.3.0-2 Adaptation to Scheduler Budgets UL Scheduler Budget (ID: 13423181)

**2.14.2.4.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13423182`)

Adaptation to Scheduler Budgets Every UL scheduler shall perform the computation specified in this requirement always, regardless of the value of any activation flags.

At the start of UL scheduling, every UL scheduler shall dynamically compute its own available scheduling budget.

Every UL scheduler shall distinguish the schedulers which are running in the current slot by means of the scheduler index i = 1...N, where N is the total number of schedulers running in the slot. The schedulers are assumed to run in the order of the their index i. Every UL scheduler shall denote its own index as n.

In slots where multiple schedulers are executed sequentially on the same core (N>1), every UL scheduler n shall assume that other schedulers which have started scheduling before UL scheduler n have already completed their scheduling tasks and thus don't need a share of the remaining CPU processing time any more. Other schedulers which have run before UL scheduler n can be DL or UL schedulers because DL schedulers always run before UL schedulers.

UL scheduler n shall compute its scheduling budget as follows:

  1. Compute the total remaining scheduling time available for all schedulers from index n onwards, including the time which UL scheduler n has already spent in this slot, if any. This is totalRemainingSchedulingBudgetNs(n).



totalRemainingSchedulingBudgetNs(n) = elapsedTimeSinceSlotStartNs(n) + timeTillSlotBoundaryNs(n) – (slotDurationNs-slotDelayNs) * (1 – slotProcessingRatio)

  1. Compute the sum of the nominal processing ratios for all schedulers which have not yet completed their execution in the current slot, i.e. from scheduler n to N.



remainingRatioSum(n) = sum_{i = n...N}_{ slotAwareOptimalRatio(i) }

An equivalent formula for the computation of remainingRatioSum is:

remainingRatioSum(n) = slotProcessingRatio - sum_{i = 1...n-1}_{ slotAwareOptimalRatio(i) }

SW development may chose which formula to use for an efficient implementation.

Note: In slots where multiple schedulers are executed sequentially, it is guaranteed that remainingRatioSum(n) is greater than or equal to slotAwareOptimalRatio(n).

  1. Compute the specific budget for scheduler n by taking a proportional share of totalRemainingSchedulingBudgetNs.



schedulerBudgetNs(n) = totalRemainingSchedulingBudgetNs(n) * slotAwareOptimalRatio(n) / remainingRatioSum(n)

With:

  * elapsedTimeSinceSlotStartNs(n): The time span in nano seconds which has elapsed since the processing start of UL scheduler n.
  * timeTillSlotBoundaryNs(n): The time span in nano seconds which is left in the current slot from the point of view of UL scheduler n.
  * slotDurationNs: The slot duration in nano seconds.
  * slotDelayNs: The slot delay measured in the current slot as per [11213446: Scheduling Phases](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), in nano seconds.
  * slotProcessingRatio: The ratio of the slot duration available for UE scheduling for all schedulers running in the current slot as per [11212528: Slot Processing Ratio (dynamic)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mESvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
  * slotAwareOptimalRatio: The nominal ratio of the slot duration which is available for one scheduler in the current slot as per [11213788: DL/UL Load Balancing](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-unJvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

---

##### 2.14.2.4.3.0-3 Adaptation to Scheduler Budgets Max CS1 Size Correction (Scheduler Budgets) (ID: 13448699)

**2.14.2.4.3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13448700`)

Adaptation to Scheduler Budgets When required in [11212913: Adaptation to Late Slot Processing](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-ogjfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), every scheduler shall adapt the maximum CS1 list size cs1ListMaxSizePreventive determined by preventive load control (see [11212669: Scheduling capacity monitoring](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-nSZPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) to the time constraints in the current slot. Every scheduler shall proceed as follows.

  1. Compute the effective correction time which reflects the scheduler's available scheduling budget (schedulerBudgetNs) and the variation of the time consumption expected for the scheduler in the current slot i (patternCorrectionTimeNs(i)):



effectiveCorrectionTimeNs = schedulerBudgetNs + patternCorrectionTimeNs(i)

  1. Compute the adapted maximum CS1 list size:



adaptedCs1ListSize = clamp{ cs1ListMaxSizePreventive * effectiveCorrectionTimeNs / (slotAwareOptimalRatio * (slotDurationNs - avgSlotDelayNs)), 1, maxNumUeTd }

With:

  * schedulerBudgetNs: Computed in [13423156: DL Scheduler Budget](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_y_iSwhh9EfGFMKAOrP5qqw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) for DL schedulers and in [13423181: UL Scheduler Budget](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_VvwMkxiCEfGFMKAOrP5qqw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) for UL schedulers.
  * patternCorrectionTimeNs: Defined in [12645241: Post-Scheduling Pattern Ratio (dynamic)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_whEQFUK0EfCH-cG2YrVgkA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9). A positive value means that the expected post-scheduling time consumption in the current slot is less than it is on average.
  * slotAwareOptimalRatio: The nominal ratio of the slot duration which is available for one scheduler in the current slot as per [11213788: DL/UL Load Balancing](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-unJvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  * slotDurationNs: The slot duration in nano seconds.
  * avgSlotDelayNs: Average of the slot delay as per [11213602: Exponential Averages](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) in nano seconds.
  * maxNumUeTd: Equal to rdMaxNumUeTdDl ([11182022](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27YYNvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) for DL schedulers and rdMaxNumUeTdUL ([11182963](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27fs-fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) for UL schedulers.

---

##### 2.14.2.4.3.0-4 Adaptation to Scheduler Budgets Reduction Factor due to Slot Delay (ID: 13471771)

**2.14.2.4.3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13471772`)

Adaptation to Scheduler Budgets When required in [11212913: Adaptation to Late Slot Processing](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-ogjfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), every scheduler shall determine the reduction of the maximum CS1 list size which can be attributed to the slot delay in the current slot. Every scheduler shall proceed as follows.

  1. Compute the adapted maximum CS1 list size considering only the slot delay:



adaptedCs1ListSizeDueToSlotDelay = clamp{ cs1ListMaxSizePreventive * (slotDurationNs - slotDelayNs) / (slotDurationNs - avgSlotDelayNs), 1, maxNumUeTd }

  1. Determine the factor by which the maximum CS1 list size has been reduced due to the slot delay:



correctiveCs1ListMaxSizeReductionFactorDueToSlotDelay = floor{ adaptedCs1ListSizeDueToSlotDelay } / floor { cs1ListMaxSizePreventive } 

With:

  * cs1ListMaxSizePreventive: Maximum CS1 list size from [11212613: Preventive Load Control](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrWfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
  * slotDurationNs: The slot duration in nano seconds.
  * slotDelayNs: The slot delay measured in the current slot as per [11213446: Scheduling Phases](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), in nano seconds.
  * avgSlotDelayNs: Average of the slot delay as per [11213602: Exponential Averages](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) in nano seconds.
  * maxNumUeTd: Equal to rdMaxNumUeTdDl ([11182022](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27YYNvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) for DL schedulers and rdMaxNumUeTdUL ([11182963](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27fs-fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) for UL schedulers.

---

#### 2.14.2.4.4 FIFO Message Queue Processing

##### 2.14.2.4.4.0-1 FIFO Message Queue Processing Prio 1 FIFO Queue (ID: 11213050)

**2.14.2.4.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11213055`)

FIFO Message Queue Processing When overload is triggered by the prio 1 FIFO queue (5G_L2_9349_replaced([11212335](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-k2JfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) at the end of the slot, 5G-L2-PS implements a corrective control by reducing the CS1 list size to only one UE to be scheduled, as long as it is in overload state.

This mechanism is available for DL schedulers.

This mechanism is not slot-aware. When the overload state defined in 5G_L2_1829_replaced([11212441](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-ldOvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is detected, 5G-L2-PS shall apply the CS1 list size reduction immediately in all subsequent slots. When the condition to switch back from the overload state to normal operation in 5G_L2_1829_replaced([11212441](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-ldOvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is met, 5G-L2-PS shall stop the CS1 list size reduction immediately in all subsequent slots.

---

##### 2.14.2.4.4.0-2 FIFO Message Queue Processing Prio 2 FIFO Queue (ID: 11213061)

**2.14.2.4.4.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11213075`)

FIFO Message Queue Processing When overload is triggered by the [Before CB010309-A] FIFO queues [CB010309-A] prio 2 FIFO queue [End CB010309-A] check at the end of the slot, 5G-L2-PS implements a corrective control by reducing the CS1 list size to only one UE to be scheduled, as long as it is in overload state.

This mechanism is available for DL schedulers.

This mechanism is not slot-aware. When the overload state defined in 5G_L2_1829_replaced([11212441](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-ldOvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is detected, 5G-L2-PS shall apply the CS1 list size reduction immediatedly in all subsequent slots. When the condition to switch back from the overload state to normal operation in 5G_L2_1829_replaced([11212441](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-ldOvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is met, 5G-L2-PS shall stop the CS1 list size reduction immediatedly in all subsequent slots.

---

##### 2.14.2.4.4.0-3 FIFO Message Queue Processing Prio 3 FIFO Queue (ID: 11213082)

**2.14.2.4.4.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11213089`)

FIFO Message Queue Processing When overload is triggered by the prio 3 FIFO queue check at the end of the slot, 5G-L2-PS implements a corrective control by reducing the CS1 list size to only one UE to be scheduled, as long as it is in overload state.

This mechanism is available for DL schedulers.

This mechanism is not slot-aware. When the overload state defined in 5G_L2_1829_replaced([11212441](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-ldOvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is detected, 5G-L2-PS shall apply the CS1 list size reduction immediatedly in all subsequent slots. When the condition to switch back from the overload state to normal operation in 5G_L2_1829_replaced([11212441](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-ldOvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is met, 5G-L2-PS shall stop the CS1 list size reduction immediatedly in all subsequent slots.
