### 2.14.2.5 List Size Reductions

#### 2.14.2.5.0-1 List Size Reductions Dynamic Reduction Factor - Based on Preventive OLC (ID: 11213322)

**2.14.2.5.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12706249`)

List Size Reductions [CB014680-B] If the first LSB of rdActCb014680OlcImprovement ([12636258](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_VQda4UAdEfCal_QUJn4xrg)) is set to zero, then [End CB014680-B]5G-L2-PS shall compute the reduction factor for list size reductions as:

dynamicCsReductionFactorPreventive = max{ 0.1, min{ 0.9, csReductionFactorOlc + 0.33 } - [Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size [CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive [End CNI-136895-A] / 100 }

With:

  * csReductionFactorOlc is received in PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and modified in 5G_L2_19958_replaced([11141304](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23n5mPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * [Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size [CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive [End CNI-136895-A] is the maximum CS1 list size proposed by preventive OLC (5G_L2_1841_replaced([11212749](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-n5cPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * The constant value of 0.33 has been defined as the greatest value in the range of maxNumPdschAllocationPerSlot or maxNumPuschAllocationPerSlot (received in PsCell_CellSetupReq, 5G_L2_IF_128_replaced([10969448](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Ucdbvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), which is 16, divided by the absolute upper limit of the CS1 list size given by the default value of rdMaxNumUeTdDl (5G_L2_3697_replaced([11182022](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27YYNvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or rdMaxNumUeTdUl (5G_L2_3702_replaced([11182963](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27fs-fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), which is 50.

---

#### 2.14.2.5.0-2 List Size Reductions Dynamic Reduction Factor - Based on Corrective OLC (ID: 11213331)

**2.14.2.5.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `12636285`)

List Size Reductions [CB014680-B] If the first LSB of rdActCb014680OlcImprovement ([12636258](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_VQda4UAdEfCal_QUJn4xrg)) is set to zero, then [End CB014680-B]5G-L2-PS shall compute the reduction factor for list size reductions as:

dynamicCsReductionFactor = max{ 0.1, min{ 0.9, csReductionFactorOlc + 0.33 } - cs1Size(n) / 100 }

With:

  * csReductionFactorOlc is received in PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and modified in 5G_L2_19958_replaced([11141304](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23n5mPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * cs1Size(n) is the maximum CS1 list size proposed by corrective OLC in the current slot n (5G_L2_1853_replaced([11212970](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-pHlfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * The constant value of 0.33 has been defined as the greatest value in the range of maxNumPdschAllocationPerSlot or maxNumPuschAllocationPerSlot (received in PsCell_CellSetupReq, 5G_L2_IF_128_replaced([10969448](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Ucdbvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), which is 16, divided by the absolute upper limit of the CS1 list size given by the default value of rdMaxNumUeTdDl (5G_L2_3697_replaced([11182022](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27YYNvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or rdMaxNumUeTdUl (5G_L2_3702_replaced([11182963](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27fs-fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), which is 50.

---

#### 2.14.2.5.0-3 List Size Reductions CS1 to FDM Factor (ID: 12737461)

**2.14.2.5.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12737462`)

List Size Reductions If the first LSB of rdActCb014680OlcImprovement ([12636258](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_VQda4UAdEfCal_QUJn4xrg)) is set to 1 AND actCsReductionFactorOlc is enabled, 5G-L2-PS shall compute the CS1 to FDM reduction factor for FDM list size reductions as:

rrmFdmToCs1FactorOlc = min{(0.5 + csReductionFactorOlc) * (rrmFdmUeMaxOlc/ rdCs1Max), 1}

With:

  * csReductionFactorOlc is received in PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq ([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and modified in ([11141304](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23n5mPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * actCsReductionFactorOlc is received in PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq ([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * rrmFdmUeMaxOlc is defined in [12584429](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wo7J4DUyEfCKaNlcHOQWmg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wo7J4DUyEfCKaNlcHOQWmg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").
  * rdCs1Max is the maximum CS1 list size given by the r&d param rdMaxNumUeTdDl (for DL scheduler defined in [11182022](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27YYNvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and rdMaxNumUeTdUl (for UL scheduler defined in [11182963](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27fs-fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * The constant value of 0.5 has been defined as the greatest value in the range of rrmFdmMax, divided by the absolute upper limit of the CS1 list size given by the rdCs1Max defined above.

---

#### 2.14.2.5.0-4 List Size Reductions FDM to CS2 Factor (ID: 12737466)

**2.14.2.5.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12737467`)

List Size Reductions If the first LSB of rdActCb014680OlcImprovement ([12636258](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_VQda4UAdEfCal_QUJn4xrg)) is set to 1 AND actCsReductionFactorOlc is enabled, 5G-L2-PS shall compute the FDM to CS2 factor for CS2 list max size as:

rrmCs2ToFdmFactorOlc = min{(0.5 + csReductionFactorOlc) * (rrmFdmUeMaxOlc/rrmCs2Max), 1} 

With:

  * csReductionFactorOlc is received in PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq ([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and modified in ([11141304](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23n5mPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * actCsReductionFactorOlc is received in PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq ([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * rrmFdmUeMaxOlc and rrmCs2Max is defined in [12584429](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wo7J4DUyEfCKaNlcHOQWmg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wo7J4DUyEfCKaNlcHOQWmg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").

---

#### 2.14.2.5.0-5 List Size Reductions CS2 List Reduction in FR1 (ID: 11213344)

**2.14.2.5.0-5.0-5**  (ID: `12636286`)

List Size Reductions This requirement applies to FR1 only.

IF actCsReductionFactorOlc = FALSE THEN 5G-L2-PS shall proceed as follows.

If scheduling fairness consideration functionality is activated for DL: (actFdmScheduling = TRUE and pucchModeSelect = longPucch) and/or for UL: (actFdmScheduling = TRUE and pucchModeSelect = longPucch and actSchedFairnessUlOlc = TRUE) (see 5G_UP_ALG_18144_replaced([11215995](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxWtNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), corresponding L2PS DL and/or L2PS UL scheduler shall limit the cs2List sorted wrt their priorities (maxCs2Size) according to the CS1 size and target FDM Ues per slot (rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc, see 5G_L2_7048_replaced([11213384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj2vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as below

maxCs2Size = max{ maxCs2SizeBasedOnCs1, maxCs2SizeBasedOnTargetFd, the number of initial transmission Msg3 }

When actSchedFairnessUlOlc = TRUE:

maxCs2SizeBasedOnCs1 = cs2ToCs1Ratio * proposedMaxCs1SizeOlc

Else:

For L2PS DL Scheduler: maxCs2SizeBasedOnCs1 = cs2ToCs1Ratio * cs1Size

For L2PS UL Scheduler: No CS2 list reduction applied.

maxCs2SizeBasedOnTargetFd = max{ minAdditionalCs2Entries + rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc, cs2FdUesFactor * rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc }

If the scheduling fairness functionality is not activated 5G-L2-PS shall set:

IF actSchedFairnessUlOlc = TRUE:

maxCs2Size = proposedMaxCs1SizeOlc

ELSE:

maxCs2Size = cs1Size

Where,

For L2PS DL scheduler

  * minAdditionalCs2Entries = 2
  * cs2FdUesFactor = 2
  * cs2ToCs1Ratio = 0.5
  * cs1Size is the actual number of Ues in the cs1 list in the given slot
  * proposedMaxCs1SizeOlc is the resultant maximum cs1List size proposed from overload control(see 5G_L2_1845_replaced([11212901](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-ogi_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in DL for the slot. Please note that, in case of no overload, proposedMaxCs1SizeOlc will be equal to max allowed entries in candidate set 1 (CS1) even though actual number of UEs with data in the slot is less.
  * rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc is the target FD Ues per slot( see 5G_L2_7048_replaced([11213384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj2vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * pucchModeSelect is received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).



For L2PS UL scheduler

  * minAdditionalCs2Entries = rdUlMinAdditionalCs2Entries(see 5G_L2_11600_replaced([11190490](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28XPpPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * cs2FdUesFactor = rdUlCs2FdUesFactor(see 5G_L2_11601_replaced([11190501](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28XPpvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * cs2ToCs1Ratio = rdUlCs2ToCs1Ratio(see 5G_L2_11602_replaced([11190514](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28XPqPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * proposedMaxCs1SizeOlc is the resultant maximum cs1List size proposed from overload control(see 5G_L2_1845_replaced([11212901](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-ogi_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in UL for the slot. Please note that, in case of no overload, proposedMaxCs1SizeOlc will be equal to max allowed entries in candidate set 1 (CS1) even though actual number of UEs with data in the slot is less.
  * rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc is the target FD Ues per slot( see 5G_L2_7048_replaced([11213384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj2vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * pucchModeSelect is received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).



IF actCsReductionFactorOlc = TRUE THEN 5G-L2-PS shall proceed as follows.

5G-L2-PS shall activate the scheduling fairness consideration functionality when all of the following conditions are met:

  * actFdmScheduling = TRUE
  * In UL only: actSchedFairnessUlOlc = TRUE
  * pucchModeSelect = longPucch
  * actCsReductionFactorOlc **= TRUE**



If the scheduling fairness functionality is activated, 5G-L2-PS shall limit the maximum CS2 list size (maxCs2Size) according to the maximum CS1 list size (cs1Size(n)) and the maximum number of FDM UEs (rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc) as follows:

**[CB014680-B] IF the first LSB of rdActCb014680OlcImprovement is set to zero:**[End CB014680-B]****

maxCs2Size = min{ cs1Size(n), floor{ max{ (1 - dynamicCsReductionFactor ) * cs1Size(n) , rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc + 2, the number of initial transmission Msg3 } } }

[CB014680-B] IF the first LSB of rdActCb014680OlcImprovement is set to enabled:

maxCs2Size = min{ cs1Size(n), max{ min{ cs1Size(n) - 1, rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlcSlotLimitNotApplied /rrmCs2toFdmFactorOlc}, rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlcSlotLimitNotApplied + rdMinCs2ToFdmUesRedundancy} }

**[End CB014680-B]**

If the scheduling fairness functionality is not activated, 5G-L2-PS shall set:

maxCs2Size = cs1Size(n)

With:

  * actFdmScheduling is received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_128_replaced([10969448](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Ucdbvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * actSchedFairnessUlOlc is received in the PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * pucchModeSelect is received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * dynamicCsReductionFactor is computed in 5G_L2_21430_replaced([11213331](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj0fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * actCsReductionFactorOlc is received in PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * cs1Size(n) is the maximum CS1 list size proposed by corrective OLC in the current slot n (5G_L2_1853_replaced([11212970](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-pHlfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc is computed in 5G_L2_7048_replaced([11213384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj2vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * [CB014680-B]rdMinCs2ToFdmUesRedundancy is defined in [12584430](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0MwLEDU0EfCKaNlcHOQWmg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).
  * rrmCs2toFdmFactorOlc is defined in [12737466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufkUA3gKEfCdZt6bzaG3fw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufkUA3gKEfCdZt6bzaG3fw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").
  * rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlcSlotLimitNotApplied is computed in [11213384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj2vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). [End CB014680-B]

---

#### 2.14.2.5.0-6 List Size Reductions CS2 List Reduction in FR2 (ID: 11213374)

**2.14.2.5.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11213379`)

List Size Reductions In FR2, in case of preventive/corrective overload conditions reached as per 5G_UP_ALG_19717_replaced([11216218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxX7W_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the CS2 list shall be reduced before the TD metric priorization to the cs2Size = max(2, floor(cs1Size * rdFr2Cs1ToCs2ReductionRatio))

where,

  * rdFr2Cs1ToCs2ReductionRatio is the CS2 list size reduction ratio (see 5G_L2_19871_replaced([11191087](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28bhEvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

#### 2.14.2.5.0-7 List Size Reductions Reduction of the maximum Number of FDM UEs per Slot (ID: 11213384)

**2.14.2.5.0-7.0-4**  (ID: `12636308`)

List Size Reductions IF actCsReductionFactorOlc = FALSE THEN 5G-L2-PS shall proceed as follows.

If scheduling fairness consideration functionality is activated for DL: (actFdmScheduling = TRUE and pucchModeSelect = longPucch) and/or for UL: (FDM enabled actFdmScheduling = TRUE and pucchModeSelect = longPucch and actSchedFairnessUlOlc = TRUE) (see 5G_UP_ALG_18144_replaced([11215995](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxWtNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), corresponding L2PS DL and/or L2PS UL scheduler shall maintain a fair ratio between the cs1List size and the target number of FD Ues in any given slot. As a result, if cs1List size is reduced due to overload control, max number of FDM Ues allowed in the slot shall also be reduced accordingly.

If scheduling fairness consideration functionality is activated, for each slot, corresponding UL/DL scheduler shall calculate target number of FD Ues per slot (rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc) as:

rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc = max{ 1, min(reductionFactor * proposedMaxCs1SizeOlc, rrmMaxNumUesFdm) }

reductionFactor = max{ maxNumPxschAllocationPerSlot /(maxNumUeTd - noReductionWindowSize), minReductionFactor }

If scheduling fairness functionality is not activated 5G-L2-PS shall set:

IF actSchedFairnessUlOlc = TRUE:

rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc = max{ 1, min(reductionFactor * proposedMaxCs1SizeOlc, 50) }

reductionFactor = max{ 50 /(maxNumUeTd - noReductionWindowSize), minReductionFactor }

ELSE:

rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc = 50

Where,

For L2PS DL scheduler:

  * proposedMaxCs1SizeOlc is the resultant maximum cs1List size proposed from overload control for the slot (see 5G_L2_1845_replaced([11212901](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-ogi_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * minReductionFactor = 0.25
  * noReductionWindowSize = 2
  * maxNumUeTd refers to rdMaxNumUeTdDl(5G_L2_3697_replaced([11182022](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27YYNvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), which defines the maximum number of UEs that can be considered for candidate set 1 (CS1)
  * maxNumPxschAllocationPerSlot refers to maxNumPdschAllocationPerSlot, the maximum number of FDM Users to be FDMed in DL (see 5G_L2_IF_128_replaced([10969448](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Ucdbvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * rrmMaxNumUesFdm refers to rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl which is the resultant value from 5G_UP_ALG_10610_replaced([11179079](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku3Z6_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * pucchModeSelect is received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).



For L2PS UL scheduler:

  * proposedMaxCs1SizeOlc is the resultant maximum cs1List size proposed from overload control for the slot (see 5G_L2_1845_replaced([11212901](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-ogi_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * minReductionFactor = rdUlMinReductionFactor (see 5G_L2_11603_replaced([11190526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28XPqvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * noReductionWindowSize = rdUlNoReductionWindowSize (see 5G_L2_11604_replaced([11190536](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28XPrPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * maxNumUeTd refers to rdMaxNumUeTdUl(5G_L2_3702_replaced([11182963](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27fs-fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), which defines the maximum number of UEs that can be considered for candidate set 1 (CS1)
  * maxNumPxschAllocationPerSlot refers to maxNumPuschAllocationPerSlot, the maximum number of FDM Users to be FDMed in UL (see 5G_L2_IF_128_replaced([10969448](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Ucdbvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * rrmMaxNumUesFdm refers to rrmMaxNumUesFdmUl which is the resultant value from 5G_UP_ALG_10654_replaced([11199273](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwMPmfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * pucchModeSelect is received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).



The resultant rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc shall be used as input for FDM/SDM scheduling.

The UL scheduler shall apply rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc for the computation of nAllocations_usable in UL VoNR (5G_UP_ALG_5024_replaced([11201259](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwUyefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and UL GBR (5G_UP_ALG_8174_replaced([11201280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwUyffvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) time domain load monitoring report.

Note: proposedMaxCs1SizeOlc is not the actual cs1Size in the slot but the maximum size proposed from OLC. In case of no overload, proposedMaxCs1SizeOlc will be rdMaxNumUeTd even though actual number of UEs with data in the slot is less. So, in case of no overload, there will be no reduction of rrmMaxNumUesFdm from load control.

IF actCsReductionFactorOlc = TRUE THEN 5G-L2-PS shall proceed as follows.

5G-L2-PS shall activate the scheduling fairness consideration functionality when all of the following conditions are met:

  * actFdmScheduling = TRUE
  * In UL only: actSchedFairnessUlOlc = TRUE
  * pucchModeSelect = longPucch



If the scheduling fairness functionality is activated, 5G-L2-PS shall maintain a fair ratio between the maximum CS1 list size (cs1Size(n)) and the maximum number of FDM UEs (rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc) in any given slot. As a result, if the maximum CS1 list size is reduced due to overload, the maximum number of FDM UEs allowed in the slot shall be reduced accordingly. 5G-L2-PS shall calculate the maximum number of FDM UEs per slot as follows:

**[CB014680-B] IF the first LSB of rdActCb014680OlcImprovement is disabled:**[End CB014680-B]****

rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc = min{ max{ 1, floor{dynamicCsReductionFactor * cs1Size(n)} }, rrmMaxNumUesFdm } 

[CB014680-B]IF the first LSB of rdActCb014680OlcImprovement is set to enabled:

IF (cs1Size(n) * rrmFdmToCs1FactorOlc >= rrmFdmToCs1SlopeSwitchingPoint)

rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlcSlotLimitNotApplied = max{ (rrmFdmToCs1FactorOlc * cs1Size(n)), 1} 

ELSE

rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlcSlotLimitNotApplied = min{ rrmFdmToCs1SlopeSwitchingPoint, min{rrmFdmToCs1FactorOlc + csReductionFactorOlc - 0.1, 1 } * cs1Size(n)}

rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlcSlotLimitNotApplied = max{ rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlcSlotLimitNotApplied, 1}

IF the cs1Size(n) is from corrective OLC, then:

rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc = min{ rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlcSlotLimitNotApplied, rrmMaxNumUesFdm }

ELSE

rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc = rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlcSlotLimitNotApplied

[End CB014680-B]

If the scheduling fairness functionality is not activated, 5G-L2-PS shall set:

rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc = rrmMaxNumUesFdm

5G-L2-PS shall apply rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc as the upper limit for the number of scheduled UEs in FDM/SDM scheduling and for the computation of nAllocations_usable in 5G_UP_ALG_28379_replaced([11201301](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwVZgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (Time Domain Load Monitoring for UL GBR RAC) and for the computation of nAllocations_available_total(P) in 5G_UP_ALG_28365_replaced([11201327](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwVZh_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (Deriving Time Domain Capacity for UL GBR RAC).

With:

  * actFdmScheduling is received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_128_replaced([10969448](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Ucdbvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * actSchedFairnessUlOlc is received in the PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * pucchModeSelect is received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * dynamicCsReductionFactor is computed in 5G_L2_21430_replaced([11213331](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj0fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * actCsReductionFactorOlc is received in PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * cs1Size(n) is the maximum CS1 list size proposed by corrective OLC in the current slot n (see 5G_L2_1853_replaced([11212970](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-pHlfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * rrmMaxNumUesFdm is equal to rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl (5G_UP_ALG_10610_replaced([11179079](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku3Z6_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the DL and equal to rrmMaxNumUesFdmUl (5G_UP_ALG_10654_replaced([11199273](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwMPmfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the UL.
  * [CB014680-B] csReductionFactorOlc is received in PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and modified in PsCell_CellGroupReconfigReq ([11141304](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23n5mPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * rrmFdmToCs1FactorOlc is defined in [12737461](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_XLfwlHgKEfCdZt6bzaG3fw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_XLfwlHgKEfCdZt6bzaG3fw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").
  * rrmFdmToCs1SlopeSwitchingPoint is the slope defined in [11216019: Scheduling Fairness Consideration in High load Detection - Algorithm](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_htBO8PvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ).[End CB014680-B]

---

### 2.14.2.6 UE Skipping

#### 2.14.2.6.0-1 UE Skipping FD-UE Skipping (ID: 11213118)

**2.14.2.6.0-1.0-11**  (ID: `11213187`)

UE Skipping As an emergency mechanism, L2-PS UL and DL schedulers shall skip the scheduling of FD-UEs if there is not enough time budget available for the scheduling of all FD-UEs.

IF (actFdmUeSkippingOlc = TRUE) AND (actFdmScheduling = TRUE): 5G-L2-PS shall not perform FD-UE skipping.

[CB009363-OO] ELSE IF (actFdmUeSkippingOlc = FALSE) AND (rdMaxNumOfFdUes > 0): 5G-L2-PS shall perform FD-UE skipping without checking time budget and use rdMaxNumOfFdUes as the maximum number of FD UEs scheduled by the FD scheduler in the slot. [End CB009363-OO]

ELSE: 5G-L2-PS shall perform FD-UE skipping by executing step 1 (5G_L2_14796_replaced([11213195](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-qVwPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), step 2 (5G_L2_14797_replaced([11213228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-qVxfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and step 3 (5G_L2_14798_replaced([11213262](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-q8xPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the given order.

Note: In FR2, only one UE is scheduled per carrier. So, if one FD-UE is being skipped, it eventually means the whole carrier is skipped. In FR1, when FDM is enabled, FD-UE skipping allows a few UEs within the carrier to be skipped.

With:

  * actFdmUeSkippingOlc is received in the PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * actFdmScheduling is received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_61_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * rdMaxNumOfFdUes is defnined in 5G_L2_15310_replaced([11190886](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Zr7PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.14.2.6.0-2 UE Skipping FD-UE Skipping - Step 1 (Available Time) (ID: 11213195)

**2.14.2.6.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11213224`)

UE Skipping 5G-L2-PS shall perform this requirement only if FD-UE skipping is active as per 5G_L2_1859_replaced([11213118](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-purfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

After TD scheduling, UL and DL schedulers shall calculate the time buget available for the scheduler as follows.

  * estimatedRemainingSchedTime = (slotDuration - slotDelay) * availableSlotRatio - elapsedTimeSinceSlotStart



IF actSmartRoundInFdUeSkipping = TRUE:

availableSlotRatio = slotAwareOptimalRatio

ELSE:

IF slotDelay > avgSlotDelay:

availableSlotRatio = slotProcessingRatioCellShare,

where slotProcessingRatioCellShare is the sum of slotAwareOptimalRatio of all the schedulers of the given cell in the given core.

Note: In the current deployment the value of slotProcessingRatioCellShare would match to the slotAwareOptimalRatio as schedulers of different cells are deployed per core.

In the second iteration (see 5G_L2_14798_replaced([11213262](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-q8xPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) only: availableSlotRatio += rdSlotProcessingRatioExtension

ELSE

availableSlotRatio = slotAwareOptimalRatio

In the second iteration (see 5G_L2_14798_replaced([11213262](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-q8xPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) only: availableSlotRatio += rdSlotProcessingRatioExtension

Note: Even if slotDelay <= avgSlotDelay, estimatedRemainingSchedTime may exceed the schedulers' share of the target duration ratio (5G_L2_5479_replaced([11212394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-ldMfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if another scheduler has run before in the same slot on the same core and has consumed more time than expected.

  * actualRemainingSchedTime = timeTillSlotBoundary - (1 - correctedSlotProcessingRatio) * slotDuration



IF actSmartRoundInFdUeSkipping = TRUE:

correctedSlotProcessingRatio = slotProcessingRatio

ELSE:

IF slotDelay > avgSlotDelay:

correctedSlotProcessingRatio = 1

ELSE:

correctedSlotProcessingRatio = slotProcessingRatio

In the second iteration (see 5G_L2_14798_replaced([11213262](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-q8xPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) only: correctedSlotProcessingRatio += rdSlotProcessingRatioExtension

  * Available time for FD scheduling:



IF (actLastSchedulerOlcEnh = FALSE) AND (actSmartRoundInFdUeSkipping = FALSE):

In DL: availableTimeForFd = min{ estimatedRemainingSchedTime, actualRemainingSchedTime } - avgResidualTdSchedTimeBeforeFd - avgPostSchedTime

If the conditions for three (3) cores deployment for FD parallelization in DL are met (refer to 5G_L2_4595_replaced([11140997](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23mEavvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), availableTimeForFd shall be computed for each of the FD cores independently since avgResidualTdSchedTimeBeforeFd is measured for each of the FD cores independently.

In UL: availableTimeForFd = min{ estimatedRemainingSchedTime, actualRemainingSchedTime } - avgPostSchedTime

ELSE:

In DL: availableTimeForFdUe = min{ estimatedRemainingSchedTime, actualRemainingSchedTime } - avgResidualTdSchedTimeBeforeFd - avgPostSchedTime - avgFdCommonTime

If the conditions for three (3) cores deployment for FD parallelization in DL are met (refer to 5G_L2_4595_replaced([11140997](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23mEavvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), availableTimeForFdUe shall be computed for each of the FD cores independently since avgResidualTdSchedTimeBeforeFd is measured for each of the FD cores independently.

In UL: availableTimeForFdUe = min{ estimatedRemainingSchedTime, actualRemainingSchedTime } - avgPostSchedTime - avgFdCommonTime

The DL scheduler (or the UL scheduler) shall fill the trace entry allowedRemainingSchedTime in the trace event dlLoadControlData (5G_L2_6440_replaced([11203804](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_299yIvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) (or ulLoadControlData, 5G_L2_6441_replaced([11203655](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_299LEPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with the value of min{ estimatedRemainingSchedTime, actualRemainingSchedTime } from the last iteration (see 5G_L2_14798_replaced([11213262](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-q8xPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

With:

  * slotDelay is defined in 5G_L2_1863_replaced([11213446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * avgSlotDelay, avgResidualTdSchedTimeBeforeFd, avgPostSchedTime and avgFdCommonTime are defined in 5G_L2_1870_replaced([11213602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * slotAwareOptimalRatio is defined in 5G_L2_6333_replaced([11212562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * rdSlotProcessingRatioExtension is defined in 5G_L2_10983_replaced([11190090](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28UMWvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * timeTillSlotBoundary: The time which is left in the current slot.
  * slotProcessingRatio is defined in 5G_L2_15692_replaced([11212528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mESvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * elapsedTimeSinceSlotStart: On the DL scheduler (or UL scheduler) it is the time which has elapsed since the start of DL pre-scheduling (or UL pre-scheduling respectively).
  * actLastSchedulerOlcEnh is received in the PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq (see 5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * actSmartRoundInFdUeSkipping is received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * For actTwoCoresL2DeploymentFddFr1 see 5G_L2_16485_replaced([11141119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23mrf_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * slotDuration is the processing time Budget for a slot and depends on the numerology (FR1 FDD 1000us, FR1 TDD 500us, FR2 TDD 125us).



In FR1 TDD, when actFlexibleBiSlotDurationMode is set to "partial" [CB013305-BC] or "full" [End CB013305-BC] and the 750us timing pattern (as defined in 5G_L2_22818_replaced([11157164](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25EEEfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is activated, the biSlot duration is extented by 250us, resulting in a total processing budget of 750us.

Note :

In DL: avgPreAndTdTime, avgResidualTdSchedTimeBeforeFd, avgFdUeTime, avgFdCommonTime are maintained for each of the FD cores independently based on the fdSchedulerIndex (refer to 5G_L2_4595_replaced([11140997](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23mEavvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for defintion), when the conditions for three (3) cores deployment for FD parallelization in DL are met (refer to 5G_L2_4595_replaced([11140997](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23mEavvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and one of the FD scheduling is running on DL core.

---

#### 2.14.2.6.0-3 UE Skipping FD-UE Skipping - Step 2 (Number of UEs) (ID: 11213228)

**2.14.2.6.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11213256`)

UE Skipping 5G-L2-PS shall perform this requirement only if FD-UE skipping is active as per 5G_L2_1859_replaced([11213118](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-purfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Based on the time budget calculated in step 1 (5G_L2_14796_replaced([11213195](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-qVwPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-PS shall compute the maximum number of FD UEs as follows.

IF actSmartRoundInFdUeSkipping = TRUE: 

With FD parallelization, the number of FD UEs determined here is valid per FD core.

In DL, 5G-L2-PS shall assume that avgFdFirstUeTime has the value of 0.

In UL, 5G-L2-PS shall assume that avgFdFirstUeTime has the value measured as per 5G_L2_1870_replaced([11213602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Both in DL and in UL, 5G-L2-PS shall execute the following algorithm.

IF (avgFdFirstUeTime = 0) AND (avgFdUeTime = 0):

5G-L2-PS shall not skip any FD-UEs and shall exit step 2.

Note: avgFdFirstUeTime and avgFdUeTime can be zero after start-up or measurement reset (see 5G_L2_1874_replaced([11213693](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAFPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). UEs shall not be skipped but scheduled to ensure that avgFdFirstUeTime (UL only) and avgFdUeTime will be filled with non-zero values at the end of the slot.

ELSE:

IF (avgFdFirstUeTime = 0):

tempFdFirstUeTime = avgFdUeTime

ELSE:

tempFdFirstUeTime = avgFdFirstUeTime

5G-L2-PS shall determine the non-rounded number of FD-UEs as:

IF availableTimeForFdUe <= tempFdFirstUeTime:

maxNumFdUesNonRounded = max{ 0, availableTimeForFdUe / tempFdFirstUeTime }

ELSE:

IF (avgFdUeTime > 0):

maxNumFdUesNonRounded = max{ 0, 1 + (availableTimeForFdUe - tempFdFirstUeTime) / avgFdUeTime }

ELSE:

maxNumFdUesNonRounded = 2

Note: This branch is to avoid division by zero when avgFdUeTime = 0. Two UEs will be scheduled to ensure that avgFdUeTime will be filled with a non-zero value at the end of the slot. This branch can't be reached in the DL.

IF all of the following conditions are met

  * In DL: tempFdFirstUeTime + max{ 0, ceil{ maxNumFdUesNonRounded } - 1 } * avgFdUeTime - availableTimeForFdUe <= rdSlotRatioExtensionForSmartRoundingDl * slotDuration * shareRatio,
  * In UL: tempFdFirstUeTime + max{ 0, ceil{ maxNumFdUesNonRounded } - 1 } * avgFdUeTime - availableTimeForFdUe <= rdSlotRatioExtensionForSmartRoundingUl * slotDuration * shareRatio,



where shareRatio is the portion of the target duration ratio (see 5G_L2_5479_replaced([11212394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-ldMfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which one DL scheduler or one UL scheduler has available for scheduling. The shareRatio is a real number in the range of [0...1]. The sum of all shareRatio values of all schedulers running on the same core and in the same slot shall be equal to 1.

THEN: 5G-L2-PS shall round up the number of UEs as:

maxNumFdUes = max{ 0, ceil{ maxNumFdUesNonRounded } }

ELSE: 5G-L2-PS shall round down the number of UEs as:

maxNumFdUes = max{ 0, floor{ maxNumFdUesNonRounded } }

ELSE:

IF actLastSchedulerOlcEnh = FALSE:

  * In DL:



IF avgFdUeTime = 0: 5G-L2-PS shall not skip any FD-UEs.   
ELSE:

IF (scs = 120) AND (slotDelay <= avgSlotDelay): maxNumFdUes = max{ 0, round{ (availableTimeForFd - avgFdCommonTime)/avgFdUeTime } }

ELSE: maxNumFdUes = max{ 0, floor{ (availableTimeForFd - avgFdCommonTime)/avgFdUeTime } }

  * In UL:



IF (avgFdFirstUeTime = 0) AND (avgFdUeTime = 0): 5G-L2-PS shall not skip any FD-UEs. 

ELSE:   
IF (availableTimeForFd < avgFdFirstUeTime) OR (avgFdFirstUeTime = 0): maxNumFdUes = 0 ELSE: maxNumFdUes = 1  
IF avgFdUeTime = 0: maxNumFdUes = 1 ELSE: maxNumFdUes += max{ 0, floor{ (availableTimeForFd - avgFdFirstUeTime - avgFdCommonTime)/avgFdUeTime } }

ELSE:

  * In DL:



IF avgFdUeTime = 0: 5G-L2-PS shall not skip any FD-UEs.   
ELSE:

IF (scs = 120) AND (slotDelay <= avgSlotDelay): maxNumFdUes = max{ 0, round{ availableTimeForFdUe / avgFdUeTime } }

ELSE: maxNumFdUes = max{ 0, floor{ availableTimeForFdUe / avgFdUeTime } }

  * In UL:



IF (avgFdFirstUeTime = 0) AND (avgFdUeTime = 0): 5G-L2-PS shall not skip any FD-UEs. 

ELSE:   
IF (availableTimeForFdUe < avgFdFirstUeTime) OR (avgFdFirstUeTime = 0): maxNumFdUes = 0 ELSE: maxNumFdUes = 1  
IF avgFdUeTime = 0: maxNumFdUes = 1 ELSE: maxNumFdUes += max{ 0, floor{ (availableTimeForFdUe - avgFdFirstUeTime)/avgFdUeTime } }

Note :

In DL: maxNumFdUesNonRounded, maxNumFdUes are computed for each of the FD cores based on the fdSchedulerIndex (refer to 5G_L2_4595_replaced([11140997](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23mEavvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for defintion), when the conditions for three (3) cores deployment for FD parallelization in DL are met (refer to 5G_L2_4595_replaced([11140997](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23mEavvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and if rdActFr2EnhParallelDlFdFor8CC is set to 2 as defined in 5G_L2_14282_replaced([11181667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27VU7vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

With:

  * actLastSchedulerOlcEnh is received in the PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq (see 5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * avgSlotDelay, avgFdUeTime, avgFdFirstUeTime and avgFdCommonTime are defined in 5G_L2_1870_replaced([11213602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * slotDelay is defined in 5G_L2_1863_replaced([11213446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * scs is received in the PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * availableTimeForFd and availableTimeForFdUe are computed in step 1 (5G_L2_14796_replaced([11213195](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-qVwPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * actSmartRoundInFdUeSkipping is received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * In DL: rdSlotRatioExtensionForSmartRoundingDl is defined in 5G_L2_20063_replaced([11190647](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28YdwPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * In UL: rdSlotRatioExtensionForSmartRoundingUl is defined in 5G_L2_20061_replaced([11190660](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28YdwvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * slotDuration is the processing time Budget for a slot and depends on the numerology (FR1 FDD 1000us, FR1 TDD 500us, FR2 TDD 125us). Refer to 5G_L2_540_replaced([11156739](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25BnwfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).



In FR1 TDD, when actFlexibleBiSlotDurationMode is set to "partial" [CB013305-BC] or "full" [End CB013305-BC] and the 750us timing pattern (as defined in 5G_L2_22818_replaced([11157164](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25EEEfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is activated, the biSlot duration is extented by 250us, resulting in a total processing budget of 750us.

---

#### 2.14.2.6.0-4 UE Skipping FD-UE Skipping - Step 3 (Reiteration) (ID: 11213262)

**2.14.2.6.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11213265`)

UE Skipping 5G-L2-PS shall perform this requirement only if FD-UE skipping is active as per 5G_L2_1859_replaced([11213118](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-purfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The UL scheduler shall perform a second iteration of step 1 (5G_L2_14796_replaced([11213195](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-qVwPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and step 2 (5G_L2_14797_replaced([11213228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-qVxfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), if all of the following conditions are met:

  * [CNI-108780-A] actSmartRoundInFdUeSkipping = FALSE [End CNI-108780-A]
  * actLastSchedulerOlcEnh = TRUE.
  * maxNumFdUes = 0.



5G-L2-PS shall perform only up to 2 iterations of steps 1 and 2.

Note: In the second iteration 5G-L2-PS increases the time budget for scheduling by rdSlotProcessingRatioExtension and thus decreases the time reservation for FIFO message queue processing, exceptionally. Like this, the chances of achieving maxNumFdUes > 0 are better and thus UEs with RA msg3 are skipped less often and the cell throughput is preserved more reliably.  


The resultant maxNumFdUes shall be the maximum number of FD UEs scheduled by the corresponding FD scheduler in the slot.

The PUSCH receive request for slot aggregation(SAg)2x or 4x bundle repetitions shall not be dropped due to overload control actions. Please refer to 5G_UL_ALG_20444 and 5G_L2_12946_replaced([11177051](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_264o9PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). As a result, for UL scheduler the maxNumFdUes shall not be less than the total number of 2x or 4x repetition scheduling UE

With:

  * actLastSchedulerOlcEnh is received in the PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq (see 5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * maxNumFdUes was computed in step 2 (5G_L2_14797_replaced([11213228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-qVxfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * rdSlotProcessingRatioExtension is defined in 5G_L2_10983_replaced([11190090](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28UMWvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * [CNI-108780-A] actSmartRoundInFdUeSkipping is received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End CNI-108780-A]

---

#### 2.14.2.6.0-5 UE Skipping FDM-UE Skipping (ID: 11213271)

**2.14.2.6.0-5.0-6**  (ID: `11213311`)

UE Skipping 5G-L2-PS shall abort the FDM UE selection according to 5G_UP_ALG_13161_replaced([11177648](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuwsOfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_13163_replaced([11196799](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwFh5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) as described hereafter.

IF (actFdmUeSkippingOlc = TRUE) AND (actFdmScheduling = TRUE)**: 5G-L2-PS shall execute the below algorithm.**

ELSE IF (/NRBTS/NRcell/actFdmSchedulingInitialBWP = TRUE ) AND (the number of initial transmission of MSG3 > 1) AND (All initial transmission of MSG3 have been selected by FDM): 5G-L2-PS shall also execute the below algorithm.

ELSE: 5G-L2-PS shall skip the below algorithm.

Right at the start of FDM scheduling (see 5G_UP_ALG_4293_replaced([11177286](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuuP-fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_4871_replaced([11196450](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwCepPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

  * UL and DL schedulers shall initialize the number of selected UEs as: numOfSelectedFdmUes = 0
  * UL and DL schedulers shall determine the amount of time which may still be used for scheduling in the current slot:



allowedRemainingSchedTime = min{ estimatedRemainingSchedTime, actualRemainingSchedTime }, with:

estimatedRemainingSchedTime = (slotDuration - slotDelay) * availableSlotRatio - elapsedTimeSinceSlotStart

IF slotDelay > avgSlotDelay + rdSlotDelayMarginForProcessingRatioExtension_uSec:

availableSlotRatio = slotProcessingRatioCellShare

Where slotProcessingRatioCellShare is the sum of slotAwareOptimalRatio of all the schedulers of the given cell in the given core.

Note: In the current deployment the value of slotProcessingRatioCellShare would match to the slotAwareOptimalRatio as schedulers of different cells are deployed per core.

ELSE: availableSlotRatio = slotAwareOptimalRatio

Note: Even if slotDelay <= avgSlotDelay + rdSlotDelayMarginForProcessingRatioExtension_uSec, estimatedRemainingSchedTime may exceed the scheduler's share of the target duration ratio (5G_L2_5479_replaced([11212394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-ldMfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if another scheduler has run before in the same slot on the same core and has consumed more time than expected.

actualRemainingSchedTime = timeTillSlotBoundary - (1 - correctedSlotProcessingRatio) * slotDuration

IF slotDelay > avgSlotDelay + rdSlotDelayMarginForProcessingRatioExtension_uSec:

correctedSlotProcessingRatio = 1

ELSE:

correctedSlotProcessingRatio = slotProcessingRatio

  * UL and DL schedulers shall reserve time for the subsequent scheduling phases, including FD scheduling for 1 UE:



[Before PR836017]

In DL: reservedTime = avgMuMimoTime + avgResidualTdSchedTimeBeforeFd + avgFdUeTime + avgFdCommonTime + avgPostSchedTime

In UL: reservedTime = avgMuMimoTime + avgFdFirstUeTime + avgFdCommonTime + avgPostSchedTime

[PR836017]

In DL: reservedTime = avgMuMimoTime + avgResidualTdSchedTimeBeforeFd + avgFdUeTime + avgFdCommonTime + avgPostSchedTime + averageExcessPostSchedTimeInNs(i)

In UL: reservedTime = avgMuMimoTime + avgFdFirstUeTime + avgFdCommonTime + avgPostSchedTime + averageExcessPostSchedTimeInNs(i)

[End PR836017]

Note: avgMuMimoTime is equal to 0 if MU-MIMO is disabled, see 5G_L2_1863_replaced([11213446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  * UL and DL schedulers shall determine the point in time when the FDM UE selection has to stop:



targetFdmStopTime = allowedRemainingSchedTime - reservedTime + elapsedTimeSinceSlotStart

IF actDlMuMimo = TRUE: 5G-L2-PS shall initialize numOfSelectedFdmUes and targetFdmStopTime as described above only when it starts the FDM UE selection for the first CS2 list. For subsequent CS2 lists (see 5G_UP_ALG_4293_replaced([11177286](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuuP-fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) 5G-L2-PS shall start the FDM UE selection with the values of numOfSelectedFdmUes and targetFdmStopTime which were valid at the end of the FDM UE selection for the previous CS2 list.

Every time before checking a UE from CS2:

  * UL and DL schedulers shall check if the FDM UE selection has to be aborted:



IF (elapsedTimeSinceSlotStart >= targetFdmSlotTime) AND (numOfSelectedFdmUes >= minSchedUesPerSlotInHighLoad) AND (numOfSelectedFdmUes >= the number of initial transmission of MSG3):

5G-L2-PS shall abort the FDM UE selection.

ELSE:

5G-L2-PS shall continue the FDM UE selection and check if the current UE and subsequent UEs can be added to the set of 'to-be-scheduled UEs' (see 5G_UP_ALG_4293_replaced([11177286](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuuP-fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_4871_replaced([11196450](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwCepPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Whenever a UE from CS2 has been added to the set of 'to-be-scheduled UEs':

  * UL and DL schedulers shall increment the number of selected UEs as: numOfSelectedFdmUes += 1
  * UL and DL schedulers shall update the point in time when the FDM UE selection has to stop: targetFdmStopTime -= avgFdUeTime



After checking the last UE from CS2 or when FDM UE selection has to be aborted, the DL scheduler (or the UL scheduler) shall re-calculate the value of allowedRemainingSchedTime as described above and copy it to the event dlLoadControlData (5G_L2_6440_replaced([11203804](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_299yIvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) (or ulLoadControlData, 5G_L2_6441_replaced([11203655](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_299LEPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If the FDM UE selection had to be aborted due to lack of time the DL scheduler (or the UL scheduler) shall set the flag fdmUesSkipped in the event dlLoadControlData (5G_L2_6440_replaced([11203804](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_299yIvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) (or in ulLoadControlData, 5G_L2_6441_replaced([11203655](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_299LEPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to TRUE, otherwise to FALSE.

With:

  * slotProcessingRatio is defined in 5G_L2_15692_replaced([11212528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mESvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * rdSlotDelayMarginForProcessingRatioExtension_uSec: See 5G_L2_8685_replaced([11190336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28WBiPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * In DL: minSchedUesPerSlotInHighLoad = rdMinDlSchedUesPerSlotInHighLoad (see 5G_UP_ALG_13379_replaced([11193503](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvtHa_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * In UL: minSchedUesPerSlotInHighLoad = rdMinUlSchedUesPerSlotInHighLoad (see 5G_UP_ALG_13381_replaced([11209025](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwxeYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * slotDelay: See 5G_L2_1863_replaced([11213446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * slotAwareOptimalRatio: See 5G_L2_6333_replaced([11212562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * elapsedTimeSinceSlotStart: On the DL scheduler (or UL scheduler) it is the time which has elapsed since the start of DL pre-scheduling (or UL pre-scheduling respectively).
  * timeTillSlotBoundary: The time which is left in the current slot.
  * avgSlotDelay, avgMuMimoTime, avgResidualTdSchedTimeBeforeFd, avgPostSchedTime, avgFdUeTime, avgFdFirstUeTime and avgFdCommonTime: See 5G_L2_1870_replaced([11213602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * actFdmUeSkippingOlc is received in the PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * For actTwoCoresL2DeploymentFddFr1 see 5G_L2_16485_replaced([11141119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23mrf_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * **slotDuration is the processing time Budget for a slot and depends on the numerology (FR1 FDD 1000us, FR1 TDD 500us, FR2 TDD 125us). Refer to 5G_L2_540_replaced([11156739](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25BnwfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**
  * [PR836017] averageExcessPostSchedTimeInNs(i) is the average excess time in the post-scheduling phase in slot i, as per [12645241](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_whEQFUK0EfCH-cG2YrVgkA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). [End PR836017]



In FR1 TDD, when actFlexibleBiSlotDurationMode is set to "partial" **[CB013305-BC] or "full"**[End CB013305-BC] and the 750us timing pattern (as defined in 5G_L2_22818_replaced([11157164](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25EEEfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is activated, the biSlot duration is extented by 250us, resulting in a total processing budget of 750us.****

---

## 2.14.3 Load Severity Monitoring

### 2.14.3.1 Severity Metrics

#### 2.14.3.1.0-1 Severity Metrics Arithmetic Averages (ID: 12620208)

**2.14.3.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12620215`)

Severity Metrics 5G-L2-PS shall compute the arithmetic averages

  * preCsListSizeEachEvalPeriod (see [11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
  * cs1ListSizeMaxEachEvalPeriod (see [11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
  * slotProcessingRatioEachEvalPeriod (see [11216106](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXURfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))



by means of the sliding window averages

  * averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet (see [11213721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAGvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
  * averageCs1ListMaxSize (see [11213721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAGvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
  * averageSlotProcessingRatio (see [11213721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAGvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))



For every arithmetic average listed above, 5G-L2-PS shall proceed as follows.

In every radio frame, 5G-L2-PS shall capture one sample of the corresponding sliding window average. 5G-L2-PS shall capture the samples of one particular sliding window average always in the same slot of the radio frame. However, if 5G-L2-PS skips the slot in which the sample shall be captured due to high load, it shall capture the sample in the next available slot.  
Note: See the note on slot skipping in [12551505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ZL-9gCRLEfCNjfqfyUlvmw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_zl-9gcrlefcnjfqfyulvmw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9").

At the end of every evaluation period t as per [11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) and [11216106](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXURfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), 5G-L2-PS shall compute the arithmetic average as the sum of the captured samples divided by their number.

However, if the number of samples available at the end of the evaluation period t is less than evalPeriodInFrames (see [12551505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ZL-9gCRLEfCNjfqfyUlvmw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), 5G-L2-PS shall skip the computation of the arithmetic average and include the samples captured in evaluation period t in the arithmetic average of the next evaluation period t+1. In this case, the arithmetic average in evaluation period t+1 is the average of samples captured in evaluation periods t and t+1, which can be more than 16 samples. 

Rationale:  
5G-L2-PS might not be able to capture the expected number of evalPeriodInFrames (see [12551505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ZL-9gCRLEfCNjfqfyUlvmw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) samples per evaluation period, if it is busy with processing messages (e.g. cell setup request) for a sufficiently high number of slots. Such load peaks prompt the adaptive scheduler budget algorithm to reduce the slot processing ratio very much. Thus, the first samples of averageSlotProcessingRatio after the load peak reflect the exceptionally high load from the past slots and shall not be used as input to the arithmetic average, unless there are enough other samples which are not biased by the load peak any more. For simplicity, preCsListSizeEachEvalPeriod and slotProcessingRatioEachEvalPeriod shall be computed in the same way as averageSlotProcessingRatio.

---

#### 2.14.3.1.0-2 Severity Metrics Exponential Averages (ID: 12621808)

**2.14.3.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12621809`)

Severity Metrics 5G-L2-PS shall update the exponential averages

  * avgPreCsListSize (see [11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
  * avgCs1ListSizeMax (see [11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
  * avgSlotProcessingRatio (see [11216106](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXURfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))



by means of the arithmetic averages

  * preCsListSizeEachEvalPeriod (see [12620208](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_k86YcjfUEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
  * cs1ListSizeMaxEachEvalPeriod (see [12620208](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_k86YcjfUEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
  * slotProcessingRatioEachEvalPeriod (see [12620208](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_k86YcjfUEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))



at the end of every evaluation period t (see [11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) and [11216106](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXURfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), with the following exception.

If 5G-L2-PS has not computed an arithmetic average as per [12620208](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_k86YcjfUEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) in this evaluation period t, it shall skip the update of the corresponding exponential average.   
Otherwise, 5G-L2-PS shall update the corresponding exponential average, using the arithmetic average computed in evaluation period t as input to the IIR filter in [11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) or [11216106](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXURfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

---

#### 2.14.3.1.0-3 Severity Metrics Update Time (ID: 12551505)

**2.14.3.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12449308`)

Severity Metrics For FR1 cells, 5G-L2-PS shall distribute the updates of the severity metrics as follows:

Each cell deployed on a core is assigned a unique core-specific identifier ranging from 0 to (evalPeriodInFrames - 1), where:

_evalPeriodMSec is the period specified in 5G_UP_ALG_31301_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_h-Ph0vvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) in milliseconds._

_evalPeriodInFrames is calculated as evalPeriodMSec/10 (converting the evaluation period from milliseconds to frames)._

Note: If a cell deletion occurs, the unique identifier assigned to the cell is freed and can be reassigned to any newly added cell.

For every cell deployed on the core 5G-L2-PS shall proceed as follows.

If (currentSfn % evalPeriodInFrames == core-specific unique identifier of the cell), then:

  * In slot n = 1:  
The DL scheduler shall update the DL RT processing load severity metric (l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric, see 5G_UP_ALG_31301_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_h-Ph0vvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [PR832251] with the exponential averages avgPreCsListSize and avgCs1ListSizeMax from [12621808](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_iAfnQDocEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), unless these averages have not been computed at the end of this evaluation period. [End PR832251]
  * In slot n = 2:  
The UL scheduler shall update the UL RT processing load severity metric (l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric, see 5G_UP_ALG_31301_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_h-Ph0vvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).  
[PR832251] with the exponential averages avgPreCsListSize and avgCs1ListSizeMax from [12621808](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_iAfnQDocEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), unless these averages have not been computed at the end of this evaluation period. [End PR832251]
  * In slot n = 3:   
The DL scheduler and the UL scheduler shall update the soft-RT/NRT processing load severity metric per core (l2PsNrtCoreLevelSeverityMetric, see 5G_UP_ALG_31303_replaced([11216106](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_iFQIwPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).   
[PR832251] with the exponential average avgSlotProcessingRatio from [12621808](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_iAfnQDocEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), unless this average have not been computed at the end of this evaluation period. [End PR832251].  
Note: Although this is a core level metric, there are two instances of this metric in every cell, one in the DL and one in the UL. When DL and UL scheduler are deployed on the same core, the metrics must have the same value. This is ensured by updating the metrics in the same slot. When DL and UL scheduler are deployed on different cores, the metrics can have different values.



In every frame:

  * In slot n = 4:  
The DL scheduler shall update the NRT processing load severity metric at L2 pool level (l2PoolNrtSeverityMetric, see 5G_UP_ALG_31302_replaced([11216095](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_iB1oYPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).



[PR832251] If a scheduler skips a slot n in which a severity metric update is due, it shall perform the corresponding metric update in the next available slot.

Note: Skipping of a slot n occurs when the processing of the previous slot n-1 takes much more time than one slot duration, such that a scheduler gets the slot start indication for slot n only in slot n+1. [End PR832251]

Note: To avoid CPU spikes by concentrating the update of all severity metrics in a single slot, the above distribution technique is specified.

---

### 2.14.3.2 Enabling of Countermeasures

#### 2.14.3.2.0-1 Enabling of Countermeasures Main Activation (ID: 12447730)

**2.14.3.2.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `12704424`)

Enabling of Countermeasures 5G-L2-PS shall determine the main activation status of Extended U-plane Overload Handling and save it in the internal variable isExtendedUpOverloadHandling. 5G-L2-PS shall set isExtendedUpOverloadHandling = TRUE if all of the following conditions are met:

  * actExtendedUpOverloadHandling = TRUE
  * frequencyRange = FR1
  * [Before CB013709-CR-E] 5G-L2-PS is runnig on a Classical deployment [End CB013709-CR-E]



If any of the above conditions is not met, 5G-L2-PS shall set isExtendedUpOverloadHandling = FALSE.

Parameters:

  * actExtendedUpOverloadHandling is received in PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq ([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_r73nYPu3Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * frequencyRange is received in PsCnfg_AddressDistributionReq ([10966093](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UL-vvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).



Note:

actExtendedUpOverloadHandling = 1 (TRUE) corresponds to NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) = 0 (TRUE)  
actExtendedUpOverloadHandling = 0 (FALSE) corresponds to NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) = 1 (FALSE)

The Boolean values of NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) are inverted intentionally.

---

#### 2.14.3.2.0-2 Enabling of Countermeasures Activation and Deactivation Thresholds (ID: 12688458)

**2.14.3.2.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13429787`)

Enabling of Countermeasures For every R&D parameter listed below, 5G-L2-PS shall check if the activation and deactivation threshold given by the parameter value is valid or invalid.

For this purpose, 5G-L2-PS shall read the activation and deactivation threshold from the parameter value, applying the mapping specified in the R&D parameter's definition requirement.

5G-L2-PS shall assume that the activation and deactivation threshold is valid only if all the following conditions are met:

  * activation threshold > 0
  * activation threshold <= 100
  * deactivation threshold > 0
  * deactivation threshold <= 100
  * activation threshold >= deactivation threshold



If any of the above conditions is not met, 5G-L2-PS shall assume that both the activation and deactivation threshold is invalid.

5G-L2-PS shall perform this check for the following R&D parameters.

[11216783: rdPowerSavingsOlcDlPerCent](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxa-oPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_kxa-opvsee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9")

[11216795: rdMicroDtxOlcDlPerCent](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxa-ovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_kxa-ovvsee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9")

[11216807: rdNominalBitrateOlcDlPerCent](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxa-pPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_kxa-ppvsee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9")

[11216820: rdIntfAvdRbgRandOlcDlPerCent](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxa-pvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_kxa-pvvsee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9")

[11216833: rdMuMimoRedvUeLowOlcDlPerCent](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxa-qPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_kxa-qpvsee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9")

[11216846: rdMuMimoRedvUeMedOlcDlPerCent](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxa-qvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_kxa-qvvsee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9")

[11216858: rdMuMimoRedvUeHighOlcDlPerCent](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxa-rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_kxa-rpvsee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9")

[11216871: rdMuMimoDeactOlcDlPerCent](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxa-rvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_kxa-rvvsee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9")

[11216884: rdCaForbidScellActOlcFddDlPerCent](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxblsPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_kxblspvsee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9")

#### 2.14.3.2.0-3 Enabling of Countermeasures Countermeasures on PsUser Interface (ID: 12553496)

**2.14.3.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12711898`)

Enabling of Countermeasures [Before CB013709-CR-E]   
5G-L2-PS shall determine the activation status of countermeasures for signaling and scheduling overload specified in [11216714](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxaXlvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) and save it in the internal variable isExtendedSigSchedOvlProtectionEnabled. 5G-L2-PS shall set isExtendedSigSchedOvlProtectionEnabled = TRUE, if all the following conditions are met:   
[CB013709-CR-E]   
5G-L2-PS shall enable countermeasures for signaling and scheduling overload specified in [11216714](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxaXlvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), if all the following conditions are met:   
[End CB013709-CR-E] 

  * isExtendedUpOverloadHandling = TRUE
  * rdL2PoolSigOvlSuspPsProcOlcPerCent is valid as per [12688458](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_M5yDcFXMEfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
  * [Before PR872929] rdRrcTriggeredOlcUlPerCent is valid as per [12688458](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_M5yDcFXMEfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
  * rdRrcTriggeredOlcDlPerCent is valid as per [12688458](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_M5yDcFXMEfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
  * [PR872929] rdRrcTriggeredOlcUlPerCentFDD for FDD ([13412282](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Pw914xIfEfG3gf_qmG8Vww)) in the UL
  * rdRrcTriggeredOlcUlPerCentTDD ([13412284](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Pwt-QBIfEfG3gf_qmG8Vww)) in the UL for FR1 TDD
  * rdRrcTriggeredOlcDlPerCentFDD ([13412273](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_4yKCtRIcEfG3gf_qmG8Vww)) in the DL for FDD
  * rdRrcTriggeredOlcDlPerCentTDD ([13412279](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_lMn7oRIeEfG3gf_qmG8Vww)) in the DL for FR1 TDD [End PR872929]
  * [Before PR878959](l1HwVariant != 0 \(loner\)) OR (rdExtLoadCtrlOnAbil = TRUE)[End PR878959]
  * [CB013709-CR-E] (5G-L2-PS is running on a Classical deployment) OR (Bit 0 of rdActBitmapExtendedUpOlcOnCloud = 1) [End CB013709-CR-E]



[Before CB013709-CR-E]   
If any of the above conditions is not met, 5G-L2-PS shall set isExtendedSigSchedOvlProtectionEnabled = FALSE and apply the countermeasures for signaling and scheduling overload specified in [11214379](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-yRh_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).   
[CB013709-CR-E]   
If any of the above conditions is not met, 5G-L2-PS shall apply the countermeasures for signaling and scheduling overload specified in [11214379](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-yRh_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).   
[End CB013709-CR-E]

[Before PR878959]  
[CB013709-CR-E] If 5G-L2-PS is running on a Cloud deployment, then 5G-L2-PS shall maintain the internal variable isExtendedSigSchedOvlProtectionEnabled with range 0 (FALSE), 1 (TRUE). 5G-L2-PS shall set

isExtendedSigSchedOvlProtectionEnabled = Bit 0 of rdActBitmapExtendedUpOlcOnCloud

[End CB013709-CR-E]

[End PR878959]

  * isExtendedUpOverloadHandling: See [12447730](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_AH2tsAmcEfCT35inaBGo7g).
  * rdL2PoolSigOvlSuspPsProcOlcPerCent: See [11217161](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcz4fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

  * [PR872929] rdRrcTriggeredOlcUlPerCentFDD ([13412282](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Pw914xIfEfG3gf_qmG8Vww))

#### 2.14.3.2.0-4 Enabling of Countermeasures Countermeasures for Slot Duration Switching (ID: 12701977)

**2.14.3.2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `12704219`)

Enabling of Countermeasures 5G-L2-PS shall enable countermeasures for slot duration switching specified in [11116341](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2-H_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) = 0, if all the following conditions are met

  * isExtendedUpOverloadHandling = TRUE
  * rdSlotDurationSwitchingOlcPerCent is valid as per [12688458](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_M5yDcFXMEfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
  * l1HwVariant is not equal to 0 (loner)
  * [CB013709-CR-E] (5G-L2-PS is running on a Classical deployment) OR (Bit 1 of rdActBitmapExtendedUpOlcOnCloud = 1) [End CB013709-CR-E]



If any of the above conditions is not met, 5G-L2-PS shall disable the countermeasures for slot duration switching specified in [11116341](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2-H_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) = 0 and apply slot duration switching specified in [11116341](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2-H_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) = 1. 

[CB013709-CR-E] If 5G-L2-PS is running on a Cloud deployment, then 5G-L2-PS shall maintain the internal variable isSlotDurationSwitchingEnabled with range 0 (FALSE), 1 (TRUE). 5G-L2-PS shall set

isSlotDurationSwitchingEnabled = Bit 1 of rdActBitmapExtendedUpOlcOnCloud

[End CB013709-CR-E]

Parameters:

  * isExtendedUpOverloadHandling: See [12447730](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_AH2tsAmcEfCT35inaBGo7g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).
  * rdSlotDurationSwitchingOlcPerCent: See [11217340](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxeB-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_kxeb-vvsee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9").
  * NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0): See note in [12447730](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_AH2tsAmcEfCT35inaBGo7g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).
  * l1HwVariant is received in PsCell_CellSetupReq ([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * [CB013709-CR-E] rdActBitmapExtendedUpOlcOnCloud: See [12696845](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kdoTUVviEfCVVMis1D3_Nw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). [End CB013709-CR-E]

#### 2.14.3.2.0-5 Enabling of Countermeasures Countermeasures for PDSCH Skipping in Special Slots (ID: 12701990)

**2.14.3.2.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `12704456`)

Enabling of Countermeasures 5G-L2-PS shall enable countermeasures for PDSCH skipping in special slots specified in [11216120](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUSPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) = 0 if all the following conditions are met

  * isExtendedUpOverloadHandling = TRUE
  * rdPDSCHSkipSpecialSlotOlcPerCent is valid as per [12688458](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_M5yDcFXMEfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
  * l1HwVariant is not equal to 0 (loner)
  * [CB013709-CR-E] (5G-L2-PS is running on a Classical deployment) OR (Bit 2 of rdActBitmapExtendedUpOlcOnCloud = 1) [End CB013709-CR-E]



If any of the above conditions is not met, 5G-L2-PS shall disable the countermeasures for PDSCH skipping in special slots specified in [11216120](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUSPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) = 0 and apply PDSCH skipping in special slots specified in [11216120](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUSPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) = 1. 

[CB013709-CR-E] If 5G-L2-PS is running on a Cloud deployment, then 5G-L2-PS shall maintain the internal variable isPdschSkippingEnabled with range 0 (FALSE), 1 (TRUE). 5G-L2-PS shall set

isPdschSkippingEnabled = Bit 2 of rdActBitmapExtendedUpOlcOnCloud

[End CB013709-CR-E]

Parameters:

  * isExtendedUpOverloadHandling: See [12447730](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_AH2tsAmcEfCT35inaBGo7g).

  * NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0): See note in [12447730](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_AH2tsAmcEfCT35inaBGo7g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).
