#### 2.14.3.2.0-6 Enabling of Countermeasures Countermeasures for CA (ID: 12551499)

**2.14.3.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `12704239`)

Enabling of Countermeasures Extended overload control counter measures for carrier aggregation related to below requirements, can be triggered only if isExtendedUpOverloadHandling == TRUE(see [12447730: Main Activation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_AH2tsAmcEfCT35inaBGo7g?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and a extended CA countermeasure release control flag(see [12514718: rdExtendedOlcReleaseFlagForCa](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NsZ2wBagEfCV0v_Ffc8sJw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and the related threshold RD parameter is valid as per [12688458: Activation and Deactivation Thresholds](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_M5yDcFXMEfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9):

[11120584: CA Relationship management for FR1 due to scheduler processing overload](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqSb4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9),

[11122209: SCell scheduler level processing load status determination for CA activation decision for DL branch](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCEfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9),

[11122218: SCell scheduler level processing load status determination for CA activation decision for UL branch](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9),

[11122225: Core level scheduler processing load status determination for CA activation decision](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9),

[11122234: Evaluation of Scell scheduler processing load for Scell deactivation for DL branch](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9),

[11122241: Evaluation of Scell scheduler processing load for Scell deactivation for UL branch](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCGfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

On classical gNB, the extended CA countermeasure release control flag is rdExtendedOlcReleaseFlagForCa(see [12514718: rdExtendedOlcReleaseFlagForCa](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NsZ2wBagEfCV0v_Ffc8sJw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

[CB013709-CR-E]

And on cloud gNB, the extended CA countermeasure release control flag is the value of Bit3 of rdActBitmapExtendedUpOlcOnCloud(see[12696845: rdActBitmapExtendedUpOlcOnCloud](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kdoTUVviEfCVVMis1D3_Nw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

[End CB013709-CR-E]

Bellow table illuminates the control of CA countermeasure branch on classical gNB[CB013709-CR-E], and on cloud gNB the value of Bit3 of rdActBitmapExtendedUpOlcOnCloud can override rdExtendedOlcReleaseFlagForCa in the table[End CB013709-CR-E]:

|  |   
---|---|---  
| isExtendedUpOverloadhandling =0 | isExtendedUpOverloadhandling =1  
rdExtendedOlcReleaseFlagForCa = 0 | CA countermeasures before extension ON | CA countermeasures before extension ON  
extended CA countermeasures from this requirement is OFF | extended CA countermeasures from this requirement is OFF |   
rdExtendedOlcReleaseFlagForCa = 1 | CA countermeasures before extension ON | CA countermeasures before extension OFF  
extended CA countermeasures from this requirement is OFF | extended CA countermeasure from this requirement is ON when its R&D threshold is valid as per [12688458](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_M5yDcFXMEfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) |   
  
[CB013709-CR-E] If 5G-L2-PS is running on a Cloud deployment, then 5G-L2-PS shall maintain the internal variable isCaCountMeasEnabled with range 0 (FALSE), 1 (TRUE). 5G-L2-PS shall set 

isCaCountMeasEnabled = Bit 3 of rdActBitmapExtendedUpOlcOnCloud 

[End CB013709-CR-E]

Note: CA countermeasures before extension in this requirement means the overload control countermeasure trigger or recover against load metrics in [11159147: SCell activation check prevention](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25PDJfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), [11162761: Suspend DL buffer status monitoring](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25h-GfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), [11162772: Resume DL buffer status monitoring](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25h-G_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

#### 2.14.3.2.0-7 Enabling of Countermeasures Countermeasures for NBR (ID: 12702716)

**2.14.3.2.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `12704465`)

Enabling of Countermeasures DL: 5G-L2-PS shall enable countermeasures for DL NBR specified in [11175517](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kujQ2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) if all the following conditions are met.

  * isExtendedUpOverloadHandling = TRUE
  * rdNominalBitrateOlcDlPerCent is valid as per [12688458](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_M5yDcFXMEfC45IKMrv0u7Q)
  * l1HwVariant is not equal to 0 (loner)
  * [CB013709-CR-E] (5G-L2-PS is running on a Classical deployment) OR (Bit 4 of rdActBitmapExtendedUpOlcOnCloud = 1) [End CB013709-CR-E]



If any of the above conditions is not met, 5G-L2-PS shall disable the countermeasures for DL NBR.

UL: 5G-L2-PS shall enable countermeasures for UL NBR specified in [11194709](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv24YfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) if all the following conditions are met.

  * rdNominalBitrateOlcUlPerCent is valid as per [12688458](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_M5yDcFXMEfC45IKMrv0u7Q)
  * l1HwVariant is not equal to 0 (loner)
  * [CB013709-CR-E] (5G-L2-PS is running on a Classical deployment) OR (Bit 4 of rdActBitmapExtendedUpOlcOnCloud = 1) [End CB013709-CR-E]



If any of the above conditions is not met, 5G-L2-PS shall disable the countermeasures for UL NBR. 

[CB013709-CR-E] If 5G-L2-PS is running on a Cloud deployment, then 5G-L2-PS shall maintain the internal variable isNbrCountMeasEnabled with range 0 (FALSE), 1 (TRUE). 5G-L2-PS shall set

isNbrCountMeasEnabled = Bit 4 of rdActBitmapExtendedUpOlcOnCloud

[End CB013709-CR-E]

Parameters:

  * isExtendedUpOverloadHandling: See [12447730](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_AH2tsAmcEfCT35inaBGo7g).
  * rdNominalBitrateOlcDlPerCent: See [11216807](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxa-pPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_kxa-ppvsee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9").

  * l1HwVariant is received in PsCell_CellSetupReq ([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

**2.14.3.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12702858`)

Otherwise, 5G-L2-PS shall never trigger the activation and deactivation of the countermeasure.

### 2.14.3.4 SCell addition and activation check prevention

#### 2.14.3.4.0-1 SCell addition and activation check prevention (ID: 11213414)

**2.14.3.4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12680436`)

SCell addition and activation check prevention With enhanced MU MIMO enabled and MU aware TD scheduler enabled

---

**2.14.3.4.0-1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12680437`)

SCell addition and activation check prevention [CB014044-F]

When NRCELL.actDlMuMimoEnh is set to TRUE and NRCELL.NRDLMUMIMO.actMuAwareTdSch is set to TRUE, follow below algorithm

Denote candidate UEs list as S(these consists of non GBR UEs in Candidate set 2 list which are not already evaluated for to-be-scheduled list) , to-be-scheduled UEs list is L, total estimated PRBs needed for all the UEs in list L is NPRB = [image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical summation symbol. The summation is from u=1 to L.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/img-05111905.png[/image_path][/image-0] RBest (Note: NPRB and L also considers the UEs added in [11177311](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuuP_vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) Step 1.

Nsched = rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl

threshold = Nsched* (NRCELL.dlHighBufferPrioUeRatio/100) (see TODO)

Go through the list of candidate UEs in the descending order of TD metric

Step 1: For a UE, If estimated PRB need, RBest, is greater than or equal to [(NBW - NPRB)/(Nsched - L)], regardless of correlation for MU-MIMO UE, add this UE to L, else skip this UE and go to next UE and repeat Step 1

  *     *       * Update NPRB= min(NPRB + RBest , NBW), remove UE from S and add to L, L=L ∪ {u}, S=S{u}



Step 2: If, NPRB, is lesser than ‘NBW‘ and L is lesser than NSched, go to next UE and repeat Step 1. (Note: Prioritize UE with high buffer)

Step 3: If all UEs in the candidate UE list have been visited ~~and total estimated PRBs, NPRB, is less then N~~~~BW~~, then go through the candidate UE list and select the non-GBR UEs to to-be-scheduled list in the order of TD metric priority until “~~NBW is equal to NPRB and~~ L is equal to Nsched.“. ~~(Note: Prioritize SU-MIMO UEs)~~

  *     *       * Update NPRB= min(NPRB + RBest , NBW), remove UE from S and add to L, L=L ∪ {u}, S=S{u}



Atleast one K UE (see [12517594](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Get-8BiLEfC3upM2pE5-4w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for definition of K UE) shall be added to the to-be-scheduled list, L. (Note: Prioritize K UE)

~~Step 4: If NPRB, is equal to ‘NBW‘, and L is lesser than NSched, (Note: Prioritize MU-MIMO UE)~~

  * ~~Search for MU eligible UE through the candidate UEs list in the order of TD metric priority,~~
  * ~~Compute the correlation of MU eligible UE’s best beam to all the beams of MU eligible users in set L, say I_corr,~~
  * ~~Check if I_corr < NRCELL.NRDLMUMIMO.dlMuAwareCorrThd, remove UE from S and add to L, L=L ∪ {u}, S=S{u}~~
  * ~~If all UEs in the candidate UE list have been visited, then go through the candidate UE list and select the non-GBR UEs to to-be-scheduled list L in the order of TD metric priority until L is equal to Nsched.. Else, repeat step 4.~~



for RBest, see [11181264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku-HkfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

[End CB014044-F]

---

**2.14.3.4.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11213424`)

SCell addition and activation check prevention For FDD and TDD FR1 to prevent the load of one specific CPU core from increasing further due to CA load, when actCaOverloadCtrlEnh([Before CNI-131110]5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))[CNI-131110]5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))[End CNI-131110]) and rdActCaOverloadCtrlEnh(5G_L2_21410_replaced([11184837](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27tvbfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) are both TRUE, L2-PS shall apply a new mechanism to prevent buffer base Scell addition and activation check in downlink when detecting the high load state.

This criterion of high load state for one specific core is defined as follows, when any one of below condition fulfills:

• Any one of the DL scheduler’s ( averageCs1ListMaxSize < rdScellCheckSuspendCs1ListThresholdDL AND averageCs1ListMaxSize < averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet ) deployed on this core.

• Any one of the UL scheduler’s ( averageCs1ListMaxSize < rdScellCheckSuspendCs1ListThresholdUL AND averageCs1ListMaxSize < averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet ) deployed on this core.

When the load of this CPU core gets mitigation, SCell addition and activation check can be resumed if both below conditions fulfills:

  * Each one of DL scheduler’s ( averageCs1ListMaxSize >= rdScellCheckSuspendCs1ListThresholdDL + rdScellCheckResumeHysterCoff OR averageCs1ListMaxSize >= averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet + rdScellCheckResumeHysterCoff ) on this core.
  * Each one of UL scheduler’s ( averageCs1ListMaxSize >= rdScellCheckSuspendCs1ListThresholdUL + rdScellCheckResumeHysterCoff OR averageCs1ListMaxSize >= averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet + rdScellCheckResumeHysterCoff ) on this core.



The definition of averageCs1ListMaxSize can refer to 5G_L2_19562_replaced([11213721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAGvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The definition of averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet is available in 5G_L2_19562_replaced([11213721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAGvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The definition of rdScellCheckSuspendCs1ListThresholdDL can refer to 5G_L2_19863_replaced([11182729](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27d3yvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The definition of rdScellCheckSuspendCs1ListThresholdUL can refer to 5G_L2_19865_replaced([11183239](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27iJM_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The definition of rdScellCheckResumeHysterCoff can refer to 5G_L2_19867_replaced([11183554](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27klc_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

## 2.14.4 Measurements

### 2.14.4.1 Instantaneous Measurements

#### 2.14.4.1.1 Measurements per OLC Instance

##### 2.14.4.1.1.0-1 Measurements per OLC Instance Scheduling Phases (ID: 11213446)

**2.14.4.1.1.0-1.0-7**  (ID: `12792535`)

Measurements per OLC Instance For each slot, UL and DL schedulers shall measure time taken for each of the below scheduling phases.

  * slotDelay - It shall consider the time delay between the theoretical start of the slot boundary (btuReferenceSync) and the slot Synchro indication received by the scheduler. In case of multiple schedulers sharing the core, slotDelay of the scheduler which started first in the slot shall be considered as the slotDelay for other schedulers in the slot.



Note: When actFlexibleBiSlotDurationMode flag is set to "partial" or "full" and the 750us timing pattern is activated (as defined in 5G_L2_22818_replaced([11157164](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25EEEfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the slot boundary (btuReferenceSync) of the second NRTslot (with 250us duration) and the second Bidirectional Slot (with a 750us duration) differs from the boundaries of other slots.

The slotDelay for these slots is computed based on the toBeScheduledSlotTable defined in 5G_L2_23089_replaced([11157211](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25EEJvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  * preAndTdTime -



The time taken by the scheduler from reception of slot synchro indication to the beginning of each FD scheduler shall be included in the preAndTdPhase. It shall be measured for each of the FD cores independently.

  * muMimoTime -



In DL: If actDlMuMimoEnh = TRUE (5G_L2_IF_1871_replaced([10968710](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UZaE_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))): The time spent for virtual UE based MU MIMO scheduling (see 5G_UP_ALG_7427_replaced([11142415](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4XVfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

ELSE: muMimoTime = 0.

In UL: If actUlMuMimo = TRUE (5G_L2_IF_2296_replaced([10968800](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UZaH_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))): The time spent for overlapFDM based MU MIMO scheduling (see 5G_UP_ALG_8265_replaced([11145653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksA6RPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

ELSE: muMimoTime = 0.

  * In DL: residualTdSchedTimeBeforeFd -



The time span from the end of TD scheduling till the start of each FD scheduling. It shall be measured for each of the FD cores independently.

Note: In the UL this time span is neglected.

  * fdTime - The complete time taken by the FD-EO shall be considered in the fdPhase. In case of deployments with FD parallelization, fdTime shall be measured for each of the FD cores independently.

  * fdCommonTime - The portion of the FD scheduling time (fdTime) which doesn't depend on the number of scheduled UEs.

  * postSchedTime - The time consumed in the TD-core from the handling of FD-scheduler responses to the end of slot handler post processing shall be considered in the postSchedPhase. if DPA is eanbled(refer to 5G_L2_589_replaced([11158134](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25Jjm_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), DPA processing time(5G_L2_589_replaced([11158134](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25Jjm_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) should be excluded from postSchedTime.

  * postSchedTimeDeviation - The difference between postSchedTime measured in the current slot and avgPostSchedTime (see [11213602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

  * [CB014680-E] pureSchedulingTime - 
  * In DL scheduler it is the time taken by preAndTdTime, postSchedTime and fdTime.
  * In UL scheduler it is the time taken from reception of slot synchro indication to the end of slot handler post processing. [End CB014680-E]

---

##### 2.14.4.1.1.0-2 Measurements per OLC Instance fdUeTime (ID: 11213485)

**2.14.4.1.1.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11213504`)

Measurements per OLC Instance For each slot, UL and DL schedulers shall calculate fdUeTime as the ratio of fdTime (see 5G_L2_1863_replaced([11213446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to the actual number of scheduled UEs. [Before CNI-105882-B] In case of deployments with FD parallelization, the max of fdUeTime from all the FD cores shall be considered as effective fdUeTime for the slot [CNI-105882-B] In case of deployments with FD parallelization and if three (3) cores are deployed for FD parallelization, fdUeTime shall be considered for each of the FD cores independently for the slot. [End CNI-105882-B]

---

##### 2.14.4.1.1.0-3 Measurements per OLC Instance fdFirstUeTime (ID: 11213511)

**2.14.4.1.1.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `12714020`)

Measurements per OLC Instance For each slot, UL scheduler and DL scheduler shall calculate fdFirstUeTime as the time taken in FD scheduling by the first scheduled UE.

In deployments with FD parallelization, the maximum of fdFirstUeTime from all the FD cores shall be considered as effective fdFirstUeTime for the slot.

[Before PR843502]

The DL scheduler shall use fdFirstUeTime only to compute the exponential average avgFdFirstUeTime (5G_L2_1870_replaced([11213602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and to log the value in the TTI trace event dlLoadControlData (5G_L2_6440_replaced([11203804](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_299yIvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The DL scheduler shall not use fdFirstUeTime for any other purpose. [End PR843502]

Note: This specification is to take into account the fact that the first Fd Ue takes more time than other Fd Ues due to hardware issues.

---

##### 2.14.4.1.1.0-4 Measurements per OLC Instance slotProcessingTime (ID: 11213529)

**2.14.4.1.1.0-4.0-10**  (ID: `12822944`)

Measurements per OLC Instance For each slot, UL and **DL schedulers shall calculate the slotProcessingTime as**

On DL schedulers:   
slotProcessingTime = max{preAndTdTime(fdSchedulerIndex) + fdCommonTime(fdSchedulerIndex) + fdFirstUeTime(fdSchedulerIndex) + [Before PR864517]fdUeTime(fdSchedulerIndex) [PR864517] adaptedFdUeTime(fdSchedulerIndex) [End PR864517] * (targetFdUes(fdSchedulerIndex) - 1) + postSchedTime

On UL schedulers:

slotProcessingTime = preAndTdTime + postSchedTime + fdFirstUeTime + [Before PR864517]fdUeTime[PR864517] adaptedFdUeTime [End PR864517]* (targetFdUes - 1) + fdCommonTime

where,

  * preAndTdTime, postSchedTime are described in 5G_L2_1863_replaced([11213446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * fdUeTime computation is described in 5G_L2_1865_replaced([11213485](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK7vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * fdFirstUeTime computation is described in 5G_L2_7009_replaced([11213511](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sx8_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * fdCommonTime is described in 5G_L2_1863_replaced([11213446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * fdSchedulerIndex (refer to 5G_L2_4595_replaced([11140997](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23mEavvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for definition) **are the indexes of the FD schedulers (PS-FD EO) deployed for FD parallelization in DL.**
  * [PR864517]adaptedFdUeTime shall prevent artificially lowering of slotProcessingTime in slots where only one UE is scheduled resulting in the fdUeTime measurement to be 0, L2-PS shall compute the adaptedFdUeTime as below:



IF fdUeTime == 0

adaptedFdUeTime = avgFdUeTime

ELSE

adaptedFdUeTime = fdUeTime

  * avgFdUeTime computation is described in [13338450](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_F1ONJNq2EfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_F1ONJNq2EfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").



[End PR864517]

On DL schedulers:

If FDM is enabled (actFdmScheduling = TRUE) scheduling fairness consideration functionality is activated:

[PR864271]IF the second LSB of rdActCb014680OlcImprovement remains unset (i.e., not equal to 1) AND (actStatelessSchedLoadBalancer is disabled), then[End PR864271]

targetFdUes = min(proposedCs1SizePreventiveOlc, rrmMaxNumUesFdmPreventiveOlc + additionalMargin)

[PR864271]

ELSE // second LSB of rdActCb014680OlcImprovement is equal to 1

targetFdUes = min{maxScheduledUes, min(proposedCs1SizePreventiveOlc, rrmMaxNumUesFdmPreventiveOlc + additionalMargin)}[End PR864271]

else

targetFdUes = numSchedAndSkippedFdUes

On UL schedulers:

If scheduling fairness consideration functionality is activated (actSchedFairnessUlOlc = TRUE):

[PR864271]IF the second LSB of rdActCb014680OlcImprovement remains unset (i.e., not equal to 1) AND (actStatelessSchedLoadBalancer is disabled), then[End PR864271]

targetFdUes = min(proposedCs1SizePreventiveOlc, rrmMaxNumUesFdmPreventiveOlc + additionalMargin)

[PR864271]ELSE // second LSB of rdActCb014680OlcImprovement is equal to 1

targetFdUes = min{maxScheduledUes, min(proposedCs1SizePreventiveOlc, rrmMaxNumUesFdmPreventiveOlc + additionalMargin)}[End PR864271]

else

targetFdUes = numSchedAndSkippedFdUes

[PR864271]

Where 5G-L2-PS shall compute maxScheduledUes as below:

maxScheduledUes = max{1, numSchedAndSkippedFdUes}

[End PR864271]

Where 5G-L2-PS shall compute rrmMaxNumUesFdmPreventiveOlc as follows.

If all of the following conditions are met:

  * actCsReductionFactorOlc = TRUE
  * actFdmScheduling = TRUE
  * In UL only: actSchedFairnessUlOlc = TRUE
  * pucchModeSelect = longPucch
  * **[CB014680-A] IF the second LSB of rdActCb014680OlcImprovement remains unset (i.e., not equal to 1) OR (actStatelessSchedLoadBalancer is disabled), then**[End CB014680-A] Only 1 scheduler is deployed on the local core.****



then

IF the first LSB of rdActCb014680OlcImprovement remains unset (i.e., not equal to 1), then

rrmMaxNumUesFdmPreventiveOlc = min{ max{ 1, floor{ dynamicCsReductionFactorPreventive * cs1ListMaxSizePreventive } }, rrmMaxNumUesFdmWithoutPoolingRestriction }

else

rrmMaxNumUesFdmPreventiveOlc is calculated as described in [11213384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj2vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), with the exception that the cs1Size used in the calculation must be the cs1ListMaxSizePreventive proposed from preventive overload control ([11212613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrWfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), [11212749](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-n5cPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-n5cPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9")), rather than the value derived from corrective overload control for the slot.

rrmMaxNumUesFdmPreventiveOlc = min{rrmMaxNumUesFdmPreventiveOlc, rrmMaxNumUesFdmWithoutPoolingRestriction}

else

rrmMaxNumUesFdmPreventiveOlc is calculated as described in 5G_L2_7048_replaced([11213384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj2vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with the exception that cs1Size used in the calculation shall be the cs1ListMaxSizePreventive from preventive overload control (5G_L2_1832_replaced([11212613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrWfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and not the final value from corrective overload control for the slot.

  * additionalMargin = 1 for DL scheduler,
  * additionalMargin = rdUlAdditionalFdUeMargin(5G_L2_12836_replaced([11190559](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28X2sPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for UL scheduler
  * proposedCs1SizePreventiveOlc is the maximum CS1 Size proposed by preventive overload control (see 5G_L2_1832_replaced([11212613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrWfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * numSchedAndSkippedFdUes = sum{ numSchedUes, numSkippedUes } by the FD EO. In case of deployments with FD parallelization, numSchedAndSkippedFdUes shall be maintained for each of the FD cores independently.
  * actCsReductionFactorOlc is received in PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * actFdmScheduling is received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_128_replaced([10969448](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Ucdbvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * actSchedFairnessUlOlc is received in the PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * dynamicCsReductionFactorPreventive is computed in 5G_L2_22296_replaced([11213322](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-q8zvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * cs1ListMaxSizePreventive is computed in 5G_L2_1841_replaced([11212749](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-n5cPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * pucchModeSelect is received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * rrmMaxNumUesFdmWithoutPoolingRestriction is equal to rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl (5G_UP_ALG_10610_replaced([11179079](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku3Z6_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the DL and equal to rrmMaxNumUesFdmUl (5G_UP_ALG_10654_replaced([11199273](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwMPmfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the UL when scheUePoolingAllowed = FALSE. scheUePoolingAllowed is received in PsCnfg_AddressDistributionReq (5G_L2_IF_4789_replaced([10966093](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UL-vvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * rdActCb014680OlcImprovement is defined in[12636258](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_VQda4UAdEfCal_QUJn4xrg).
  * actStatelessSchedLoadBalancer is received in the PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq ([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and modified in PsCell_CellGroupReconfigReq([10966782](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UQQMfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UQQMfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9")).



Note1: numSkippedUes shall only consider the UEs which are skipped scheduling due to overload control (see 5G_L2_1859_replaced([11213118](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-purfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For example,

  * if maxUesSchedulableByFdEo=4 #cs2Ues=2 & #FdUes proposed by overload control = 2, numSkippedFd = 0
  * if maxUesSchedulableByFdEo=4 #cs2Ues=3 & #FdUes proposed by overload control = 1, numSkippedFd = 2



Note2: additionalMargin=1 is added as a workaround to reduce FD skipping. Depending on the change in the load, there will be slight fluctuations in CS1 size/target FD Ues proposed from load control. As a result, during those fluctuations, FD skipping is observed due to slightly higher load in few of the slots. So, to mitigate this effect, with additional margin, FD time of one additional UE is artificially added in slot processing time. When FD skipping functionality is changed so that unused PRBs doesnt occur in FR1, this additional margin could be removed.

Note3:  
Only the scheduling of the first FD UE takes more time than other FD UEs scheduling. So the fdFirstUeTime is added separately of (targetFdUes - 1) * fdUeTime.

---

##### 2.14.4.1.1.0-5 Measurements per OLC Instance remainingSchedulingBudget (ID: 13381549)

**2.14.4.1.1.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `13381551`)

Measurements per OLC Instance For each slot, DL and UL scheduler shall determine the remainingSchedulingBudget which is the difference between scheduler budget allocated for the current slot and the pureSchedulingTime used by that scheduler in the same slot:

remainingSchedulingBudget = schedulerBudget - pureSchedulingTime 

where,

schedulerBudget is computed as:

schedulerBudget = slotAwareOptimalRatio * (slotDuration - slotDelay)

[PR873363]

Additionally, scheduler shall compute an instantaneous boolean variable "isRemainingBudgetTooHighPerSlot" as below:

isRemainingBudgetTooHighPerSlot = remainingSchedulingBudget > rdRemainingBudgetThresholdForLoadBalancing_Us

which is used in computation of sliding-window metric "percentageSlotsWithTooHighRemainingBudget".

[End PR873363]

Note:

  * slotDelay and pureSchedulingTime are described in [11213446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  * slotDuration is the processing time Budget for a slot and depends on the numerology (FR1 FDD 1000us, FR1 TDD 500us, FR2 TDD 125us). Refer [11156739](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25BnwfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). In FR1 TDD, when actFlexibleBiSlotDurationMode is set to "partial" or "full" and the 750us timing pattern (as defined in [11157164](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25EEEfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is activated, the biSlot duration is extended by 250us, resulting in a total processing budget of 750us.
  * slotAwareOptimalRatio is calculated in [11212562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) and adjusted in [11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)/[12823011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3sa_QaoJEfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3sa_QaoJEfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9") (if Load Balancing between schedulers applies).
  * [PR873363]rdRemainingBudgetThresholdForLoadBalancing_Us is defined in [13379557](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Q_4QZ_3kEfCPDo8cGBoqIw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Q_4QZ_3kEfCPDo8cGBoqIw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").
  * percentageSlotsWithTooHighRemainingBudget is defined in [11213721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAGvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAGvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").[End PR873363]

---

#### 2.14.4.1.2 Measurements per 5G-L2-PS Core

##### 2.14.4.1.2.0-1 Measurements per 5G-L2-PS Core Slot Utilization (ID: 11213581)

**2.14.4.1.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13452884`)

Measurements per 5G-L2-PS Core The slot utilization is the total amout of time which a 5G-L2-PS core spends on scheduling, message processing or any other task in a certain slot.

5G-L2-PS shall measure the slotUtilization per 5G-L2-PS core. 

5G-L2-PS shall measure the slotUtilization in every slot of the slot pattern, regardless of the slot's format (see 5G_UP_ALG_2293_replaced([11114641](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpmfaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and load type (see 5G_L2_6333_replaced([11212562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and no matter if the slot is muted due to PRB pooling (see 5G_L2_4516_replaced([11174514](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26kf6vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or blanked due to RF cooling (see 5G_L2_12735_replaced([11177084](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_264o-vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

In every slot, 5G-L2-PS shall sum up the time it has spent on all tasks and write the result to parameter slotUtilization. Depending on a slot's format and load type and on the current load, this can include the following tasks:

  * pre-scheduling
  * TD scheduling
  * FD scheduling
  * post-scheduling
  * BBRM processing
  * DPA processing
  * message processing
  * any other task



However, 5G-L2-PS shall exclude the following tasks from the slot utilization measurements:

  * [CB015122-A]Only if DFT beam selection algorithm is proceeded by 5G-L2-PS (see [11214197](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_ZkY68PvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ) and [11153567](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_SqaksPvMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), then [End CB015122-A]SRS beam management.  
Rationale: [CB015122-A]When actSrsBmCalcInL1 is set to False (see [11214197](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_ZkY68PvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), then [End CB015122-A]SRS has its own load control (see 5G_L2_10210_replaced([11214193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-xDcfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and doesn't need the adaptive scheduler budget algorithm to reserve processing time for it. [CB015122-A]When actSrsBmCalcInL1 is True, then CoMa handling and beam calculations are moved to 5G-L1-DU and PS-SRSBM EO is not created.[End CB015122-A]



In deployments with FD parallelization, if the main scheduler is running on the given core:

  * 5G-L2-PS shall also add to the slotUtilization: the time of FD scheduling on DL core, if the conditions for three (3) cores deployment for FD parallelization in DL are met (refer to 5G_L2_4595_replaced([11140997](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23mEavvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and if rdActFr2EnhParallelDlFdFor8CC is set to 2 as defined in 5G_L2_14282_replaced([11181667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27VU7vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * Note: There is an idle time in the main scheduler while it is waiting for FD scheduling to be completed on other cores. This idle time is not reflected in the slotUtilization. It is not needed because the slotUtilization is not used in FR2 (see 5G_L2_15692_replaced([11212528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mESvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).



Notes:

  * The processing start and processing end of a slot in 5G-L2-PS differs from the slot boundaries in system time. When the load is high, the processing of a slot in 5G-L2-PS may take more time than one slot duration. Thus, the measured slotUtilization may be greater than one slot duration.
  * The slotUtilization shall be measured in every slot and reported in the TTI trace (5G_L2_6440_replaced([11203804](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_299yIvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_6441_replaced([11203655](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_299LEPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). However, not every slotUtilization value is considered for the computation of the average slot utilization (avgSlotUtilization), see 5G_L2_15591_replaced([11213737](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAHfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 2.14.4.1.2.0-2 Measurements per 5G-L2-PS Core Accumulated Scheduling Time (ID: 13457301)

**2.14.4.1.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13457302`)

Measurements per 5G-L2-PS Core 5G-L2-PS shall compute the accumulated scheduling time as the sum of all pureSchedulingTime values which all schedulers deployed on this core are logging in [11203804: dlLoadControlData](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_299yIvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) and [11203655: ulLoadControlData](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_299LEPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) in the current slot.

5G-L2-PS shall log the accumulated scheduling time in nano seconds as accumulatedSchedulingTimeNs in the TTI trace in [12460881: coreLoadControlData](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PDy28AqsEfCT35inaBGo7g?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

---

### 2.14.4.2 Average Measurements

#### 2.14.4.2.1 Measurements per OLC Instance

##### 2.14.4.2.1.0-1 Measurements per OLC Instance Exponential Averages (ID: 11213602)

**2.14.4.2.1.0-1.0-10**  (ID: `13338449`)

Measurements per OLC Instance In every OLC instance defined in 5G_L2_6333_replaced([11212562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 5G-L2-PS shall maintain the following exponential averages.

  * avgSlotDelay
  * avgPreAndTdTime
  * avgMuMimoTime
  * In DL: avgResidualTdSchedTimeBeforeFd
  * avgFdUeTime
  * avgFdFirstUeTime
  * avgFdCommonTime
  * avgPostSchedTime
  * averageExcessPostSchedTimeInNs[i]
  * avgSlotProcessingTime



In every OLC instance, 5G-L2-PS shall maintain multiple averages averageExcessPostSchedTimeInNs. For every slot i in a radio frame in which the OLC instance controls the load, 5G-L2-PS shall maintain one average averageExcessPostSchedTimeInNs[i].

If the conditions for three (3) cores deployment for FD parallelization in DL are met (refer to 5G_L2_4595_replaced([11140997](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23mEavvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and rdActFr2EnhParallelDlFdFor8CC is set to 2 as defined in 5G_L2_14282_replaced([11181667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27VU7vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) then:

in DL: avgPreAndTdTime, avgResidualTdSchedTimeBeforeFd, avgFdUeTime, avgFdCommonTime shall be maintained for each of the FD cores independently based on the fdSchedulerIndex (refer to 5G_L2_4595_replaced([11140997](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23mEavvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for defintion).

The exponential filter calculation for each of the above averages is:

avgValue(n) = filterCoefficient * instantValue(n) + (1-filterCoefficient) * avgValue(n-1)

where avgValue is a placeholder for the parameter name of the average and n is the current slot number. The initial value of avgValue shall be 0. When a filter is reset (see 5G_L2_1874_replaced([11213693](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAFPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) avgValue shall be reset to 0.

instantValue corresponds to:

  * slotDelay (5G_L2_1863_replaced([11213446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), preAndTdTime (5G_L2_1863_replaced([11213446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), muMimoTime (5G_L2_1863_replaced([11213446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), residualTdSchedTimeBeforeFd (5G_L2_1863_replaced([11213446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), fdUeTime (5G_L2_1865_replaced([11213485](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK7vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), fdFirstUeTime (5G_L2_7009_replaced([11213511](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sx8_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), fdCommonTime (5G_L2_1863_replaced([11213446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), postSchedTime (5G_L2_1863_replaced([11213446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), postSchedTimeDeviation ([11213446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and slotProcessingTime (5G_L2_1867_replaced([11213529](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sx9_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  
for  
avgSlotDelay, avgPreAndTdTime, avgMuMimoTime, **avgResidualTdSchedTimeBeforeFd, avgFdUeTime, avgFdFirstUeTime, avgFdCommonTime, avgPostSchedTime, averageExcessPostSchedTimeInNs[i] and avgSlotProcessingTime respectively.**
  * 5G-L2-PS shall use the instant values from the slots and the scheduler the OLC instance is mapped to.
  * For DL Exhaustive Scheduling, muMimoTime is the total time consumed for all MU UEs in [12483324](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_qbsGEQ-XEfCvOvZoOJBSnQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).



If DL and UL scheduler are running on different cores filterCoefficient corresponds to:

  * rdSlotMeasurementFilterCoefficient (see 5G_L2_1502_replaced([11189925](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28S-QPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))



Note: if Above6Ghz (i.e. scs received in the PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq is equal to 120) or if actTwoCoresL2DeploymentFddFr1 is set to True , DL and UL scheduler are always running on different cores and this filter is always used.

Otherwise, filterCoefficient corresponds to:

**TDD:**

  * rdSlotMeasurementFilterCoefficient (see 5G_L2_1502_replaced([11189925](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28S-QPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for DL and UL OLC instances 1.
  * rdSlotMeasurementFilterCoefficientInst2Tdd (see 5G_L2_1502_replaced([11189925](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28S-QPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for DL and UL OLC instances 2.



**FDD:**

  * rdSlotMeasurementFilterCoefficientInst1CommonCoreFdd (see 5G_L2_1502_replaced([11189925](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28S-QPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for DL and UL OLC instances 1.
  * rdSlotMeasurementFilterCoefficientLoadInst2Fdd (see 5G_L2_1502_replaced([11189925](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28S-QPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for DL and UL OLC instances 2.



**For actTwoCoresL2DeploymentFddFr1 see 5G_L2_16485_replaced([11141119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23mrf_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

[PR864517]

Note: avgFdUeTime shall follow the above definition for computing the exponential average. Additional special-case handling shall be applied as specified in [13338450](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_F1ONJNq2EfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_F1ONJNq2EfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").

[End PR864517]

---

##### 2.14.4.2.1.0-2 Measurements per OLC Instance Special-Case handling for avgFdUeTime (ID: 13338450)

**2.14.4.2.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13338452`)

Measurements per OLC Instance To address inconsistencies in avgFdUeTime when only one UE is scheduled, no fdUeTime measurement is available within L2-PS because the metric requires at least two UEs to be scheduled in a slot. In such cases, the average value is not updated and may may negatively impacting the system. To prevent this, any use of avgFdUeTime now applies the minimum of the avgFdUeTime and avgFdFirstUeTime.

avgFdUeTime = min {avgFdUeTime, avgFdFirstUeTime}

Note:

  * avgFdUeTime and avgFdFirstUeTime is defined in [11213602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").
  * fdUeTime is defined in [11213485](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK7vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

---

##### 2.14.4.2.1.0-3 Measurements per OLC Instance Updates of Average Measurements (ID: 11213648)

**2.14.4.2.1.0-3.0-10**  (ID: `13453575`)

Measurements per OLC Instance UL and DL schedulers shall consider the instantaneous slot measurements

  * [Before CB015327-SR-B] slotDelay [End CB015327-SR-B]
  * preAndTdTime
  * muMimoTime
  * residualTdSchedTimeBeforeFd (in DL only)
  * postSchedTime
  * fdUeTime
  * fdFirstUeTime
  * fdCommonTime
  * slotProcessingTime



for updating the corresponding average measurements as described in [11213602: Exponential Averages](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) only from the slots which satisfy the below conditions[.](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

  * At least one Ue is scheduled.
  * Only non DPA process slot if 2 FDD Cells or more than 2 FDD Cells are deployed in the same core and the number of active CA UE (count in PCELL in the same L2 sub pool) is greater than rdFDMReducedThresholdActiveCAUEnumber ([11188204](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Gw-PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), otherwise all slots.
  * At least one of the following conditions is met:
  * [Before CB015327-SR-B] The slot measurement is the slotDelay. [End CB015327-SR-B]
  * The max CS1 list size reduced by corrective OLC (overall reduction, see cs1Size(n) in [11212970: Control based on run-time measurements](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-pHlfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) is at least rdMinCs1ReductionOverallForOlcAverage of the size determined by preventive OLC cs1ListMaxSizePreventive, see [11212613: Preventive overload control](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrWfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9). I.e.:



correctiveCs1ListMaxSizeReductionFactor >= rdMinCs1ReductionOverallForOlcAverage

AND

The max CS1 list size reduced by corrective OLC (reduction due to slot delay only, see adaptedCs1ListSize in [11212970: Control based on run-time measurements](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-pHlfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) is at least rdMinCs1ReductionSlotDelayForOlcAverage of the size determined by preventive OLC (cs1ListMaxSizePreventive, see[11212613: Preventive overload control](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrWfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)). I.e.:

correctiveCs1ListMaxSizeReductionFactorDueToSlotDelay >= rdMinCs1ReductionSlotDelayForOlcAverage

Rationale: Average measurements shall not be updated in slots in which UL or DL scheduling take significantly less time than in other slots.

[Before CB015327-SR-B]

UL and DL schedulers shall consider the slot measurement postSchedTimeDeviation ([11213446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) from all slots for the average measurements averageExcessPostSchedTimeInNs[i], where i is a slot number ([11213602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

[CB015327-SR-B]

UL and DL schedulers shall consider the instantaneous slot measurements 

  * slotDelay
  * postSchedTimeDeviation



for updating the corresponding average measurements as described in [11213602: Exponential Averages](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) from all slots. UL and DL schedulers shall update averageExcessPostSchedTimeInNs[i] with postSchedTimeDeviation from the current slot i.

[End CB015327-SR-B]

With:

  * correctiveCs1ListMaxSizeReductionFactor was determined at the start of the current slot, see 5G_L2_1853_replaced([11212970](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-pHlfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * correctiveCs1ListMaxSizeReductionFactorDueToSlotDelay was determined at the start of the current slot, see 5G_L2_1853_replaced([11212970](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-pHlfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * rdMinCs1ReductionOverallForOlcAverage is defined in 5G_L2_21178_replaced([11191111](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28bhFvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * rdMinCs1ReductionSlotDelayForOlcAverage is defined in 5G_L2_21180_replaced([11191119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28bhGPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * [CB015327-SR-B] Instantaneous slot measurements are defined in [11213446: Scheduling Phases](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). [End CB015327-SR-B]

---

##### 2.14.4.2.1.0-4 Measurements per OLC Instance Reset of Average Measurements (ID: 11213693)

**2.14.4.2.1.0-4.0-4**  (ID: `13386097`)

Measurements per OLC Instance L2-PS UL and **DL schedulers shall reset the average measurements described in 5G_L2_1870_replaced([11213602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) if the number of FD Ues proposed due to overload control(see 5G_L2_1858_replaced([11213112](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-purPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is zero for _n consecutive slots._**

where n is taken from (1,6,11) in an incremental manner. For example, initially, n=1. After first reset, n is incremented to 6 and after second reset, n in incremented to 11.

[Before PR867568]  
Every UL and DL scheduler shall reset the measurements described in 5G_L2_1870_replaced([11213602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) after a period without UE scheduling. For this purpose, the scheduler shall distinguish the measurements by the OLC instance they belong to. If the following condition is met:

  * There was no UE scheduling in the last 100 slots mapped to a certain OLC instance.



Then the scheduler shall reset the average measurements which belong to this OLC instance.

[PR867568]  
Every OLC instance shall record the number of consecutive slots without UEs in the pre-scheduler candidate set in the variable numOfConsecutiveSlotsWithoutUes as described below.

At start-up, every OLC instance shall set 

numOfConsecutiveSlotsWithoutUes = 0.

In every slot mapped to the OLC instance in which there are no UEs in the pre-scheduler candidate set, the OLC instance shall set

numOfConsecutiveSlotsWithoutUes = numOfConsecutiveSlotsWithoutUes + 1.

In every slot mapped to the OLC instance in which there is at least 1 UE in the pre-scheduler candidate set, the OLC instance shall set

numOfConsecutiveSlotsWithoutUes = 0.

If the value of numOfConsecutiveSlotsWithoutUes is greater than or equal to 100, the OLC instance shall perform the following actions.

Set numOfConsecutiveSlotsWithoutUes = 0.

Reset the measurements in [11213602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

Furthermore, every OLC instance shall use the variable numOfConsecutiveSlotsWithoutUes for the reset of preventive load control specified in [13386484](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ZWcLMAHgEfGhFrIQm2O4Ew?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

[End PR867568]

---

#### 2.14.4.2.2 Measurements per Scheduler

##### 2.14.4.2.2.0-1 Measurements per Scheduler Sliding Window Averages (ID: 11213721)

**2.14.4.2.2.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `13451134`)

Measurements per Scheduler Every scheduler shall maintain the following sliding window averages.

  * averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet
  * averageCs1ListMaxSize
  * averageCs2ListMaxSize
  * averageRrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc
  * averageScheduledUes
  * [Before PR878826] avgRemainingSchedulingBudget [End PR878826]
  * percentageSlotsWithTooHighRemainingBudget



Every DL scheduler shall maintain the following sliding window averages.

  * averageSlotProcessingRatio



Every scheduler shall compute the sliding window averages as described in 5G_L2_19433_replaced([11213773](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-unJPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), where the length of the window is equal to the number of slots N in a radio frame, i.e. N=10 in FDD, N=20 in TDD FR1 and N=80 in TDD FR2.

For the sliding window average of percentageSlotsWithTooHighRemainingBudget, the length of the window for both DL and UL schedulers corresponds to the total number of slots within four consecutive radio frames.

  * FDD: Each radio frame contains 10 slots, resulting in a window size of N = 40 slots (10 slots × 4 frames).
  * TDD FR1: Each radio frame contains 20 slots, resulting in a window size of N = 80 slots (20 slots × 4 frames).
  * TDD FR2: Each radio frame contains 80 slots, resulting in a window size of N = 320 slots (80 slots × 4 frames).



The input samples to the sliding window average are:

  * DL: numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDl (5G_L2_226_replaced([11147731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NIYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * UL: numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUl (5G_L2_378_replaced([11151479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24ifmPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * cs1Size (5G_L2_1853_replaced([11212970](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-pHlfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * maxCs2Size (5G_L2_7049_replaced([11213344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj0_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc (5G_L2_7048_replaced([11213384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj2vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * slotProcessingRatio ([11212528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mESvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
  * scheduledUes ([11213112](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-purPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-purPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ"))
  * remainingSchedulingBudget ([13381549](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_j3ISxAAfEfGhFrIQm2O4Ew?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_j3ISxAAfEfGhFrIQm2O4Ew?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9"))
  * isRemainingBudgetTooHighPerSlot ([13381549](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_j3ISxAAfEfGhFrIQm2O4Ew?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_j3ISxAAfEfGhFrIQm2O4Ew?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9"))



For averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet, averageCs1ListMaxSize, averageCs2ListMaxSize, averageRrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc, averageScheduledUes, [Before PR878826] avgRemainingSchedulingBudget [End PR878826] and percentageSlotsWithTooHighRemainingBudget:

The DL scheduler shall use input samples only from slots with loadTypeDlOnly or loadTypeMixed.

The UL scheduler shall use input samples only from slots with loadTypeUlOnly or loadTypeMixed.

For averageSlotProcessingRatio:

The DL scheduler shall use input samples from all slots, no matter which load type they have.

loadTypeDlOnly, loadTypeUlOnly and loadTypeMixed are defined in 5G_L2_6333_replaced([11212562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 2.14.4.2.2.0-2 Measurements per Scheduler Exponential Averages (ID: 12792297)

**2.14.4.2.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12792298`)

Measurements per Scheduler Every scheduler shall maintain the exponential averages of the following parameters:

  * avgPureSchedulingTimeForSingleUe
  * [PR853954] avgPureSchedulingTimeForMaxSched [End PR853954]



The exponential filter calculation is given by:

avgValue(n) = (1 - filterCoefficient) * avgValue(n-1) + filterCoefficient * instantValue(n)

Here,

'avgValue' - represents the parameter name of the above average. The initial value of the filter would be set to first 'instantValue'.

'n' - represents the current slot number.

'instantValue' - corresponds to:

  * pureSchedulingTime measured in DL or UL scheduler as defined here [11213446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9"), when both cs1Size(n) and scheduledUes in the slot 'n' is equal to 1.
  * [PR853954] pureSchedulingTime measured in DL or UL scheduler as defined here [11213446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-sK5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9"), when  
for DL scheduler, cs1Size(n) is equal to rdMaxNumUeTdDl OR scheduledUes in the slot 'n' is equal to rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl.   
for UL scheduler, cs1Size(n) is equal to rdMaxNumUeTdUl OR scheduledUes in the slot 'n' is equal to rrmMaxNumUesFdmUl. [End PR853954]



'filterCoefficient' value are set as following:

  * For computing avgPreSchedulingTimeForSingleUe the filterCoefficient would be set to 0.1
  * [PR853954] For computing avgPureSchedulingTimeForMaxSched the filterCoefficient would be set to 0.1 [End PR853954]



For avgPureSchedulingTimeForSingleUe [PR853954], avgPureSchedulingTimeForMaxSched [End PR853954]:

  * DL scheduler shall use the input samples only from slots with loadTypeDlOnly and loadTypeMixed.
  * UL scheduler shall use the input samples only from slots with loadTypeUlOnly and loadTypleMixed.



[PR853954]For avgPureSchedulingTimeForMaxSched, each scheduler shall maintain an array of values corresponding to different rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl/rrmMaxNumUesFdmUl configured by BBRM.[End PR853954]

Note:

  1. loadTypeDlOnly, loadTypeUlOnly and loadTypeMixed are defined in [11212562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  2. cs1Size(n) is the maximum CS1 list size proposed by corrective OLC in current slot 'n' defined in [11212970](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-pHlfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  3. scheduledUes is the number of scheduled UEs defined in [11213112](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-purPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-purPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ").
  4. [PR853954]rdMaxNumUeTdDl is defined in [11182022](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27YYNvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27YYNvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").
  5. rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl is defined in [11179079](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku3Z6_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku3Z6_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").
  6. rdMaxNumUeTdUl is defined in [11182963](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27fs-fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27fs-fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").
  7. rrmMaxNumUesFdmUl is defined in [11199273](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwMPmfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwMPmfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").[End PR853954]

---

#### 2.14.4.2.3 Measurements per 5G-L2-PS Core

##### 2.14.4.2.3.0-1 Measurements per 5G-L2-PS Core Average Slot Utilization (ID: 11213737)

**2.14.4.2.3.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11213753`)

Measurements per 5G-L2-PS Core The average slot utilization is the average of the slot utilization (slotUtilization) defined in 5G_L2_15565_replaced([11213581](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-syAPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall determine the average slot utilization per 5G-L2-PS core.

At start-up, 5G-L2-PS shall initialize the average slot utilization as:

avgSlotUtilization = slotDuration * rdTargetSlotUtilization_perCent/100

5G-L2-PS shall update avgSlotUtilization at the beginning of slot n as follows:

avgSlotUtilization(n) = rdSlotUtilizationFilterCoeff * slotUtilization(n-1) + (1-rdSlotUtilizationFilterCoeff) * avgSlotUtilization(nPrevious)

5G-L2-PS shall update avgSlotUtilization in every slot, no matter which tasks it performs in the slot.

With:

  * rdTargetSlotUtilization_perCent is defined in 5G_L2_15239_replaced([11190670](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28YdxPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * rdSlotUtilizationFilterCoeff is defined in 5G_L2_15233_replaced([11190681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28YdxvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * n is the index of the current slot.
  * nPrevious is the index of the slot with the previous filter update.
  * slotUtilization(n) is the slot utilization measured in the current slot as per 5G_L2_15565_replaced([11213581](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-syAPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * slotDuration is the processing time Budget for a slot and depends on the numerology (FR1 FDD 1000us, FR1 TDD 500us, FR2 TDD 125us). Refer to 5G_L2_540_replaced([11156739](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25BnwfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).



In FR1 TDD, when actFlexibleBiSlotDurationMode is set to "partial" [CB013305-BC] or "full" [End CB013305-BC] and the 750us timing pattern (as defined in 5G_L2_22818_replaced([11157164](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25EEEfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is activated, the biSlot duration is extented by 250us, resulting in a total processing budget of 750us.

---

##### 2.14.4.2.3.0-2 Measurements per 5G-L2-PS Core Scheduler Processing Time (ID: 11213759)

**2.14.4.2.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11213764`)

Measurements per 5G-L2-PS Core The scheduler processing time is the average time spent by all schedulers on the core for scheduling tasks. The time spent on message processing is not included.

5G-L2-PS shall determine the scheduler processing time per 5G-L2-PS core.

5G-L2-PS shall update schedulerProcessingTime at the beginning of slot n, provided that the avgSlotUtilization is also updated in slot n as per 5G_L2_15591_replaced([11213737](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAHfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Otherwise, 5G-L2-PS shall not update schedulerProcessingTime. 5G-L2-PS shall perform the update as follows:

schedulerProcessingTime(n) = rdSlotUtilizationFilterCoeff * sum [k = 1...N] { contribution(k) } + (1-rdSlotUtilizationFilterCoeff) * schedulerProcessingTime(nPrevious)

N is the number of the schedulers running on the core.

k = 1..N is the scheduler index.

contribution(k) is:

  * 0, if scheduler k can't schedule UEs in slot n because the load type of the slot doesn't allow. Load types are defined in 5G_L2_6333_replaced([11212562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * avgSlotProcessingTime, if scheduler k can schedule UEs in slot n as per the slot's load type. If scheduler k has multiple OLC instances, then avgSlotProcessingTime is the value belonging to the OLC instance mapped to slot n.



With:

  * rdSlotUtilizationFilterCoeff is defined in 5G_L2_15233_replaced([11190681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28YdxvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * n is the index of the current slot.
  * nPrevious is the index of the slot with the previous filter update.
  * avgSlotProcessingTime is defined in 5G_L2_1870_replaced([11213602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.14.4.2.4 Computation Principles for Averaging

##### 2.14.4.2.4.0-1 Computation Principles for Averaging Sliding Window Averages (ID: 11213773)

**2.14.4.2.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11213782`)

Computation Principles for Averaging 5G-L2-PS shall compute sliding window averages as follows.

The length of the sliding window is denoted as N. The slots in the sliding window are the N-1 last slots plus the current slot. When a new slot n starts, 5G-L2-PS shall push the window forward by one slot, such that slot n is inside the window and slot n-N is pushed out of the window.

A slot in the sliding window may or may not contain a valid sample. The slots with valid samples in the window have indices k[0]...k[V-1], where V<=N is the number of valid samples in the window.

In every slot, 5G-L2-PS shall update the sliding window average as:

average = sum[ i=0...V-1 ] { sample in slot k[i] } / V

If there are no valid samples in the sliding window (V=0) then 5G-L2-PS shall set:

average = 0

---

### 2.14.5 DL/UL Load Balancing

#### 2.14.5.1 Load Control of schedulers placed on same core

##### 2.14.5.1.0-2 Load Control of schedulers placed on same core Enabling of Load Balancing (ID: 11213804)

**2.14.5.1.0-2.0-6**  (ID: `12591180`)

Load Control of schedulers placed on same core 5G-L2-PS shall enable load balancing for schedulers placed on same core

[CB014680-A]If NRBTS.actStatelessSchedLoadBalancer is set to False, then [End CB014680-A]5G-L2-PS shall perform load balancing with 4 load states [Before CB014680-A](5G_L2_9387_replaced\(\[11212471\]\(https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-ldP_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ\)\), 5G_L2_12520_replaced\(\[11212488\]\(https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mEQvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ\)\)) [CB014680-A] [12823009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_vxN4saoIEfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_vxN4saoIEfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9") [End CB014680-A].

[CB014680-A]If NRBTS.actStatelessSchedLoadBalancer is set to True, then 5G-L2-PS shall perform load balancing based on schedRatio as defined in [12823010](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0HPBQqoJEfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0HPBQqoJEfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9"). [End CB014680-A]

Load balancing between schedulers shall be done in all the different load types

\- loadTypeDlOnly (when Multiple DL scheduler are executed on same core)

\- loadTypeUlOnly (when Multiple UL scheduler are executed on same core)

\- loadTypeMixed (when DL-UL schedulers are executed on same core)

The defaultRatio for each of the DL / UL scheduler is the static share that is configured for scheduler during cell setup scenario or cell delete scenario. The defaultRatio is a factor of the slotProcessingRatio (5G_L2_15692_replaced([11212528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mESvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The defaultRatio shall follow following conditions.

  * In every slot, the sum of defaultRatio for all the schedulers on the core does not exceed 100%.
  * The defaultRatio of DL schedulers are greater than the defaultRatio of UL Schedulers on the same core.
  * In case of loadTypeUlOnly with UL and DL schedulers present on the same core, factoring of rdUlProcessingShareInUlOnlySlots (see 5G_L2_5893_replaced([11190262](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28VaevvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be done as defined in 5G_L2_6333_replaced([11212562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * Static share values are dependent on the deployment and if actTwoCoresL2DeploymentFddFr1 is set as false also on load type (loadTypeDlOnly, loadTypeUlOnly, loadTypeMixed), otherwise static share values do not depend on load type since only UL schedulers or only DL schedulers are deployed on one core.



IF **actTwoCoresL2DeploymentFddFr1 is set as TRUE**

|  |   
---|---|---  
Schedulers executed per slot | Default / Static Share Per DL scheduler on DL core of L2 Sub Pool | Default / Static Share per UL scheduler on UL core of same L2 Sub Pool  
1 DL / 1 UL | 100 | 100  
2 DL / 2 UL | 50 | 50  
3 DL / 3 UL | 33.3 | 33.3  
4 DL / 4 UL | 25 | 25  
5 DL / 5 UL | 20 | 20  
6 DL / 6 UL | 16.7 | 16.7  
  
ELSE

|  |   
---|---|---  
Schedulers executed per slot : Load Type | Default / Static Share Per DL scheduler | Default / Static Share per UL scheduler  
1 DL / 1 UL : loadTypeMixed | 70 | 30  
2 DL : loadTypeDlOnly | 50 | -  
2 DL / 1 UL : loadTypeMixed | 35 | 30  
1 DL / 2 UL : loadTypeMixed | 40 | 30  
2 UL : loadTypeUlOnly | - | rdUlProcessingShareInUlOnlySlots * 50  
1 DL : loadTypeDlOnly | 100 | -  
1 UL : loadTypeUlOnly | - | 100  
2 DL / 2 UL : loadTypeMixed | 35 | 15  
  
Notes:

  1. With CB009836, L2-PS supports up to 6 FDD DL or 6 FDD UL schedulers per core but support of such configuration at system level is left to subsequent feature.

---

##### 2.14.5.1.0-3 Load Control of schedulers placed on same core Supported Deployments in Load Balancing (ID: 11213845)

**2.14.5.1.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `11213873`)

Load Control of schedulers placed on same core 5G-L2-PS supports dynamic calculation of time budget on deployments with one DL and one UL Scheduler placed in same core.

The DL and UL scheduler can be of different cells in the same L2 Sub Pool.

In vDU deplyment, for TDD cells, 3 cells can be supported within one L2 Sub Pool.

Load balancing is done on a core deployed with 2 DL schedulers and 1 UL scheduler and on the other core deployed with 2 UL schedulers and 1 DL scheduler. Refer 5G_L2_4307_replaced([11140781](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23ldUPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

In FDD deployment with 2 cells or 1 cell per core and actTwoCoresL2DeploymentFddFr1 = False, any scheduler can exceed more than 450us in a slot such that aggregated slot ratio for all the scheduler does not exceed the slotProcessingRatio, as defined in 5G_L2_15692_replaced([11212528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mESvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In Classic HW, FDD deployment, if actTwoCoresL2DeploymentFddFr1 = False, Load Balancing is done for 2 cells on the same core between the 4 schedulers (2 DL schedulers, 2 UL schedulers), otherwise if actTwoCoresL2DeploymentFddFr1 = True, Load Balancing is done for up to [Before CB009836-C] 5 [CB009836-C] 6 [End CB009836-C] cells per two core L2 Sub Pool between up to [Before CB009836-C] 5 [CB009836-C] 6 [End CB009836-C] DL schedulers deployed on a core or between up to [Before CB009836-C] 5 [CB009836-C] 6 [End CB009836-C] UL schedulers deployed on the other core.

For actTwoCoresL2DeploymentFddFr1 see 5G_L2_16485_replaced([11141119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23mrf_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[Before CB009836-C] Note: L2-PS supports up to 5 cells per two core L2 sub pool (up to 5 FDD DL or 5 FDD UL schedulers per core). Nevertheless verification of up to 4 cells per two core L2 sub pool is in CB012528's scope but verification of 5 cells per two core L2 sub pool is in CB010448's scope. [End CB009836-C]

---

##### 2.14.5.1.0-4 Load Control of schedulers placed on same core Maximum and minimum value of single scheduler share (ID: 11214158)

**2.14.5.1.0-4.0-4**  (ID: `11214184`)

Load Control of schedulers placed on same core [Before PR732380]

Usage of Maximum value of single scheduler share shall follow rdSlotProcessingMaxPercentSingleSchedulerShare 

and Minimum value of single scheduler share shall follow

when Number of Scheduler per core in given slot = 2 , 1- rdSlotProcessingMaxPercentSingleSchedulerShare

when Number of scheduler per core in given slot >2 , (1- rdSlotProcessingMaxPercentSingleSchedulerShare )/ (Number of scheduler per core in given slot -1)

[Before PR732941-24R1]

[PR732380]

Usage of Minimum value of single scheduler share (MinSingleSchedShare) shall follow rdSlotProcessingMinSingleSchedulerShare_perCent (5G_L2_15593_replaced([11190176](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28UzbPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

and Maximum value of single scheduler share (MaxSingleSchedShare) shall follow

when Number of Scheduler per core in given slot = 2 , 1- rdSlotProcessingMinSingleSchedulerShare_perCent

when Number of scheduler per core in given slot >2 , (1- (rdSlotProcessingMinSingleSchedulerShare_perCent * (Number of scheduler per core in given slot -1))

[End PR732380]

[PR732941-24R1]

Usage of Minimum value of single scheduler share (MinSingleSchedShare) shall follow rdSlotProcessingMinSingleSchedulerShare_perCent (5G_L2_15593_replaced([11190176](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28UzbPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or rdMinSingleSchedulerShareTwoSchedulerPerCore_perCent (5G_L2_16235_replaced([11190185](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28UzbvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

and Maximum value of single scheduler share (MaxSingleSchedShare) shall follow

when Number of Scheduler per core in given slot = 2 , 1- rdMinSingleSchedulerShareTwoSchedulerPerCore_perCent

when Number of scheduler per core in given slot >2 , (1- (rdSlotProcessingMinSingleSchedulerShare_perCent * (Number of scheduler per core in given slot -1))

[PR732941-24R1]

Number of scheduler per core is derived from the PsCnfg_AddressDistributionReq (5G_L2_IF_4795_replaced([10966119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UMlw_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Rationale:

The maximum and minum value of single scheduler share is made as rnd parameter configurable. The value shall be finetuned based on testing results
