##### 2.14.5.1.1 State Based Load Balancing Algorithm

###### 2.14.5.1.1.0-1 State Based Load Balancing Algorithm Dynamic allocation of time budget between schedulers (ID: 11213879)

**2.14.5.1.1.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `12590937`)

State Based Load Balancing Algorithm [CB014680-A] When state based load balancing is configured (i.e. actStatelessSchedLoadBalancer is disabled),[End CB014680-A] 5G-L2-PS shall dynamically calculate slotAwareOptimalRatio between schedulers placed on same core, following below principles:

  * slotAwareOptimalRatio is **scheduler specific for each DL and UL scheduler.**
  * ratio value for each DL and UL schedulers are calculated individually.
  * dynamic calculation works only with FDM scheduling enabled
  * Algorithm starts with defaultRatio (see below)
  * The following applies:



There are four states defined . Each DL and UL Scheduler are evaluated for calculation of their respective load state.

  * Low load - when averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet (5G_L2_19562_replaced([11213721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAGvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for the given scheduler is equal to 0, for calculations see 5G_L2_5847_replaced([11213912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vOOvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * Nominal Load - refer to 5G_L2_12271_replaced([11214033](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-v1UPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for calculation.
  * Degraded Moderate Load - refer to 5G_L2_12271_replaced([11214033](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-v1UPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for calculation.
  * Degraded High Load - refer to 5G_L2_7901_replaced([11213922](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vOPPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for calculation.



Refer to 5G_UP_ALG_18049_replaced([11216367](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxYidfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the definition of each load state.

  * Calculated ratios are clipped to maximum and minimum values defined in 5G_L2_5852_replaced([11214158](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-xDYvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).



Following definitions are used:

cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdDL - calculated as: 0.9 * rdMaxNumUeTdDl (see. 5G_L2_3697_replaced([11182022](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27YYNvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdUL - calculated as: 0.9 * rdMaxNumUeTdUl (see. 5G_L2_3702_replaced([11182963](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27fs-fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Following constants are defined:

  * maxNumFdmUesForHighLoad = 6
  * defaultRatio as defined in 5G_L2_5841_replaced([11213804](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-unKfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * throttlingStep - equal to rdThrottlingStep (see 5G_L2_11851_replaced([11190548](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28XPrvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))



Rationale for constant values:

  * throttlingStep was chosen based on initial SCT testing, higher step is causing too much variation in other overload control mechanisms leading to more FD skipped UEs.



defaultRatio is set as legacy value from before with static allocation 70/30.

  * maxNumFdmUesForHighLoad was chosen arbitrary base on initial L2L3 integration testing as limit when 5G L2 PS starts cuting scheduling more drastically.
  * 90% for calculation cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdDL & cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdUL was chosen based on SCT testing. Higher values were causing too much toggling of algorithm at beginning of scheduling when cs1List size is unstable due to lack of measurements.



The slotAwareOptimalRatio of each scheduler shall be throttled up or down depending upon overallLoadcondition of the schedulers deployed in a core. Refer to 5G_UP_ALG_18051_replaced([11216380](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxZJcPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details on the handling of different overallLoadcondition.

overallLoadCondition - is the aggretated value of Loadstate of all the schedulers deployed in a core.

---

###### 2.14.5.1.1.0-2 State Based Load Balancing Algorithm Calculation of share on low load (ID: 11213912)

**2.14.5.1.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11213916`)

State Based Load Balancing Algorithm Under low load state share ratio should trend to default value.

For defaultRatio and throttlingStep see 5G_L2_5845_replaced([11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

IF (slotAwareOptimalRatio < defaultRatio)

slotAwareOptimalRatio += throttlingStep

ELSE IF (slotAwareOptimalRatio > defaultRatio)

slotAwareOptimalRatio -= throttlingStep

END

---

###### 2.14.5.1.1.0-3 State Based Load Balancing Algorithm Calculation of share on High load (ID: 11213922)

**2.14.5.1.1.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11213941`)

State Based Load Balancing Algorithm [Before CB012716-A]

Under High load state as defined in 5G_L2_5841_replaced([11213804](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-unKfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), share ratio calculation is as follow:

For avgCs1Size see 5G_L2_1832_replaced([11212613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrWfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If (rdEnableOLCforNScheduler (5G_L2_12274_replaced([11190587](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28X2tfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = False)

IF ( (numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL (5G_L2_226_replaced([11147731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NIYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) < avgCs1Size on DL) AND (numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUL (5G_L2_378_replaced([11151479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24ifmPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) < avgCs1Size on UL) AND (actSchedFairnessUlOlc(5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = FALSE) )

Number of UEs in the pre-scheduler candidate lists DL and UL is less than maximum allowed limit.

Keep current ratio as both DL and UL are not limited by maximum number of CS1 UEs

This means that currently calculated slotAwareOptimalRatio is enough for DL and UL to process everything on time.

ELSE IF ( (numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL (5G_L2_226_replaced([11147731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NIYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) > 0) AND (numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUL (5G_L2_378_replaced([11151479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24ifmPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) > 0) )

We are in High load and both DL and UL have UEs in the pre-scheduler candidate lists

calculate according to 5G_L2_7479_replaced([11214115](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-wcWvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

ELSE

We are in High load but only DL or UL have UEs in the pre-scheduler candidate lists

calculate according to 5G_L2_7483_replaced([11214145](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-xDYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

END

[End CB012716-A]

---

###### 2.14.5.1.1.0-4 State Based Load Balancing Algorithm Degraded High load State (ID: 11213947)

**2.14.5.1.1.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11213960`)

State Based Load Balancing Algorithm [Before PR770180] For avgCs1Size see 5G_L2_1832_replaced([11212613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrWfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End PR770180]

Degraded High Load is determined for a given scheduler when the following conditions are true:

  * [Before CB012716-A] rdEnableOLCforNScheduler (5G_L2_12274_replaced([11190587](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28X2tfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = True [End CB012716-A]
  * [Before PR770180] The numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL > 0 for given DL scheduler OR numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUL > 0 for given UL scheduler



[PR770180] averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet > 0 for the given scheduler. [End PR770180]

  * [Before PR770180] avgCs1Size < cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdDL for given DL scheduler OR avgCs1Size < cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdUL for given UL Scheduler



[PR770180] averageCs1ListMaxSize < cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdDL for a given DL scheduler OR averageCs1ListMaxSize < cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdUL for a given UL scheduler. [End PR770180]

  * IF (actSchedFairnessUlOlc(5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = True or given scheduler is DL scheduler )



[Before PR770180] when rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc (5G_L2_7048_replaced([11213384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj2vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) drops below defined threshold maxNumFdmUesForHighLoad for given scheduler

[PR770180] When averageRrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc drops below the defined threshold maxNumFdmUesForHighLoad for the given scheduler. [End PR770180]

ELSE

[Before PR770180] when avgCs1Size drops below defined threshold maxNumFdmUesForHighLoad for UL scheduler

[PR770180] When averageCs1ListMaxSize drops below the defined threshold maxNumFdmUesForHighLoad for the UL scheduler. [End PR770180]

  * IF (actSchedFairnessUlOlc(5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = FALSE)



[Before PR770180] numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUL (5G_L2_378_replaced([11151479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24ifmPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) >= avgCs1Size for given UL scheduler or

numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL (5G_L2_226_replaced([11147731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NIYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) >= avgCs1Size for given DL scheduler

[PR770180] averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet >= averageCs1ListMaxSize for given scheduler. [End PR770180]

Once Degraded High load is detected for a scheduler, the share is calculated as specified in 5G_UP_ALG_18051_replaced([11216380](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxZJcPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),5G_L2_12724_replaced([11214052](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-wcUvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[PR770180]

  * averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet, averageCs1ListMaxSize and averageRrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc are defined in 5G_L2_19562_replaced([11213721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAGvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).



[End PR770180]

---

###### 2.14.5.1.1.0-5 State Based Load Balancing Algorithm Caclulation of share based on number of UEs in the pre-scheduler candidate lists and number of allowed FD UEs (ID: 11213968)

**2.14.5.1.1.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `12776373`)

State Based Load Balancing Algorithm When number of FD UEs on DL or UL are limited below maxNumFdmUesForHighLoad (5G_L2_5845_replaced([11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) treshold by reduction of target FD users per slot mechanism (5G_L2_7048_replaced([11213384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj2vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), we try to even ratio of CS1 UEs as follows:

For throttlingStep see 5G_L2_5845_replaced([11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

csListRatioDL = rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc (5G_L2_7048_replaced([11213384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj2vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) on DL / numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL (5G_L2_226_replaced([11147731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NIYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

IF (actSchedFairnessUlOlc(see 5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = TRUE)

csListRatioUL = rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc (5G_L2_7048_replaced([11213384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj2vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) on UL / numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUL (5G_L2_378_replaced([11151479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24ifmPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

ELSE

csListRatioUL = [Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size [CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive [End CNI-136895-A] (5G_L2_1832_replaced([11212613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrWfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) on UL / numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUL (5G_L2_378_replaced([11151479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24ifmPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) 

IF (csListRatioDL < csListRatioUL)

Ratio for DL is smaller so give more time to DL  
slotAwareOptimalRatio += throttlingStep

ELSE IF (csListRatioDL > csListRatioUL)

Ratio for UL is smaller so give more time to UL  
slotAwareOptimalRatio -= throttlingStep

END

---

###### 2.14.5.1.1.0-6 State Based Load Balancing Algorithm Calculation of share on moderate load (ID: 11213986)

**2.14.5.1.1.0-6.0-3**  (ID: `11214006`)

State Based Load Balancing Algorithm [Before CB012716-A]

Under moderate load state share ratio should be based on DL/UL number of UEs in the pre-scheduler candidate lists

For avgCs1Size see 5G_L2_1832_replaced([11212613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrWfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

If (rdEnableOLCforNScheduler (5G_L2_12274_replaced([11190587](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28X2tfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = False)

IF ( (numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL (5G_L2_226_replaced([11147731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NIYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) < avgCs1Size on DL) AND (numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUL (5G_L2_378_replaced([11151479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24ifmPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) < avgCs1Size on UL) ) AND ( actSchedFairnessUlOlc(5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = FALSE ) )

Number of UEs in the pre-scheduler candidate lists DL and UL is less than maximum allowed limit.

Keep current ratio as both DL and UL are not limited by maximum number of CS1 UEs

This means that currently calculated slotAwareOptimalRatio is enough for DL and UL to process everything on time.

ELSE IF ( (numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL (5G_L2_226_replaced([11147731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NIYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) > 0) AND (numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUL (5G_L2_378_replaced([11151479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24ifmPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) > 0) )

Number of UEs in the pre-scheduler candidate lists on DL or UL is greater than maximum allowed limit.

Both DL and UL has UEs in the pre-scheduler candidate lists.

Calculate ratio as described in 5G_L2_7479_replaced([11214115](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-wcWvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

ELSE

Number of UEs in the pre-scheduler candidate lists on DL and UL is greater than maximum allowed limit.

Only DL or UL has UEs in the pre-scheduler candidate lists.

Calculate ratio as described in 5G_L2_7483_replaced([11214145](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-xDYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

END

[End CB012716-A]

###### 2.14.5.1.1.0-7 State Based Load Balancing Algorithm Degraded Moderate Load State (ID: 11214012)

**2.14.5.1.1.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11214026`)

State Based Load Balancing Algorithm Under Degraded moderate load state share ratio should be based on DL/UL number of UEs in the pre-scheduler candidate lists.

[Before PR770180] For avgCs1Size see 5G_L2_1832_replaced([11212613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrWfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End PR770180]

Degraded Moderate Load is determined for a given scheduler when the following conditions are true:

  * [Before CB012716-A] rdEnableOLCforNScheduler (5G_L2_12274_replaced([11190587](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28X2tfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = True [End CB012716-A]
  * [Before PR770180] The numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL > 0 for given DL scheduler OR numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUL > 0 for given UL scheduler



[PR770180] averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet > 0 for the given scheduler. [End PR770180]

  * [Before PR770180] avgCs1Size < cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdDL for given DL scheduler OR avgCs1Size < cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdUL for given UL Scheduler



[PR770180] averageCs1ListMaxSize < cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdDL for a given DL scheduler OR averageCs1ListMaxSize < cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdUL for a given UL scheduler. [End PR770180]

  * IF (actSchedFairnessUlOlc(5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = True or given scheduler is DL scheduler )



[Before PR770180] when rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc (5G_L2_7048_replaced([11213384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj2vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is above defined threshold maxNumFdmUesForHighLoad for given Scheduler

[PR770180] averageRrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc is above the defined threshold maxNumFdmUesForHighLoad for the given scheduler [End PR770180]

ELSE

[Before PR770180] when avgCs1Size is above defined threshold maxNumFdmUesForHighLoad for UL scheduler 

[PR770180] averageCs1ListMaxSize is above the defined threshold maxNumFdmUesForHighLoad for the UL scheduler. [End PR770180]

  * IF (actSchedFairnessUlOlc(5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = FALSE)



[Before PR770180] numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUL (5G_L2_378_replaced([11151479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24ifmPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) >= avgCs1Size for given UL scheduler or

numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL (5G_L2_226_replaced([11147731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NIYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) >= avgCs1Size for given DL scheduler

[PR770180] averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet > averageCs1ListMaxSize for the given scheduler. [End PR770180]

Once Degraded Moderate load is detected for a Scheduler , the share is calculated as specified in 5G_UP_ALG_18051_replaced([11216380](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxZJcPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),5G_L2_12724_replaced([11214052](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-wcUvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[PR770180]

  * averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet, averageCs1ListMaxSize and averageRrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc are defined in 5G_L2_19562_replaced([11213721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAGvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).



[End PR770180]

###### 2.14.5.1.1.0-8 State Based Load Balancing Algorithm Nominal Load State (ID: 11214033)

**2.14.5.1.1.0-8.0-2**  (ID: `11214045`)

State Based Load Balancing Algorithm [Before PR770180] For avgCs1Size see 5G_L2_1832_replaced([11212613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrWfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End PR770180]

Nominal Load is determined for a given scheduler when the following conditions are true:

  * [Before CB012716-A] rdEnableOLCforNScheduler (5G_L2_12274_replaced([11190587](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28X2tfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = True [End CB012716-A]
  * [Before PR770180] The numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL (5G_L2_226_replaced([11147731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NIYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for DL scheduler or numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUL (5G_L2_378_replaced([11151479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24ifmPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for UL scheduler > 0



[PR770180] averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet > 0 for the given scheduler. [End PR770180]

  * IF (actSchedFairnessUlOlc(5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = FALSE)



[Before PR770180] numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUL (5G_L2_378_replaced([11151479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24ifmPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) < avgCs1Size on UL for given UL scheduler or

numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL (5G_L2_226_replaced([11147731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NIYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) < avgCs1Size on DL for given DL scheduler

[PR770180] (averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet < averageCs1ListMaxSize for the given scheduler.) [End PR770180]

OR

[Before PR770180] avgCs1Size > cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdDL (5G_L2_5845_replaced([11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for given DL scheduler or avgCs1Size > cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdUL (5G_L2_5845_replaced([11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for given UL scheduler

[PR770180] (averageCs1ListMaxSize > cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdDL (5G_L2_5845_replaced([11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for a given DL scheduler or averageCs1ListMaxSize > cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdUL (5G_L2_5845_replaced([11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for a given UL scheduler.) [End PR770180]

  * IF (actSchedFairnessUlOlc(5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = TRUE)



[Before PR770180] avgCs1Size > cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdUL (5G_L2_5845_replaced([11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for given UL scheduler or

avgCs1Size > cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdDL (5G_L2_5845_replaced([11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for given DL scheduler

[PR770180] averageCs1ListMaxSize > cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdUL (5G_L2_5845_replaced([11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for given a UL scheduler or

averageCs1ListMaxSize > cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdDL (5G_L2_5845_replaced([11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for a given DL scheduler. [End PR770180]

Once nominal load is detected for a Scheduler , the share is calculated as specified in 5G_UP_ALG_18051_replaced([11216380](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxZJcPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) , 5G_L2_12724_replaced([11214052](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-wcUvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[PR770180]

  * averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet, averageCs1ListMaxSize and averageRrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc are defined in 5G_L2_19562_replaced([11213721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAGvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).



[End PR770180]

###### 2.14.5.1.1.0-9 State Based Load Balancing Algorithm Calculation of Share based on overallLoadCondition of all schedulers (DL &amp; UL) on core (ID: 11214052)

**2.14.5.1.1.0-9.0-3**  (ID: `11214074`)

State Based Load Balancing Algorithm This requirement is to support the implementation of algorithm in 5G_UP_ALG_18051_replaced([11216380](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxZJcPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) .

OverallLoadCondition is the aggregated load state of all the schedulers executed on a core.

For throttlingStep see 5G_L2_5845_replaced([11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[Before PR770180] For numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL see 5G_L2_226_replaced([11147731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NIYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) , numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUL see 5G_L2_378_replaced([11151479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24ifmPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End PR770180]

[Before PR770180] For maxCs2Size see 5G_L2_7049_replaced([11213344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj0_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End PR770180]

[Before PR770180] For rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc see 5G_L2_7048_replaced([11213384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj2vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End PR770180]

For defaultRatio see 5G_L2_5841_replaced([11213804](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-unKfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

For slotAwareOptimalRatio see 5G_L2_5845_replaced([11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[Before PR770180] For avgCs1Size see 5G_L2_1832_replaced([11212613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrWfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End PR770180]

For MinSingleSchedShare, MaxSingleSchedShare see 5G_L2_5852_replaced([11214158](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-xDYvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[PR744122] For avgSlotProcessingTime see 5G_L2_1870_replaced([11213602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-tZA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End PR744122]

[PR744122] For slotProcessingRatio see 5G_L2_15692_replaced([11212528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mESvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End PR744122]

[PR770180] For averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet, averageCs1ListMaxSize, averageCs2ListMaxSize and averageRrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc see 5G_L2_19562_replaced([11213721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAGvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End PR770180]

The decrement and increment of slotAwareOptimalRatio is always done for a pair of schedulers on the same core.

IF [Before PR770180] avgCs1Size [PR770180] averageCs1ListMaxSize [End PR770180] = 1 for a given scheduler, then the scheduler's slotAwareOptimalRatio shall not be decreased further.

[PR744122] IF (avgSlotProcessingTime > slotAwareOptimalRatio * slotProcessingRatio * slotDuration) THEN

5G-L2-PS shall not decrease the scheduler's slotAwareOptimalRatio any further.

Note: In a stable operating point, a scheduler's avgSlotProcessingTime doesn't exceed the time budget given by its slotAwareOptimalRatio. When a scheduler exceeds its budget it is likely too loaded to obey to the limit given by slotAwareOptimalRatio. In such a situation it doesn't make sense to reduce the scheduler's budget any further as the scheduler is going to exceed it constantly.

Note: In this requirement, slotAwareOptimalRatio is assumed to be in the range [0.0 ... 1.0] and the sum of the slotAwareOptimalRatio values of all schedulers running on the core is assumed to be 1.0. [End PR744122]

The decrement and increment of slotAwareOptimalRatio is always done for schedulers such that their slotAwareOptimalRatio is within the limits of MinSingleSchedShare and MaxSingleSchedShare.

[Before PR770180] Note: For DL scheduler, the rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc is always computed as in 5G_L2_7048_replaced([11213384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj2vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) , the maxCs2Size is always computed as in 5G_L2_7049_replaced([11213344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj0_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End PR770180]

All schedulers in 'Low Load State' :

overallLoadCondition = allLowLoad

Under low load state share ratio should trend to default value.

For each scheduler

Calculate the deviation of slotAwareOptimalRatio and defaultRatio

slotRatioDeviationFromDefault = slotAwareOptimalRatio - defaultRatio

Order the schedulers according to the slotRatioDeviationFromDefault from lowest to highest.

If highest value of ordered slotRatioDeviationFromDefault is a positive value (i.e slotAwareOptimalRatio > defaultRatio) AND lowest value of ordered slotRatioDeviationFromDefault is negative (i.e slotAwareOptimalRatio < defaultRatio) then

slotAwareOptimalRatio += throttlingStep , for scheduler with lowest slotRatioDeviationFromDefault

slotAwareOptimalRatio -= throttlingStep , for scheduler with highest slotRatioDeviationFromDefault

Else

No change in slotAwareOptimalRatio

All Scheduler in 'Low Load' or 'Nominal Load'

overallLoadCondition = allLowNominalLoad

For each scheduler

No change in slotAwareOptimalRatio

All Scheduler in mix of Load States : 'Low Load', 'Nominal Load', 'Degraded Moderate Load' ,'Degraded High Load'

Refer to 5G_L2_13024_replaced([11214083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-wcVvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

All Scheduler in 'Degraded Moderate Load' or 'Degraded High Load'

Refer to 5G_L2_13024_replaced([11214083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-wcVvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

All Scheduler in 'Degraded Moderate Load'

overallLoadCondition = allDegModLoad

For each scheduler

calculate the ratio degradedModerateLoadCompareRatio:

IF UL Scheduler,

IF actSchedFairnessUlOlc(5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = false

[Before PR770180] degradedModerateLoadCompareRatio = avgCs1Size / numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUL

[PR770180] degradedModerateLoadCompareRatio = averageCs1ListMaxSize / averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet [End PR770180]

ELSE

[Before PR770180] degradedModerateLoadCompareRatio = maxCs2Size / numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUL

[PR770180] degradedModerateLoadCompareRatio = averageCs2ListMaxSize / averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet [End PR770180]

IF DL Scheduler,

[Before PR770180] degradedModerateLoadCompareRatio = maxCs2Size / numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL

[PR770180] degradedModerateLoadCompareRatio = averageCs2ListMaxSize / averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet [End PR770180]

List the schedulers according to the value of degradedModerateLoadCompareRatio.

slotAwareOptimalRatio += throttlingStep , for scheduler with lowest degradedModerateLoadCompareRatio

slotAwareOptimalRatio -= throttlingStep , for scheduler with highest degradedModerateLoadCompareRatio

All Scheduler in 'Degraded High Load'

overallLoadCondition = allDegHighLoad

For each scheduler

calculate the ratio degradedHighLoadCompareRatio:

IF UL Scheduler,

IF actSchedFairnessUlOlc(5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = false

[Before PR770180] degradedHighLoadCompareRatio = avgCs1Size / numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUL

[PR770180] degradedHighLoadCompareRatio = averageCs1ListMaxSize / averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet [End PR770180]

ELSE

[Before PR770180] degradedHighLoadCompareRatio = rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc / numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUL

[PR770180] degradedHighLoadCompareRatio = averageRrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc / averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet [End PR770180]

IF DL Scheduler,

[Before PR770180] degradedHighLoadCompareRatio = rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc / numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL

[PR770180] degradedHighLoadCompareRatio = averageRrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc / averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet [End PR770180]

List the schedulers according to the value of degradedHighLoadCompareRatio.

slotAwareOptimalRatio += throttlingStep , for scheduler with lowest degradedHighLoadCompareRatio

slotAwareOptimalRatio -= throttlingStep , for scheduler with highest degradedHighLoadCompareRatio

In such a situation it doesn't make sense to reduce the scheduler's budget any further as the scheduler is going to exceed it constantly.

All Scheduler in mix of Load States : 'Low Load', 'Nominal Load', 'Degraded Moderate Load' ,'Degraded High Load'

For each scheduler in 'Low Load' or 'Nominal Load'

If the decrement of slotAwareOptimalRatio is not possible for a scheduler (based on the check for MinSingleSchedShare ) remove the scheduler from the overallLoadCondition handling.

If there are no schedulers from whom decrement of slotAwareOptimalRatio is possible consider the overallLoadCondition as allDegHighDegModLoad or allDegModLoad or allDegHighLoad based on the load state of the other schedulers.

If any scheduler in 'Low Load' state

slotAwareOptimalRatio -= throttlingStep,For scheduler with with 'Low Load' state and highest slotAwareOptimalRatio

else

slotAwareOptimalRatio -= throttlingStep,For scheduler with with 'Nominal Load' state and highest slotAwareOptimalRatio

If there are no scheduler from whom increment of slotAwareOptimalRatio is possible consider the overallLoadCondition as allLowNominalLoad or allLowLoad based on the load state of the other scheduler.

For each scheduler in 'Degraded High Load'

calculate the ratio degradedHighLoadCompareRatio:

IF UL Scheduler, 

IF actSchedFairnessUlOlc(5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = false

[PR770180] degradedHighLoadCompareRatio = averageCs1ListMaxSize / averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet [End PR770180]

ELSE

[PR770180] degradedHighLoadCompareRatio = averageRrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc / averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet [End PR770180]

IF DL Scheduler,

[Before PR770180] degradedHighLoadCompareRatio = rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc / numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL

[PR770180] degradedHighLoadCompareRatio = averageRrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc / averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet [End PR770180]

List the schedulers according to the value of degradedHighLoadCompareRatio

calculate the ratio degradedModerateLoadCompareRatio:

IF UL Scheduler ,

IF actSchedFairnessUlOlc(5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = false

[PR770180] degradedModerateLoadCompareRatio = averageCs1ListMaxSize / averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet [End PR770180]

ELSE

[Before PR770180] degradedModerateLoadCompareRatio = maxCs2Size / numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUL

[PR770180] degradedModerateLoadCompareRatio = averageCs2ListMaxSize / averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet [End PR770180]

IF DL Scheduler ,

[Before PR770180] degradedModerateLoadCompareRatio = maxCs2Size / numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL

[PR770180] degradedModerateLoadCompareRatio = averageCs2ListMaxSize / averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet [End PR770180]

List the schedulers according to the value of degradedModerateLoadCompareRatio

If list of schedulers with 'Degraded High Load' is not empty

slotAwareOptimalRatio += throttlingStep, for scheduler with highest degradedHighLoadCompareRatio

Else

If list of shedulers with 'Degraded Moderate Load' is not empty

slotAwareOptimalRatio += throttlingStep, for scheduler with highest degradedModerateLoadCompareRatio

overallLoadCondition = allDegHighDegModLoad

IF DL Scheduler,

[Before PR770180] degradedHighLoadCompareRatio = avgCs1Size / numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUL

[PR770180] degradedHighLoadCompareRatio = averageCs1ListMaxSize / averageNumOfUesInPreSchedCandSet [End PR770180]

###### 2.14.5.1.1.0-11 State Based Load Balancing Algorithm Calculation of share when both DL and UL number of UEs in the pre-scheduler candidate lists are greater than 0 (ID: 11214115)

**2.14.5.1.1.0-11.0-2**  (ID: `12776383`)

State Based Load Balancing Algorithm For [Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size [CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive [End CNI-136895-A] see see 5G_L2_1832_replaced([11212613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrWfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

For cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdDL, cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdUL, throttlingStep see 5G_L2_5845_replaced([11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[Before CNI-136895-A] 

IF ( (avgCs1Size on DL > cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdDL) AND (avgCs1Size on UL > cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdUL) )

avgCs1Size on DL and UL is still above 90% of maximum number.

Keep current ratio as both schedulers are not limited by preventive control

[CNI-136895-A] 

IF ( (cs1ListMaxSizePreventive on DL > cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdDL) AND (cs1ListMaxSizePreventive on UL > cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdUL) )

cs1ListMaxSizePreventive on DL and UL is still above 90% of maximum number.

Keep current ratio as both schedulers are not limited by preventive control

[End CNI-136895-A]

ELSE IF ([Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size [CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive [End CNI-136895-A] on DL > cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdDL)

DL is not limited so we can decrease its share

slotAwareOptimalRatio -= throttlingStep

ELSE IF ([Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size [CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive [End CNI-136895-A] on UL > cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdUL)

UL is not limited so we can decrease its share

slotAwareOptimalRatio += throttlingStep

ELSE

Both DL and UL is beeing limited

In High Load state calculate ratio as described in 5G_L2_7905_replaced([11213968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-v1RfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

In Moderate load state calculate as described in 5G_L2_7481_replaced([11214126](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-wcaPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

END

###### 2.14.5.1.1.0-12 State Based Load Balancing Algorithm Caclulation of share based on number of UEs in the pre-scheduler candidate lists and CS2 lists (ID: 11214126)

**2.14.5.1.1.0-12.0-3**  (ID: `12776488`)

State Based Load Balancing Algorithm When number of [Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size [CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive [End CNI-136895-A] on DL and UL are limited below cs1ListNotLimitedThreshold (5G_L2_5845_replaced([11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) by reduction of [Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size [CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive [End CNI-136895-A] (see 5G_L2_1832_replaced([11212613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrWfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), we try to even ratio of CS1 UEs as follows:

For throttlingStep see 5G_L2_5845_replaced([11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

csListRatioDL = maxCs2Size (5G_L2_7049_replaced([11213344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj0_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) on DL / numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL (5G_L2_226_replaced([11147731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NIYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

IF (actSchedFairnessUlOlc(see 5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = TRUE)

csListRatioUL = maxCs2Size (5G_L2_7049_replaced([11213344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj0_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) on UL / numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUL (5G_L2_378_replaced([11151479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24ifmPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

ELSE

csListRatioUL = [Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size [CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive [End CNI-136895-A] (5G_L2_1832_replaced([11212613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrWfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) on UL / numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUL (5G_L2_378_replaced([11151479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24ifmPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

IF (csListRatioDL < csListRatioUL)

Ratio for DL is smaller so give more time to DL

slotAwareOptimalRatio += throttlingStep

ELSE IF (csListRatioDL > csListRatioUL)

Ratio for UL is smaller so give more time to UL

slotAwareOptimalRatio -= throttlingStep

END

---

###### 2.14.5.1.1.0-13 State Based Load Balancing Algorithm Calculation of share when one of DL or UL number of UEs in the pre-scheduler candidate lists is grather that 0 (ID: 11214145)

**2.14.5.1.1.0-13.0-2**  (ID: `12776498`)

State Based Load Balancing Algorithm For [Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size [CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive [End CNI-136895-A] see 5G_L2_1832_replaced([11212613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrWfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

For cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdDL, cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdUL, throttlingStep see 5G_L2_5845_replaced([11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

IF ( (numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL (5G_L2_226_replaced([11147731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NIYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) == 0) AND ([Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size [CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive [End CNI-136895-A] on UL <= cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdUL) )

Here there is no DL and UL is limited by preventive control so we give more time to UL

slotAwareOptimalRatio -= throttlingStep

ELSE IF ( (numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetUL (5G_L2_378_replaced([11151479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24ifmPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) == 0) AND ([Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size [CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive [End CNI-136895-A] on DL <= cs1ListNotLimitedThresholdDL) )

Here there is no UL and DL is limited by preventive control so we give more time to DL

slotAwareOptimalRatio += throttlingStep

END

##### 2.14.5.1.2 Stateless Load Balancing Algorithm

###### 2.14.5.1.2.0-1 Stateless Load Balancing Algorithm Dynamic allocation of processing budget among schedulers (ID: 12823011)

**2.14.5.1.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12823012`)

Stateless Load Balancing Algorithm 5G-L2-PS shall dynamically calculate slotAwareOptimalRatio between schedulers placed on same core, following below principles:

  * slotAwareOptimalRatio is **scheduler specific for each DL and UL scheduler.**
  * slotAwareOptimalRatio value for each DL and UL schedulers are calculated individually.
  * dynamic calculation works only with FDM scheduling enabled.
  * When actStatelessSchedLoadBalancer is set to 1, stateless load balancing is enabled which redistributes the processing share among the (DL/UL) schedulers based on the metric defined in [12572228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_8nUmUC8jEfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg). [PR847189] The processing share redistribution among scheduler shall fulfil the minimum share allocated per scheduler as defined in [12792665](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tB8F85U2EfC7Wp-sWxcfJw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tB8F85U2EfC7Wp-sWxcfJw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9"). [End PR847189]
  * Calculated slotAwareOptimalRatio are clipped to maximum and minimum values defined in [11214158](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-xDYvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).



Following constants are defined for Stateless load balancer:

  * Algorithm starts with defaultRatio as defined in [11213804](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-unKfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  * Adjustment size of processing share among schedulers is equal to rdThrottlingStep ([11190548](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28XPrvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * If the difference between of highest schedRatio (evaluated using [12572228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_8nUmUC8jEfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg)) of scheduler to the lowest schedRatio is less than rdSchedRatioThreshold ([12591175](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_Eis28DbDEfCKaNlcHOQWmg)), then processing share among the scheduler will not be adjusted.
  * The processing share adjustment shall occur on load types with more than one scheduler. Load types is defined in [11212562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9")



The slotAwareOptimalRatio of each scheduler shall be throttled up or down depending upon schedRatio (evaluated as defined [12572228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_8nUmUC8jEfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg)) of the schedulers deployed on the core. Refer [12572973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_cg6a0C80EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_cg6a0C80EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9") and [12823017](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2173oKoTEfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2173oKoTEfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9") for details on how load balancing is performed.

---

###### 2.14.5.1.2.0-2 Stateless Load Balancing Algorithm Calculation of Share based in schedRatio (ID: 12823017)

**2.14.5.1.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12823018`)

Stateless Load Balancing Algorithm This requirement is to support the implementation of the algorithm defined in [12572973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_cg6a0C80EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_cg6a0C80EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").

Following constants are used in stateless load balancer:

  * throttlingStep is defined in [11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  * defaultRatio is defined in [11213804](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-unKfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  * slotAwareOptimalRatio is defined in [11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  * MinSingleSchedShare and MaxSingleSchedShare are defined in [11214158](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-xDYvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).



Constraints on stateless load balancing:

  * Adjustments (increment/decrement) to slotAwareOptimalRatio are always performed for a pair of schedulers deployed on the same core.
  * The decrement/increment of slotAwareOptimalRatio is only applied to schedulers whose slotAwareOptimalRatio values remain within the limits defined by MinSingleSchedShare and MaxSingleSchedShare.
  * 5G-L2-PS shall not increase a scheduler’s slotAwareOptimalRatio if the condition specified in [12572973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_cg6a0C80EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_cg6a0C80EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9") is met.
  * Load balancing based on schedRatio is skipped, if the difference between highest schedRatio and lowest schedRatio is less than rdSchedRatioThreshold ([12591175](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_Eis28DbDEfCKaNlcHOQWmg)).
  * [PR847189]Load sharing based on schedRatio is executed only when all schedulers on the core satisfy the conditions defined in [12792665](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tB8F85U2EfC7Wp-sWxcfJw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tB8F85U2EfC7Wp-sWxcfJw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9"), which ensures the minimum processing share is allocated to scheduler to at-least schedule one UE. If these conditions are not met, load balancing based on schedRatio is skipped. [End PR847189]



[Before PR853954]

Load balancing based on schedRatio:

  * slotAwareOptimalRatio += throttlingStep, for scheduler with the lowest schedRatio.
  * slotAwareOptimalRatio -= throttlingStep, for scheduler with the highest schedRatio.



[PR853954]

#### Overview of Stateless Load Balancing Steps:

If there are more than one schedulers (DL/UL) are placed on the same core, for which scheduling will be performed in the current slot, then following steps shall be performed.

###### Step 1: Initialization of Scheduler Lists at the Start of Each Slot

5G-L2-PS creates three lists:

"toBeIncreased": Contains schedulers with allocated processing share below the dynamic minimum (refer [12792665](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tB8F85U2EfC7Wp-sWxcfJw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tB8F85U2EfC7Wp-sWxcfJw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9")).  
"toBeDecreased": Contains schedulers with allocated processing share above the dynamic maximum (refer [12882289](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NG3A8LRlEfCQT7hYUxERAg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NG3A8LRlEfCQT7hYUxERAg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9")).  
"toBeLoadBalanced": Includes all remaining schedulers not present in the above two lists.

Note: Each scheduler on the same core must be assigned to one of the above lists. A scheduler cannot appear in more than one list.

###### Step 2: Load Balancing for "toBeIncreased" List

IF "toBeIncreased" is not empty:

Select the scheduler with the lowest slotAwareOptimalRatio from "toBeIncreased" to increase its ratio.

For decreasing slotAwareOptimalRatio, choose scheduler:

IF "toBeDecreased" is not empty: 

Select the scheduler with the highest slotAwareOptimalRatio from "toBeDecreased" list.

ELSE IF "toBeLoadBalanced" is not empty:

Select the scheduler with the highest schedRatio from "toBeLoadBalanced" list.

ELSE

If neither list has entries, no load balancing is performed in this slot.

Proceed to Step 5.

ELSE // "toBeIncreased" is empty

Proceed to Step 3.

###### Step 3: Load Balancing for "toBeDecreased" List

IF "toBeDecreased" is not empty:

IF "toBeLoadBalanced" is not empty:

Select the scheduler with the lowest schedRatio from "toBeLoadBalanced" list to increase its slotAwareOptimalRatio.

Select the scheduler with the highest slotAwareOptimalRatio from "toBeDecreased" list to decrease its slotAwareOptimalRatio.

ELSE // "toBeLoadBalanced" is empty

Select the scheduler with the lowest schedDiff from "toBeDecreased" to increase its slotAwareOptimalRatio.

Select the scheduler with the highest schedDiff from "toBeDecreased" to decrease its slotAwareOptimalRatio.

Proceed to Step 5.

ELSE // "toBeDecreased" is empty

Proceed to Step 4.

###### Step 4: Load Balancing for "toBeLoadBalanced" List

Select the scheduler with the lowest schedRatio from "toBeLoadBalanced" list to increase its slotAwareOptimalRatio.

Select the scheduler with the highest schedRatio from "toBeLoadBalanced" list to increase its slotAwareOptimalRatio.

Proceed to Step 5.

###### Step 5: Load balancing

slotAwareOptimalRatio += throttlingStep, for the scheduler selected for increase.  
slotAwareOptimalRatio -= throttlingStep, for the scheduler selected for decrease.

[End PR853954]

Notes:

  * slotAwareOptimalRatio is assumed to be within the range [0.0, 1.0].
  * The sum of slotAwareOptimalRatio values for all schedulers on a given core is assumed to be 1.0.
  * schedRatio is defined in [12572228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_8nUmUC8jEfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg).
  * [PR853954] schedDiff computation is specified in [12882299](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_4oHvEbRoEfCQT7hYUxERAg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_4oHvEbRoEfCQT7hYUxERAg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").[End PR853954]

---

###### 2.14.5.1.2.0-3 Stateless Load Balancing Algorithm Dynamic minimum of single scheduler share with stateless load balancer (ID: 12792665)

**2.14.5.1.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12792666`)

Stateless Load Balancing Algorithm When actStatelessSchedLoadBalancer is enabled, then the following condition applies:

5G-L2-PS shall check if the scheduler share allocated for each scheduler deployed on the core satisfy below criteria:

slotProcessingDurationBudget * slotAwareOptimalRatio > avgPureSchedulingTimeForSingleUe

**[PR851749]**

OR

rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc >= 2

**[End PR851749]**

where, slotProcessingDurationBudget refers to the time allocated for scheduling within the current slot, calculated based on slotProcessingRatio.

If this condition is not met, **[Before PR853954]slotAwareOptimalRatio is incremented by the value of throttlingSteps.**

i.e.: slotAwareOptimalRatio = slotAwareOptimalRatio + throttlingStep;

The above adjustment shall be performed only once per slot.

**[PR853954] then such schedulers are added to "toBeIncreased" list.**[End PR853954]****

Note:

  * **[Before PR853954]throttlingStep is defined in[11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).**[End PR853954]****
  * slotAwareOptimalRatio is defined in [11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  * slotProcessingRatio is defined in [11212528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mESvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  * avgPureSchedulingTimeForSingleUe is defined in [12792298](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_MsN7EJSiEfCoxNjZXyLbRA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_MsN7EJSiEfCoxNjZXyLbRA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").
  * **[PR851749]rrmMaxNumUesFdmOlc is the target FD UEs per slot, defined in[11213384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj2vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). **[End PR851749]****
  * **[PR853954]"toBeIncreased" list is defined in[12823017](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2173oKoTEfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2173oKoTEfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9"). **[End PR853954]****

---

###### 2.14.5.1.2.0-4 Stateless Load Balancing Algorithm Dynamic maximum of single scheduler share with stateless load balancer (ID: 12882289)

**2.14.5.1.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12882290`)

Stateless Load Balancing Algorithm When actStatelessSchedLoadBalancer is enabled, then the following condition applies:

5G-L2-PS shall check if the scheduler share allocated for each scheduler deployed on the core satisfy below criteria:

slotProcessingDurationBudget * slotAwareOptimalRatio > avgPureSchedulingTimeForMaxSched

OR

slotAwareOptimalRatio + throttlingStep > MaxSingleSchedShare

where, slotProcessingDurationBudget refers to the time allocated for scheduling within the current slot, calculated based on slotProcessingRatio.

If this condition is met, then such schedulers are added to "toBeDecreased" list.

**[Before PR873363] [PR868538] If the avgRemainingSchedulingBudget exceeds the configured threshold rdAvgRemainingBudgetThresholdForLoadBalancing_Us, than the scheduler is added to the "toBeDecreased" list.**[End PR868538]****

**[PR873363]**

If the percentage of scheduling slots with a remaining budget value (percentageSlotsWithTooHighRemainingBudget) above the threshold(rdRemainingBudgetThresholdForLoadBalancing_Us) is greater than highRemainingBudgetPercentageThreshold, than the scheduler is added to the "toBeDecreased" list.

i.e.: percentageSlotsWithTooHighRemainingBudget > highRemainingBudgetPercentageThreshold

where,

highRemainingBudgetPercentageThreshold is equal to 59.

Note: This metric reflects consistent underutilization of the scheduler’s allocated budget and indicates that the scheduler does not need as much budget as it is currently allocated.

**[End PR873363]**

Note:

  * throttlingStep is defined in [11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  * slotAwareOptimalRatio is defined in [11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  * slotProcessingRatio is defined in [11212528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mESvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  * avgPureSchedulingTimeForMaxSched is defined in [12792298](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_MsN7EJSiEfCoxNjZXyLbRA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_MsN7EJSiEfCoxNjZXyLbRA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").
  * "toBeDecreased" list is defined in [12823017](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2173oKoTEfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2173oKoTEfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").
  * MaxSingleSchedShare are defined in [11214158](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-xDYvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  * **[Before PR873363] [PR868538] avgRemainingSchedulingBudget is defined in[11213721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAGvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAGvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9"). **[End PR868538][End PR873363]****
  * **[PR868538] rdRemainingBudgetThresholdForLoadBalancing_Us is defined in[13379557](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Q_4QZ_3kEfCPDo8cGBoqIw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Q_4QZ_3kEfCPDo8cGBoqIw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").**[End PR868538]****
  * **[PR873363]percentageSlotsWithTooHighRemainingBudget is defined in[11213721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAGvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAGvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").**[End PR873363]****

---

###### 2.14.5.1.2.0-5 Stateless Load Balancing Algorithm Redistribution of Processing Budget for Schedulers Above Dynamic Maximum. (ID: 12882299)

**2.14.5.1.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `12882300`)

Stateless Load Balancing Algorithm This requirement specifies the process for redistributing the processing budget of schedulers whose slotAwareOptimalRatio exceeds the dynamic maximum. The steps below are applied only when all schedulers on the same core have processing budgets exceeding the dynamic maximum.

[Before PR878826]

[PR873363]

The below redistribution procedure applies only when at least one scheduler on the same core does NOT satisfy condition

percentageSlotsWithTooHighRemainingBudget > highRemainingBudgetPercentageThreshold

[End PR873363]

[End PR878826]

  1. Compute Expected Share: 

For each scheduler i: 




[image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is: $$ \text{expectedShare}_i = \frac{\text{avgPureSchedulingTimeForMaxSched}_i}{\sum_{j=1}^{n} \text{avgPureSchedulingTimeForMaxSched}_j} $$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/a12c4cc8-f901-4f23-adf4-763b5238e301.png[/image_path][/image-0]

where,  
expectedShare represents the ratio of the average processing budget (avgPureSchedulingTimeForMaxSched) required by scheduler i compared to the total average processing budget required by all schedulers on the same core. 2\. Calculate shareDiff: 
    
    
    For each scheduler i:
    

[image-1][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in black text on a white background. The equation is: `shareDiffᵢ = slotAwareOptimalRatioᵢ - expectedShareᵢ`[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/89d8573b-8778-409c-8824-ebc9cc7856a1.png[/image_path][/image-1] 
    
    
    where,
    

shareDiff represents the difference between the allocated processing budget(slotAwareOptimalRatio) and the ratio required processing budget (expectedShare).

Load balancing is performed based on the shareDiff metric as defined in [12823017](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2173oKoTEfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2173oKoTEfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").

[Before PR878826]

[PR873363]

If all scheduler on the same core does satisfy below condition:

percentageSlotsWithTooHighRemainingBudget > highRemainingBudgetPercentageThreshold

Then each scheduler’s normalized remaining budget is evaluated using the metric relativeRemainingSchedulerBudget, computed as:

For each scheduler i:

[image-2][image_desc]relativeRemainingSchedulerBudget$_{i}$ = $\frac{\text{avgRemainingSchedulerBudget}_{i}}{\text{slotAwareOptimalRatio}_{i}}$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/relativeRemainingSchedulerBudget_Formaula.png[/image_path][/image-2]

where,  
avgRemainingSchedulerBudget is the average of remainingSchedulingBudget over the sliding‑window length.  
slotAwareOptimalRatio is the scheduler’s currently assigned share.

Load balancing is performed by redistributing budget from scheduler with highest relativeRemainingSchedulerBudget to the scheduler with smallest relativeRemainingSchedulerBudget, as defined in [12823017](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2173oKoTEfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2173oKoTEfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").

[End PR873363]

[End PR878826]

Note:

  * slotAwareOptimalRatio is defined in [11213879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-vONfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  * avgPureSchedulingTimeForMaxSched is defined in [12792298](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_MsN7EJSiEfCoxNjZXyLbRA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_MsN7EJSiEfCoxNjZXyLbRA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").
  * dynamic maximum is defined in [12882289](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NG3A8LRlEfCQT7hYUxERAg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NG3A8LRlEfCQT7hYUxERAg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").
  * [Before PR878826] [PR873363] avgRemainingSchedulerBudget is defined in [11213721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAGvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAGvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").[End PR873363] [End PR878826]

---

## 2.14.6 SRS Overload Control

### 2.14.6.0-1 SRS Overload Control Overview (ID: 11214197)

**2.14.6.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `13452872`)

SRS Overload Control Overview

[CB015122-A]5G-L2-PS shall not create the PS-SRSBM EO when actSrsBmCalcInL1 is set to True (see [13431287](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_99L1aB4KEfG9L99MQBns2Q)). The DFT beam selection algorithm is moved to 5G-L1-DU (see [11153567](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_SqaksPvMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). 5G-L2-PS shall apply SRS overload control requirements only if actSrsBmCalcInL1 is set to False.[End CB015122-A]

SRS EO (Execution object) is deployed in the same core as UL and DL scheduler EO. Therefore the need to limit the time for SRS processing of CoMa for many UE's and limit the time for Beam Selection to a certain timebox value and save CPU processing resources:

  1. To avoid to process the outdated periodic SRS measurements by discarding of aged messages of _UlData_SrsReceiveRespBmPs ._
  2. To aviod to process the unnecessary periodic osDFT beam calculation for UEs that have been a long time without any DRB data in buffer, or UE is FWA UE with channel condition does not changes much by skipping part of their SRS BM measurement and Beam selection (refer 5G_L2_21703_replaced([11155566](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_245r-vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).



SRS processing does not impact the functioning of higher priority RT scheduling (DL and UL EO). 

The processing of SRS EO shall be controlled by the rdSrsProcessingControl (5G_L2_10225_replaced([11183873](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27nBwPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The parameter shall be used to control the following:

  * SRS EO Triggering Event (Refer 5G_L2_10228_replaced([11214253](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-xqcvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * Fragment handling of ULData_SrsReceiveRespBmPs processing and Beam Selection (Refer 5G_L2_10230_replaced([11214267](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-xqdPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * Scalar multiplier for DL Beam Selection timer used in conjunction with rdDlBeamSelectTimer (5G_L2_5821_replaced([11183859](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27nBt_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * Delay Counter Threshold for SRS EO overload Detection (Refer 5G_L2_10234_replaced([11214292](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-xqePvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * Scalar multiplier for count of Ues' to be moved to **SRS_DL_BM_AGED state. (Refer 5G_L2_10235_replaced([11214304](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-xqevvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**



Overload in SRS shall be detected when the periodic operation of SRS Beam Selection of an UE are delayed than the defined timer limit (Beam Selection Timer) . Such delay instance are counted and once the count exceeds the Count Threshold (5G_L2_10234_replaced([11214292](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-xqePvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) the SRS EO Overload state is changed

There are 3 Overload States of SRS EO 

SRS EO Normal

SRS EO Overload

SRS EO High Overload

The detection and action of each state are defined in 5G_L2_10211_replaced([11214317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-xqfPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_10214_replaced([11214331](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-xqfvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

### 2.14.6.0-2 SRS Overload Control SRS BM measurement Event (ID: 11214222)

**2.14.6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11214229`)

SRS Overload Control SRS BM Measurement Event outdate determination

---

**2.14.6.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11214234`)

SRS Overload Control [CNI-125153] When 5G-L2-PS receives covariance matrices from L1 via message UlData_SrsReceiveRespBmPs (5G_L1_257_replaced([11483775](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fDtHvPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), it shall store and process CoMa matrices.

Before storing and processing CoMa matrices, the age of SrsReceiveRespBmPs shall be evaludated , if aging, then event shall be discarded. if not aging, then continue process.

The age shall be determined by the

IF current_SFN < BmPs_SFN

age = (1024+current_SFN- BmPs_SFN)*20 + (current_slot - BmPs_slot)

ELSE 

age = (current_SFN- BmPs_SFN)*20 + (current_slot - BmPs_slot)

Note: 20 slots per SFN is for RF1 with SC30khz.

BmPs_SFN and BmPs_slot is SFN and slot in the message of UlData_SrsReceiveRespBmPs .

[End CNI-125153]

---

**2.14.6.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11214242`)

SRS Overload Control SRS BM Measurement Event disacrding

---

**2.14.6.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11214247`)

SRS Overload Control [CNI-125153] When 5G-L2-PS receives covariance matrices from L1 via message UlData_SrsReceiveRespBmPs (5G_L1_257_replaced([11483775](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fDtHvPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), it shall store and process CoMa matrices.

Before storing and process CoMa matrices, the age of SrsReceiveRespBmPs shall be evaludated first

For storing

If age > rdSrsResponseAging (5G_UP_ALG_28319_replaced([11158864](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktFRO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

current event and the events pending in FIFO queue shall all be discarded.

Else

curent event shall be stored in FIFO queue.

For processing

If age > rdSrsResponseAging (5G_UP_ALG_28319_replaced([11158864](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktFRO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

only currrent event shall all be discarded.

Else

current event shall be continue processing.

Note: SrsReceiveRespBmPs may contain several UEs CoMa information, and the RD counter is recorded based on event number rather UE. Pending event is disacrd in FIFO queue shall also be counted.

rdSrsResponseAging is supporting online modification.

[End CNI-125153]

---

### 2.14.6.0-3 SRS Overload Control SRS EO Triggering Event (ID: 11214253)

**2.14.6.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11214260`)

SRS Overload Control SRS EO Triggering Event

When 5G-L2-PS receives covariance matrices from L1 via message UlData_SrsReceiveRespBmPs (5G_L1_257_replaced([11483775](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fDtHvPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), it shall store and process CoMa matrices according to the below steps. See 5G_L2_6301_replaced([11154615](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_240zePvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 6302 about the state machine for Dl BM.

[Before CB009058-B] The processing of CoMa data as defined in 5G_L2_6566_replaced([11154651](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_240zfvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is done in Non UL slot based on the trigger SlotTypeInd Trigger [CB009058-B] SlotSynchroInd trigger as defined in 5G_L2_6488_replaced([11246670](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3CEPEPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is used to trigger the processing of CoMa as in 5G_L2_6566_replaced([11154651](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_240zfvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The Bit#0 of rdSrsProcessingControl is configured for usage of SlotSynchroInd to trigger CoMa processing [End CB009058-B]

### 2.14.6.0-4 SRS Overload Control Fragment handling of UlData_SrsReceiveRespBmPs and Beam Selection (ID: 11214267)

**2.14.6.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11214272`)

SRS Overload Control [CB009058-B]

Bit #1 of rdSrsProcessingControl (5G_L2_10225_replaced([11183873](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27nBwPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) controls the usage of fragment or timeboxed handling of SRS EO functionality ( 5G_L2_6486_replaced([11246643](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3CEPDPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ). Fragment message handling is confiured by default.

[End CB009058-B]

### 2.14.6.0-5 SRS Overload Control Extension of DL Beam Selection timer during SRS EO Overload (ID: 11214280)

**2.14.6.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `12519200`)

SRS Overload Control If SRS EO is detected to be in SRS EO Overload State (as in 5G_L2_10211_replaced([11214317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-xqfPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , the values of Bit #2-Bit#4 of rdSrsProcessingControl (5G_L2_10225_replaced([11183873](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27nBwPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is usage of extension multiplier of the timer rdDlBeamSelectTimer (5G_L2_5821_replaced([11183859](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27nBt_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

By default , SRS EO Overload state the value of rdDlBeamSelectTimer is doubled and used for Beam Selection.

[CB014465-B]If a static UE is set as isPeriodDoubledForSrs= TRUE and its beam selection timer is enlarged as [12488174: Extension of DL and UL Beam Selection timer if the SRS period is doubled](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NKmuYhBXEfCvOvZoOJBSnQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), its beam selection timer can't be changed further. And if the enlargement as [12488174: Extension of DL and UL Beam Selection timer if the SRS period is doubled](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NKmuYhBXEfCvOvZoOJBSnQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) recovers, the static UE with isPeriodDoubledForSrs= TRUE shall keep its beam selection timer doubled.[End CB014465-B]

### 2.14.6.0-6 SRS Overload Control Extension of DL and UL Beam Selection timer if the SRS period is doubled (ID: 12488174)

**2.14.6.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `12689738`)

SRS Overload Control If SRS EO is detected to be in SRS EO Overload State (as in 5G_L2_10211_replaced([11214317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-xqfPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , the values of Bit #2-Bit#4 of rdSrsProcessingControl (5G_L2_10225_replaced([11183873](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27nBwPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is usage of extension multiplier of the timer rdDlBeamSelectTimer (5G_L2_5821_replaced([11183859](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27nBt_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

By default , SRS EO Overload state the value of rdDlBeamSelectTimer is doubled and used for Beam Selection.

[CB014465-B]If a static UE is set as isPeriodDoubledForSrs= TRUE and without any AntennaSwitching SRS (see [10975309: srsConfig structure content](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeFfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), and and its beam selection timer is already enlarged as [12488174: Extension of DL and UL Beam Selection timer if the SRS period is doubled](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NKmuYhBXEfCvOvZoOJBSnQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), its beam selection timer can't be doubled further. And if the enlargement as [12488174: Extension of DL and UL Beam Selection timer if the SRS period is doubled](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NKmuYhBXEfCvOvZoOJBSnQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) recovers, the static UE with isPeriodDoubledForSrs= TRUE and without any AntennaSwitching SRS (see [10975309: srsConfig structure content](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeFfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) configured shall keep its beam selection timer doubled.[End CB014465-B]

### 2.14.6.0-7 SRS Overload Control Delay Counter Thresold for SRS EO Overload (ID: 11214292)

**2.14.6.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11214296`)

SRS Overload Control [CB009058-B]

Bit#5-Bit#8 of rdSrsProcessingControl (5G_L2_10225_replaced([11183873](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27nBwPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) provide the Consecutive Counter limit (default 10) to be counted when beam selection timer is exceeded for an UE during the periodic processing . Counted once per SlotSynchInd. Once this limit is reached the overload state of SRS EO is changed to the next higher Level (SRS EO Normal -> SRS EO Overload or SRS EO Overload -> SRS EO Highoverload)

[End CB009058-B]

### 2.14.6.0-8 SRS Overload Control Count of UE to be moved to SRS_DL_BM_AGED state during SRS EO High Overload (ID: 11214304)

**2.14.6.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11214312`)

SRS Overload Control [CB009058-B]

Bit#9-Bit#11 of rdSrsProcessingControl (5G_L2_10225_replaced([11183873](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27nBwPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) provide the scalar multiplier to be used together with rdLimitUeNumberPerSlot ( 5G_L2_5829_replaced([11183932](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27nBzPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to count the number of UE to be moved to SRS_DL_BM_AGED state as part of SRS EO High overload handlng. Default multiplier value is 7. A special value 0 for this multiplier shall inidcate that all the UE ready for Beam Selection shall be moved to SRS_DL_BM_AGED state.

[End CB009058-B]

### 2.14.6.0-9 SRS Overload Control SRS EO Congestion Detection (ID: 11214317)

**2.14.6.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11214323`)

SRS Overload Control Congestion States for SRS

[CB009058-B]

SRS EO Normal

Normal Operation of SRS . No change in the parameter setting for SRS

\- rdDlBeamSelectTimer (5G_L2_5821_replaced([11183859](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27nBt_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) used for DL Beam Selection

SRS EO Overload

Initial State : SRS EO Normal State

SRS EO Overload State is detected when Beam Selection processing for UE is delayed consecutively by rdSrsProcessingControl (5G_L2_10234_replaced([11214292](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-xqePvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) during each processing trigger of SlotSynchroInd

Action

\- Log and Change state to SRS EO Overload

SRS EO High Overload

Initial State : SRS EO Overload

SRS EO High Overload State is detected when Beam Selection processing using extended Beam Selection Timer ( 5G_L2_10231_replaced([11214280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-xqdvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for UE is delayed consecutively by rdSrsProcessingControl (5G_L2_10234_replaced([11214292](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-xqePvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) during each processing trigger of SlotSynchroInd

Action :

\- Log and Change state to SRS High Overload

[End CB009058-B]

### 2.14.6.0-10 SRS Overload Control SRS EO Congestion State Handling - Normal (ID: 11214331)

**2.14.6.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `11214334`)

SRS Overload Control SRS EO - Normal State

No Special handlng.

[End CB009058-B]

### 2.14.6.0-11 SRS Overload Control SRS EO Congestion State Handling - Overload (ID: 11214341)

**2.14.6.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `11214347`)

SRS Overload Control SRS EO - Overload State

Use Scaled DL Beam selection timer

Scaled value of DL Beam Selection timer ( rdDlBeamSelectTimer * rdSrsProcessingControl (5G_L2_10231_replaced([11214280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-xqdvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))))

[End CB009058-B]

### 2.14.6.0-12 SRS Overload Control SRS EO Congestion State Handling - High Overload (ID: 11214353)

**2.14.6.0-12.0-3**  (ID: `11214372`)

SRS Overload Control SRS EO - High Overload State

Move UE to SRS_DL_BM_AGED state . Number of UEs to be moved depend on rdSrsProcessingControl (5G_L2_10235_replaced([11214304](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-xqevvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) * rdLimitUeNumberPerSlot

Move to SRS EO Normal State

Note, [CB009527-A] Due to supporting SB SRS for SB BF, the names shall be replaced, but keep the habitual understanding, SBSRS is meaning of WB BF SRS , even it can be full BW SRS. WBSRS is meaning of SB BF SRS, even it can be sub-band SRS , see definition in 5G_L2_18130_replaced([11155228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2432wvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [ End CB009527-A]

for UE with TAS WBSRS configured, it's shall not be move to SRS_DL_BM_AGED status. Only UEs with SBSRS configured are move to SRS_DL_BM_AGED status.
