### 2.14.6.0-13 SRS Overload Control SRS EO Processing Time Control with Parallel Scheduling (ID: 12763104)

**2.14.6.0-13.0-1**  (ID: `12763105`)

SRS Overload Control If rdEnableDlFdSchOnULCores([12686252](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wQhl0VMfEfCnPp04H8v-AQ)) is set as 1, in loadTypeDlOnly slot, SRS EO processing time shall be controlled as below.

  1. Set allowed processing time for SRS EO when SlotSynchroInd is received to ensure DL FD scheduler can be started on time.



allowedNsCurrentSlotSrs = max(0, min(rdDlSrsReservedCpuUs, timeRemainForFdSchReq))  
where,

timeRemainForFdSchReq = DL avgPreAndTdTime - (Current Tsc - DL SlotSynchroInd Tsc)

  1. Sync up avgPreAndTdTime between TD/FD EO and SRS EO



At the end of DL FD scheduling, a new message SlotSynchroIndCont will be sent to SRS EO with avgPreAndTdTime and xsfn.

  1. Continue handling after DL FD 



SRS EO shall continue to handle SRS related tasks when SlotSynchroIndCont is received on SRS EO in the same slot(SlotSynchroIndCont.xsfn == Current xsfn), set allowedNsCurrentSlotSrs = min(rdDlSrsReservedCpuUs, timeTillSlotBoundaryNs) as Processing Time Control.

Note:

1) For the loadTypeMixed, the Processing Time Control is same as legacy.

2) avgPreAndTdTime shall be added in message FdScheduleReq if DL FD scheduler doesn't have it.

3) A new message UlToSrsSlotTypeSync is used to send SlotType from UL Eo to SRS Eo after cell setup.

---

## 2.14.7 Overload Protection

### 2.14.7.0-1 Overload Protection Overview (ID: 11214384)

**2.14.7.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11214398`)

Overload Protection **[Before CB013709-C] CNI-120418 introduces**[End CB013709-C] Overload Protection shall support “signaling overload” notification to 5G-CP-RT. When overload protection mechanism is enabled on the 5G-CP-RT side, it leads to reduced number of control plane/signaling events processed by 5G-L2-PS.****

5G-L2-PS shall trigger an indication towards 5G-CP-RT after the overload is cleared when the load falls below the threshold.

**[Before CB013709-C]**

5G-L2-PS shall have independent R&D parameters defining the thresholds for the “signaling” and “scheduling” overload scenarios.

**[End CB013709-C]**

5G-L2-PS shall explicitly trigger overload indication to 5G-CP-RT by the two types of overload:

**[Before CB013709-C]**

**1.** Signaling Overload****

  * L2-PS might end up being overloaded when it experiences a massive inflow of CP-RT events in some of scenarios which might deplete the resources in L2-PS and this results in unexpected crash or hanging resources.
  * L2-PS shall notify CP-RT of the “signaling overload” scenario by the interface PsCell_OverloadProtection.
  * L2-PS shall indicate the “signaling overload” on a pool level. All the cells in the pool shall be considered as overloaded by CP-RT.
  * L2-PS shall use listed R&D parameters to trigger signaling overload:
  * rdNbProcedureContextsMaxLimit,
  * rdNbProcedureContextsHigh,
  * rdNbProcedureContextsLow.



**2\. Scheduling Overload**

  * L2-PS might end up being overloaded when the averaged CS1 max in DL/UL is less than the threshold due to processing overload and the number of UEs with data in DL/UL buffer is high by comparing against the thresholds.
  * L2-PS shall notify CP-RT of the “scheduling overload” scenario by the interface PsCell_OverloadProtection.
  * L2-PS shall indicate the “scheduling overload” on cell level.
  * L2-PS shall use listed R&D parameters to trigger scheduling overload:
  * rdCs1OverloadProtectionEntryDL,
  * rdCs1OverloadProtectionExitDL,
  * rdAvgUesWithDrbOverloadProtectionEntryDL,
  * rdAvgUesWithDrbOverloadProtectionExitDL,
  * rdCs1OverloadProtectionFilterCoeffDL,
  * rdCs1OverloadProtectionEntryUL,
  * rdCs1OverloadProtectionExitUL,
  * rdAvgUesWithDrbOverloadProtectionEntryUL,
  * rdAvgUesWithDrbOverloadProtectionExitUL,
  * rdCs1OverloadProtectionFilterCoeffUL.



**[CB013709-C]**

  * **Signaling Overload - see 5G_L2_21783_replaced([11214405](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-yRi_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**
  * **Scheduling Overload - see 5G_L2_21785_replaced([11214423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-yRjvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**



**[End CB013709-C]**

In both these kinds of overload situations, gNB-DU shall reject any new RRC Setup and Resume requests that happen on the cells that are overloaded.

**[Before CB013709-C] Overload detection at 5G-L2-PS shall not be controlled by Feature Activation Flag.**[End CB013709-C]゜****

---

### 2.14.7.0-4 Overload Protection Calculating for Scheduling Overload L2-PS shall configure overload trigger for scheduling overload by using the CS1 size max, the average number of UEs with buffered data and the protection filter coefficient Alpha parameters to calculate. (ID: 11214443)

**2.14.7.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11214450`)

Overload Protection Calculating Averaging Filter for Alpha factor

---

**2.14.7.0-4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11214463`)

Overload Protection [Before PR799640]

smoothedCs1Size = smoothedCs1Size * (1-alpha) + actualCs1Size * alpha

[End PR799640]

smoothedUeWithDrbCount = smoothedUeWithDrbCount * (1-alpha) + ueWithDrbData * alpha

Note:

  1. R&D parameters define protection filter coefficient alpha: rdCs1OverloadProtectionFilterCoeffUL/DL.

---

**2.14.7.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11214469`)

Overload Protection Calculating for Scheduling Overload trigger

---

**2.14.7.0-4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11214480`)

Overload Protection IF (**[Before PR799640]smoothedCs1Size**[PR799640]averageCs1ListMaxSize**[End PR799640] < rdCs1OverloadProtectionEntryUL/DL) and (smoothedUeWithDrbCount > rdAvgUesWithDrbOverloadProtectionEntryUL/DL) then initiate Cplane backpressure******

IF (**[Before PR799640]smoothedCs1Size**[PR799640]averageCs1ListMaxSize**[End PR799640] > rdCs1OverloadProtectionExitUL/DL) or (smoothedUeWithDrbCount < rdAvgUesWithDrbOverloadProtectionExitUL/DL) then abate Cplane backpressure******

**[PR799640]**

Note:

  1. The definition of averageCs1ListMaxSize can refer to 5G_L2_19562_replaced([11213721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-uAGvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).



**[End PR799640]**

---

### 2.14.7.0-5 Overload Protection Fail-safe periodic CSI and SR load control in-L2-PS (ID: 11214487)

**2.14.7.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11214493`)

Overload Protection Dropping of CSI/SR related Uplink L1 Messages

---

**2.14.7.0-5.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11214500`)

Overload Protection In L2PS overload scenarios, to improve the number of UEs scheduled per slot, Requirement 5G_UP_ALG_28229_replaced([11216726](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxaXmfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) specifies the mechanism of dropping theCSI report and SR report which are later processed at NRT tasks.

CSI report and SR report are received at l2PS through two L1 messages UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs (5G_L1_IF_221_replaced([11514182](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BQvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs (5G_L1_IF_200_replaced([11513831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRzlAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) .L2PS will now check the validity of these two messages by comparing the time on which the message is received against the current system time.

This is done by deriving the time received from message header SFN/Slot and comparing against current SFN/Slot. This difference in time is compared against the configured time threshold. The messages which are exceeding the time threshold are dropped and not processed further. Even the other parameters like TaMetrics etc are not processed in the message.

The R&D parameter rdEnableFailSafeCsiSr (see 5G_L2_19776_replaced([11191076](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28bhEPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is used to enable/disable this functionality.

The R&D parameter rdNrtEventAgingThreshold_msecs (see 5G_UP_ALG_28361_replaced([11216753](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxaXnfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) defines the Time Threshold for difference in time(received Vs current)until which the UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs message and

UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs are considered valid. Since this R&D parameter is onlne modifiable, L2-PS reads this parameter from RAD database once in 100 slots in order to optimize the CPU performance.

---

**2.14.7.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11214506`)

Overload Protection R&D Counter

---

**2.14.7.0-5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11214512`)

Overload Protection Based on Req 5G_L2_21797_replaced([11214517](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-y4sfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ,Whenever there is a dropping of UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs message at DL scheduler the R&D counter DROPPED_CSI_SR_PUCCH_MSG_COUNT is incremented. Whenever there is a dropping of UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs message at UL scheduler the R&D counter DROPPED_CSI_SR_PUSCH_MSG_COUNT is incremented.

These are debug counters which gives a measure of load by indicating how many messages were dropped at each scheduler.

---

**2.14.7.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `11214517`)

Overload Protection Dropping of Split UlData_PuschReceiveResPs

---

**2.14.7.0-5.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11214523`)

Overload Protection When CNI-123026 (splitting of UlData Pusch ReceiveResPs) is enabled along with CNI-125242, the aging comparision (to check if msg is too late) is done for both the initial UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs message and as well as for split UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs message. In case if initial UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs

is not dropped and the next corresponding any split UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs message is dropped, the EM context having split information is also cleared to ensure that same split UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs message is not enqueued back.

---

## 2.14.8 System Queue Load Control

### 2.14.8.0-1 System Queue Load Control Prevention of System Queue Overflow (ID: 13400873)

**2.14.8.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13400875`)

System Queue Load Control 5G-L2-PS shall perform the below mechanism if all the following conditions are met:

  * 5G-L2-PS is running on a Classical deployment
  * l1HwVariant != 0 (loner)



If any of the above conditions are not met, 5G-L2-PS shall not perform this mechanism.

At the beginning of every slot, 5G-L2-PS shall check the number of events pending in the system queue with the lowest priority level (numOfLowestPrioEvents). If numOfLowestPrioEvents is greater than rdSysQueueEmergencyThreshold then:

5G-L2-PS shall skip UE scheduling in this slot.

Otherwise:

5G-L2-PS shall perform UE scheduling as per the slot's load type (see [11212562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-mrUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

Parameters:

  * rdSysQueueEmergencyThreshold is defined in [13400543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_JeBqAAtBEfGu_4itz1o3RA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
  * l1HwVariant is received in PsCell_CellSetupReq ([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---
